## Callbacks

Define any of these in `main.lua`. All are optional.

```lua
  function lurek.load()                                    end  -- called once after script loads
  function lurek.update(dt)                                end  -- dt: number; called every frame before draw
  function lurek.draw()                                    end  -- called every frame; push draw commands here
  function lurek.keypressed(key, scancode, isrepeat)       end  -- key: string; isrepeat: bool
  function lurek.keyreleased(key, scancode)                end  -- key: string; scancode: string
  function lurek.textinput(text)                           end  -- text: string; Unicode character input
  function lurek.mousepressed(x, y, button)                end  -- button: 1=left 2=right 3=middle
  function lurek.mousereleased(x, y, button)               end  -- button: number
  function lurek.wheelmoved(x, y)                          end  -- x,y: scroll delta this frame
  function lurek.input.gamepadpressed(id, button)          end  -- id: number; button: string
  function lurek.input.gamepadreleased(id, button)         end  -- id: number; button: string
  function lurek.input.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)        end  -- value: -1.0 to 1.0
  function lurek.joystickadded(id)                         end  -- gamepad connected
  function lurek.joystickremoved(id)                       end  -- gamepad disconnected
  function lurek.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)  end  -- touch start
  function lurek.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)    end  -- touch move
  function lurek.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure) end  -- touch end
  function lurek.focus(focused)                            end  -- focused: bool; window focus changed
  function lurek.visible(visible)                          end  -- visible: bool; window hidden or shown
  function lurek.resize(w, h)                              end  -- w, h: new window dimensions
  function lurek.quit()                                    end  -- return true to cancel shutdown
  function lurek.errorhandler(msg)                         end  -- return replacement string or nil
```

## lurek.render {#render}

> Immediate-mode 2D rendering: images, shapes, text, canvas, shaders, blend modes, transforms.

```lua
  lurek.render.applyTransform( mat )  -- Applies an affine transform matrix.
  lurek.render.arc( )  -- Draws a partial circle arc at the given position with specified radius and angle range.
  lurek.render.beginSortGroup( id )  -- Begins a Y/Z depth sort group. Draw commands until flushSortGroup are depth-sortable.
  lurek.render.captureScreenshot( callback )  -- Calls the given callback with an ImageData captured from the current frame (stub: creat...
  lurek.render.circle( mode, x, y, radius )  -- Draws a filled or outlined circle at the given world-space position.
  lurek.render.clear( [r], [g], [b] )  -- Clears the draw command queue (resets the screen).
  lurek.render.clearStencil( )  -- Resets the stencil mode to the default (keep / always / 0).
  lurek.render.currentLayer( )  -- Returns the name of the currently active named layer.
  lurek.render.draw( ... )  -- Draws a drawable (Image, Canvas, SpriteBatch, Mesh) at the given position.
  lurek.render.drawBevelRect( )  -- Queues a beveled border rectangle with inner fill.
  lurek.render.drawColoredPolygon( vertices, colors, [mode] )  -- Queues a convex polygon with per-vertex colours.
  lurek.render.drawCubicBezier( )  -- Queues a cubic BĂ©zier curve from (x1,y1) to (x2,y2) with two control points.
  lurek.render.drawGradientRect( )  -- Queues a gradient-filled rectangle. color1/color2 are {r,g,b,a} tables.
  lurek.render.drawHexTile( )  -- Queues a hexagonal tile at centre (cx, cy) with given circumradius.
  lurek.render.drawIsoCubeTile( sx, sy, half_w, half_h, [opts] )  -- Queues a three-face isometric cube tile at screen position (sx, sy).
  lurek.render.drawNineSlice( slice, x, y, w, h )  -- Queues a 9-slice draw call inside lurek.draw / lurek.draw_ui.
  lurek.render.drawPath( path, [mode], [close] )  -- Queues a multi-segment vector path.
  lurek.render.drawQuadBezier( )  -- Queues a quadratic BĂ©zier curve from (x1,y1) to (x2,y2) with one control point.
  lurek.render.drawq( )  -- Draws a portion of an image defined by a Quad.
  lurek.render.ellipse( mode, x, y, rx, ry )  -- Draws a filled or outlined ellipse with independent x/y radii.
  lurek.render.flushSortGroup( id )  -- Sorts and flushes all draw commands in the sort group.
  lurek.render.getBackgroundColor( )  -> BackgroundColor  -- Returns the current background color.
  lurek.render.getBlendMode( )  -> BlendMode  -- Returns the current blend mode as a string.
  lurek.render.getCanvas( )  -> Canvas  -- Returns the current canvas, or nil if drawing to screen.
  lurek.render.getCanvasSize( ud )  -> CanvasSize  -- Returns the dimensions of a canvas.
  lurek.render.getColor( )  -> Color  -- Returns the current drawing color.
  lurek.render.getColorMask( )  -> ColorMask  -- Returns the current color mask.
  lurek.render.getDefaultFilter( )  -> DefaultFilter  -- Returns the default texture filter mode.
  lurek.render.getDefaultFont( [pixel_height] )  -> DefaultFont  -- Returns a built-in font by pixel height (snaps to nearest available size).
  lurek.render.getDepthMode( )  -> DepthMode  -- Returns the current depth mode as (mode, write).
  lurek.render.getDimensions( )  -> Dimensions  -- Returns window width and height.
  lurek.render.getFont( )  -> Font  -- Returns the currently active font, or nil.
  lurek.render.getFontAscent( ud )  -> FontAscent  -- Returns the ascent of the given font.
  lurek.render.getFontCellWidth( ud )  -> FontCellWidth  -- Returns the cell width of the given font (for monospaced bitmap fonts).
  lurek.render.getFontDescent( ud )  -> FontDescent  -- Returns the descent of the given font.
  lurek.render.getFontHeight( ud )  -> FontHeight  -- Returns the line height of the given font.
  lurek.render.getFontLineHeight( ud )  -> FontLineHeight  -- Returns the line height of the given font (alias for getFontHeight).
  lurek.render.getFontSizes( )  -> FontSizes  -- Returns a table of available built-in font pixel heights.
  lurek.render.getFontWidth( ud, text )  -> FontWidth  -- Returns the pixel width of text in the given font.
  lurek.render.getFontWrap( text, limit )  -> FontWrap  -- Returns wrapped lines and the maximum line width.
  lurek.render.getHeight( )  -> Height  -- Returns the window height in pixels.
  lurek.render.getLayerZOrder( name )  -> LayerZOrder  -- Returns the z-order of the named layer, or `0` if unregistered.
  lurek.render.getLineWidth( )  -> LineWidth  -- Returns the current line width.
  lurek.render.getPointSize( )  -> PointSize  -- Returns the current point size.
  lurek.render.getScissor( )  -> Scissor  -- Returns the active scissor rectangle, or nothing.
  lurek.render.getShader( )  -> Shader  -- Returns the active shader, or nil.
  lurek.render.getStats( )  -> Stats  -- Returns a table of renderer statistics.
  lurek.render.getStencilMode( )  -> StencilMode  -- Returns the current stencil mode as (action, compare, value).
  lurek.render.getWidth( )  -> Width  -- Returns the window width in pixels.
  lurek.render.intersectScissor( x, y, w, h )  -- Intersects the current scissor with a new rectangle.
  lurek.render.isLayerVisible( name )  -- Returns `true` if the named layer is visible (default: `true`).
  lurek.render.isWireframe( )  -- Returns whether wireframe mode is active.
  lurek.render.line( ... )  -- Draws a line between two points.
  lurek.render.newCanvas( width, height )  -> Canvas  -- Creates an off-screen render canvas.
  lurek.render.newDrawLayer( )  -> DrawLayer  -- Creates a new z-ordered draw-call queue.
  lurek.render.newFont( ... )  -> Font  -- Loads a bitmap font PNG from a file, or selects a built-in size by pixel height.
  lurek.render.newImage( arg )  -> Image  -- Loads an image from a file path or creates one from ImageData.
  lurek.render.newLayer( name, [z_order] )  -> Layer  -- Registers a named render layer with an optional z-order (default 0).
  lurek.render.newMesh( verts, [mode] )  -> Mesh  -- Creates a custom mesh from vertex data.
  lurek.render.newNineSlice( image, top, right, bottom, left )  -> NineSlice  -- Creates a 9-slice descriptor from a texture and inset values.
  lurek.render.newQuad( x, y, w, h, sw, sh )  -> Quad  -- Creates a new Quad viewport into a texture.
  lurek.render.newShader( code )  -> Shader  -- Compiles a custom WGSL shader and returns its handle.
  lurek.render.newShape( )  -> Shape  -- Creates a new empty [`CompoundShape`] stored in the resource pool.
  lurek.render.newSpriteBatch( ud, [max] )  -> SpriteBatch  -- Creates a new sprite batch for the given image.
  lurek.render.origin( )  -- Resets the transform to the identity.
  lurek.render.points( ... )  -- Draws a batch of individual points at the specified world-space coordinates.
  lurek.render.polygon( ... )  -- Draws a polygon from a list of vertices.
  lurek.render.pop( )  -- Pops the transform from the stack.
  lurek.render.popLayer( id )  -- Ends and composites the named layer back to its parent.
  lurek.render.print( text, [x], [y], [scale] )  -- Draws text at the given position.
  lurek.render.printRich( spans_table, x, y )  -- Draws a sequence of individually-styled text spans at `(x, y)`.
  lurek.render.printf( text, x, y, limit, [align] )  -- Draws word-wrapped text within a given width.
  lurek.render.push( )  -- Pushes the current transform onto the stack.
  lurek.render.pushLayer( id, [alpha], [blend_mode] )  -- Begins a named compositing layer with optional alpha and blend mode.
  lurek.render.pushSortKey( depth )  -- Associates the previous draw command with a depth value within the active sort group.
  lurek.render.rectangle( )  -- Draws a filled or outlined axis-aligned rectangle at the given position.
  lurek.render.rotate( angle )  -- Rotates the coordinate system.
  lurek.render.saveScreenshot( path )  -- Queues a screenshot to be saved after the current frame.
  lurek.render.scale( sx, [sy] )  -- Scales the coordinate system.
  lurek.render.setBackgroundColor( r, g, b )  -- Sets the background clear color.
  lurek.render.setBlendMode( mode )  -- Sets the blend mode for drawing.
  lurek.render.setCanvas( [ud] )  -- Sets the active render target to a Canvas, or back to the screen.
  lurek.render.setColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the current drawing color.
  lurek.render.setColorMask( ... )  -- Sets which RGBA channels are written. Reset with no args.
  lurek.render.setDefaultFilter( min, mag, [anisotropy] )  -- Sets the default texture filter mode.
  lurek.render.setDepthMode( mode, [write] )  -- Sets the depth test comparison and write enable.
  lurek.render.setFont( ud )  -- Sets the active font for print calls.
  lurek.render.setFontLineHeight( font, lh )  -- Sets the line height of the given font (stub â€” returns nil; fonts are immutable in he...
  lurek.render.setLayer( name )  -- Sets the active named layer. Draw calls made after this will be
  lurek.render.setLayerVisible( name, visible )  -- Shows or hides the named layer. Hidden layers are excluded from
  lurek.render.setLayerZOrder( name, z )  -- Updates the z-order of the named layer. Auto-creates the layer if
  lurek.render.setLineWidth( w )  -- Sets the line width for outline drawing.
  lurek.render.setPointSize( size )  -- Sets the point diameter in pixels.
  lurek.render.setScissor( ... )  -- Restricts drawing to a rectangle, or clears scissor if no args.
  lurek.render.setShader( [ud] )  -- Sets the active shader, or clears it.
  lurek.render.setStencilMode( action, [compare], [value] )  -- Sets the stencil buffer write/test mode.
  lurek.render.setStencilTest( [compare], [value] )  -- Sets the stencil comparison test, or disables stencil testing.
  lurek.render.setWireframe( enabled )  -- Enables or disables wireframe rendering.
  lurek.render.shear( kx, ky )  -- Shears the coordinate system.
  lurek.render.stencil( [action], [value] )  -- Begins stencil writing with the given action and value.
  lurek.render.translate( x, y )  -- Translates the coordinate system.
  lurek.render.triangle( mode, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3 )  -- Draws a filled or outlined triangle connecting three world-space vertices.
```

**`Canvas`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to an off-screen render target stored in SharedState.

```lua
  Canvas:getDimensions( )  -> Dimensions  -- Returns width and height of this canvas.
  Canvas:getHeight( )  -> Height  -- Returns the height of this canvas in pixels.
  Canvas:getWidth( )  -> Width  -- Returns the width of this canvas in pixels.
  Canvas:release( )  -- Releases GPU framebuffer memory for this canvas.
  Canvas:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Canvas:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

**`DrawLayer`** methods:

> Lua-side z-ordered draw queue. Callbacks are sorted by z and called on `flush()`.

```lua
  DrawLayer:clear( )  -- Removes all queued callbacks without calling them.
  DrawLayer:flush( )  -- Sorts and calls all queued callbacks, then empties the queue.
  DrawLayer:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the number of queued callbacks.
  DrawLayer:queue( z, f )  -- Queues a draw callback at the given z-order.
  DrawLayer:type( )  -- Returns the string type identifier of this draw layer (e.g. `'sprite'`).
  DrawLayer:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is an instance of the given type name.
```

**`Font`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a loaded font stored in SharedState.

```lua
  Font:getAscent( )  -> Ascent  -- Returns the ascent of this font in pixels.
  Font:getDescent( )  -> Descent  -- Returns the descent of this font in pixels.
  Font:getHeight( )  -> Height  -- Returns the line height of this font.
  Font:getLineHeight( )  -> LineHeight  -- Returns the line height multiplier of this font.
  Font:getWidth( text )  -> Width  -- Returns the rendered width of the given text string.
  Font:getWrap( text, limit )  -> Wrap  -- Wraps text to the given width and returns the lines.
  Font:release( )  -- Releases this font and frees its atlas memory.
  Font:setLineHeight( height )  -- Sets the line height multiplier for this font.
  Font:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Font:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

**`Image`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a loaded GPU texture stored in the engine's texture pool.

```lua
  Image:getDimensions( )  -> Dimensions  -- Returns width and height of this image.
  Image:getHeight( )  -> Height  -- Returns the height of this image in pixels.
  Image:getWidth( )  -> Width  -- Returns the width of this image in pixels.
  Image:release( )  -- Releases the GPU texture memory for this image.
  Image:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Image:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

**`Mesh`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a mesh stored in SharedState.

```lua
  Mesh:getVertex( index )  -> Vertex  -- Returns vertex data at the given 1-based index.
  Mesh:getVertexCount( )  -> VertexCount  -- Returns the number of vertices in this mesh.
  Mesh:release( )  -- Releases the GPU mesh resource, freeing VRAM immediately.
  Mesh:setTexture( [ud] )  -- Assigns a texture to this mesh.
  Mesh:setVertex( index, data )  -- Sets vertex data at the given 1-based index.
  Mesh:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Mesh:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

**`NineSlice`** methods:

> Lua-side 9-slice descriptor.

```lua
  NineSlice:draw( x, y, w, h )  -- Compatibility stub: queuing handled by lurek.graphic.drawNineSlice.
  NineSlice:getInsets( )  -> Insets  -- Returns the four inset values as (top, right, bottom, left).
  NineSlice:getTextureSize( )  -> TextureSize  -- Returns the width and height of the source texture.
  NineSlice:type( )  -- Returns the type name "NineSlice".
  NineSlice:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true when the given name matches "NineSlice" or a parent type.
```

**`Quad`** methods:

> Lua-side quad viewport into a texture.

```lua
  Quad:getTextureDimensions( )  -> TextureDimensions  -- Returns the reference texture dimensions.
  Quad:getViewport( )  -> Viewport  -- Returns the quad viewport rectangle.
  Quad:setViewport( x, y, w, h )  -- Sets the quad viewport rectangle.
  Quad:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Quad:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

**`Shader`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a compiled shader stored in SharedState.

```lua
  Shader:hasUniform( name )  -- Returns whether this shader has a uniform with the given name.
  Shader:release( )  -- Releases the compiled GPU shader, freeing VRAM and shader slots.
  Shader:send( name, value )  -- Sends a uniform value to this shader.
  Shader:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Shader:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

**`Shape`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a [`CompoundShape`] stored in [`SharedState::shapes`].

```lua
  Shape:arc( )  -- Queues a filled or outlined arc draw command onto this shape.
  Shape:circle( mode, x, y, r )  -- Queues a filled or outlined circle draw command onto this shape.
  Shape:clear( )  -- Removes all commands and resets the shape to empty.
  Shape:draw( )  -- Queues a draw command for this shape at the given position.
  Shape:ellipse( mode, x, y, rx, ry )  -- Queues an ellipse command.
  Shape:getCommandCount( )  -> CommandCount  -- Returns the number of drawing commands currently stored.
  Shape:line( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Queues a line segment command.
  Shape:polygon( mode, coords )  -- Queues a polygon command from variadic (x, y) coordinate pairs.
  Shape:polyline( )  -- Queues a polyline command from variadic (x, y) coordinate pairs.
  Shape:rectangle( mode, x, y, w, h )  -- Queues a rectangle command.
  Shape:roundedRectangle( mode, x, y, w, h, rx, [ry] )  -- Queues a rounded rectangle command.
  Shape:setColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the drawing color for subsequent primitives.
  Shape:setLineWidth( w )  -- Sets the stroke width for subsequent outlined primitives.
  Shape:triangle( mode, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3 )  -- Queues a triangle command.
  Shape:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Shape:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if the given type name matches this object's type or any parent type.
```

**`SpriteBatch`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a sprite batch stored in SharedState.

```lua
  SpriteBatch:add( )  -- Adds a sprite entry to this batch.
  SpriteBatch:clear( )  -- Removes all sprites from this batch.
  SpriteBatch:getBufferSize( )  -> BufferSize  -- Returns the maximum capacity of this batch.
  SpriteBatch:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the number of sprites in this batch.
  SpriteBatch:release( )  -- Releases this sprite batch.
  SpriteBatch:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  SpriteBatch:typeOf( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
```

## lurek.audio {#audio}

> Sound playback: load audio files, play/pause/stop, volume, pitch, looping, panning.

```lua
  lurek.audio.add_effect( bus_name, effect_type_str, [params] )  -- Adds a DSP effect to a bus.
  lurek.audio.applyBandpass( sd_ud, low_hz, high_hz )  -- Applies a bandpass filter (high-pass then low-pass) to a SoundData in-place.
  lurek.audio.applyGain( sd_ud, gain )  -- Scales every sample by gain (clamped to [-1, 1]).
  lurek.audio.applyHighpass( sd_ud, cutoff_hz )  -- Applies a first-order IIR high-pass filter to a SoundData in-place.
  lurek.audio.applyLowpass( sd_ud, cutoff_hz )  -- Applies a first-order IIR low-pass filter to a SoundData in-place.
  lurek.audio.clearFilter( id_val )  -- Removes any active filter from a source.
  lurek.audio.clearMidiSoundFont( )  -- Unloads the active SoundFont.
  lurek.audio.clearRandomPitch( src_ud )  -- Clears any random pitch range on a source, restoring fixed pitch.
  lurek.audio.clone( id_val )  -- Creates an independent copy of a source.
  lurek.audio.create_bus( name, [parent_name] )  -- Creates a bus by name (functional style).
  lurek.audio.crossfade( from_ud, to_ud, duration )  -- Crossfades from one source to another over a duration.
  lurek.audio.fadeIn( id_val, dur )  -- Fades a source in from silence over the given duration.
  lurek.audio.getActiveSourceCount( )  -> ActiveSourceCount  -- Returns the number of currently playing sources.
  lurek.audio.getBusPeak( bus_name )  -> BusPeak  -- Returns the peak signal level of the named bus (stub: always 0.0).
  lurek.audio.getBusRms( bus_name )  -> RMS  -- Returns the RMS signal level of the named bus (stub: always 0.0).
  lurek.audio.getDistanceModel( )  -> DistanceModel  -- Returns the current distance model name.
  lurek.audio.getDopplerScale( )  -> DopplerScale  -- Returns the current Doppler scale.
  lurek.audio.getDuration( id_val )  -> Duration  -- Returns the total duration of a source in seconds.
  lurek.audio.getFadeIn( id_val )  -> FadeIn  -- Returns the fade-in duration of a source.
  lurek.audio.getFreeBufferCount( qsource_id )  -> FreeBufferCount  -- Returns the free buffer slots in a queueable source.
  lurek.audio.getHighpass( id_val )  -> Highpass  -- Returns the high-pass filter cutoff of a source.
  lurek.audio.getListener( )  -> Listener  -- Returns the 3D listener position (x, y, z).
  lurek.audio.getListener2D( )  -> Listener2D  -- Returns the 2D listener position (x, y).
  lurek.audio.getLowpass( id_val )  -> Lowpass  -- Returns the low-pass filter cutoff of a source.
  lurek.audio.getMasterVolume( )  -> MasterVolume  -- Returns the global master volume.
  lurek.audio.getMaxSources( )  -> MaxSources  -- Returns the maximum number of simultaneous sources.
  lurek.audio.getMeter( )  -> Meter  -- Returns the stored master peak meter level.
  lurek.audio.getOrientation( id_val )  -> Orientation  -- Returns the 6-component orientation of a source.
  lurek.audio.getPan( id_val )  -> Pan  -- Returns the source stereo panning.
  lurek.audio.getPitch( id_val )  -> Pitch  -- Returns the source pitch multiplier.
  lurek.audio.getPlaybackDevice( )  -> PlaybackDevice  -- Returns the current audio output device name.
  lurek.audio.getPlaybackDevices( )  -> PlaybackDevices  -- Returns a table of available audio output device names.
  lurek.audio.getPosition( id_val )  -> Position  -- Returns the 3D position of a source (x, y, z).
  lurek.audio.getSourceBus( id_val )  -> SourceBus  -- Returns the bus a source is assigned to, or nil.
  lurek.audio.getSourceCount( )  -> SourceCount  -- Returns the total number of registered sources.
  lurek.audio.getSourceType( id_val )  -> SourceType  -- Returns the type string ("static" or "stream") of a source.
  lurek.audio.getStereoWidth( src_ud )  -> StereoWidth  -- Returns the current stereo width for a source.
  lurek.audio.getVelocity( id_val )  -> Velocity  -- Returns the velocity of a source (x, y, z).
  lurek.audio.getVolume( id_val )  -> Volume  -- Returns the source volume.
  lurek.audio.hasMidiSoundFont( )  -- Returns true if a SoundFont is loaded.
  lurek.audio.isLooping( id_val )  -- Returns true if looping is enabled.
  lurek.audio.isPaused( id_val )  -- Returns true if the source is paused.
  lurek.audio.isPlaying( id_val )  -- Returns true if the source is playing.
  lurek.audio.isStopped( id_val )  -- Returns true if the source is stopped.
  lurek.audio.mixInto( dest_ud, src_ud )  -- Additively mixes another SoundData into the destination in-place.
  lurek.audio.newBus( name )  -> Bus  -- Creates a named audio bus for grouping sources.
  lurek.audio.newDecoder( source, [buffersize] )  -> Decoder  -- Creates a streaming audio decoder.
  lurek.audio.newMidiPlayer( [path] )  -> MIDI  -- Creates a MIDI player, optionally loading a file.
  lurek.audio.newPool( file_path, voice_count )  -> Pool  -- Creates a polyphonic sound pool for the given file with N simultaneous voices.
  lurek.audio.newQueueableSource( )  -> QueueableSource  -- Creates a queueable source for manual PCM buffering.
  lurek.audio.newSawtoothWave( freq, duration, sample_rate, amplitude )  -> SawtoothWave  -- Generate a mono sawtooth-wave SoundData buffer.
  lurek.audio.newSineWave( freq, duration, sample_rate, amplitude )  -> SineWave  -- Generate a mono sine-wave SoundData buffer.
  lurek.audio.newSoundData( ... )  -> SoundData  -- Creates a SoundData from a file or as a silent buffer.
  lurek.audio.newSource( ... )  -> Source  -- Loads an audio file and returns a Source handle.
  lurek.audio.newSquareWave( freq, duration, sample_rate, amplitude )  -> SquareWave  -- Generate a mono square-wave SoundData buffer.
  lurek.audio.newTriangleWave( freq, duration, sample_rate, amplitude )  -> TriangleWave  -- Generate a mono triangle-wave SoundData buffer.
  lurek.audio.newWhiteNoise( duration, sample_rate, amplitude, seed )  -> WhiteNoise  -- Generate a reproducible white-noise SoundData buffer.
  lurek.audio.normalizeFile( input, output, target )  -- Normalizes a WAV file peak amplitude to target_level and writes output.
  lurek.audio.pause( id_val )  -- Pauses playback at the current position.
  lurek.audio.pauseAll( )  -- Pauses all currently playing sources.
  lurek.audio.play( id_val, [options] )  -- Plays a source, with optional bus routing via options table.
  lurek.audio.playLooping( id_val )  -- Plays the source in a continuous loop.
  lurek.audio.playQueueable( qsource_id )  -- Starts playback of a queueable source.
  lurek.audio.processOffline( input, output, effects_tbl )  -- Applies a DSP effect chain to a WAV file and writes output.
  lurek.audio.queueSource( qsource_id, sd )  -- Pushes a SoundData buffer into a queueable source.
  lurek.audio.release( id_val )  -- Releases a source and frees its memory.
  lurek.audio.remove_effect( bus_name, effect_id )  -- Removes a DSP effect from a bus.
  lurek.audio.resume( id_val )  -- Resumes playback from pause.
  lurek.audio.resumeAll( )  -- Resumes all paused sources.
  lurek.audio.saveWAV( sd_ud, filename )  -- Saves a SoundData as a 16-bit PCM WAV file at the given path.
  lurek.audio.seek( id_val, pos )  -- Seeks to a time position in seconds.
  lurek.audio.setDistanceModel( model )  -- Sets the distance attenuation model.
  lurek.audio.setDopplerScale( scale )  -- Sets the global Doppler effect scale.
  lurek.audio.setHighpass( id_val, cutoff_hz )  -- Applies a high-pass filter to a source.
  lurek.audio.setListener( x, y, [z] )  -- Sets the 3D listener position.
  lurek.audio.setListener2D( x, y )  -- Sets the 2D listener position for spatial audio.
  lurek.audio.setLooping( id_val, looping )  -- Enables or disables looping.
  lurek.audio.setLowpass( id_val, cutoff_hz )  -- Applies a low-pass filter to a source.
  lurek.audio.setMasterVolume( vol )  -- Sets the global master volume.
  lurek.audio.setMeter( level )  -- Sets the master peak meter level (0.0â€“1.0).
  lurek.audio.setMidiSoundFont( path )  -- Sets the global SoundFont for MIDI synthesis.
  lurek.audio.setOrientation( id_val, fx, fy, fz, ux, uy, uz )  -- Sets the 6-component orientation of a source.
  lurek.audio.setPan( id_val, pan )  -- Sets stereo panning (-1.0 left to 1.0 right).
  lurek.audio.setPitch( id_val, pitch )  -- Sets source pitch multiplier.
  lurek.audio.setPlaybackDevice( name )  -- Selects an audio output device by name.
  lurek.audio.setPosition( id_val, x, y, [z] )  -- Sets the 3D position of a source.
  lurek.audio.setRandomPitch( src_ud, min, max )  -- Sets a random pitch range applied each time the source is played.
  lurek.audio.setSourceBus( id_val, bus_val )  -- Assigns a source to a bus.
  lurek.audio.setStereoWidth( src_ud, width )  -- Sets the stereo width multiplier for a source (1.0 = normal, 0.0 = mono).
  lurek.audio.setVelocity( id_val, x, y, [z] )  -- Sets the velocity of a source for Doppler.
  lurek.audio.setVolume( id_val, vol )  -- Sets source playback volume.
  lurek.audio.set_bus_volume( name, volume )  -- Sets a bus volume by name.
  lurek.audio.set_effect_param( bus_name, effect_id, param_name, value )  -- Sets a parameter on a DSP effect.
  lurek.audio.spectrogramToPng( input, output, width, height )  -- Renders a time-frequency spectrogram of a WAV file to a PNG image.
  lurek.audio.stop( id_val )  -- Stops playback and resets seek position.
  lurek.audio.stopAll( )  -- Stops all currently playing sources.
  lurek.audio.stopQueueable( qsource_id )  -- Stops a queueable source and drains its buffers.
  lurek.audio.tell( id_val )  -- Returns the current playback position in seconds.
  lurek.audio.waveformToPng( input, output, width, height )  -- Renders the waveform of a WAV file to a PNG image.
```

**`Bus`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for an audio bus resource.

```lua
  Bus:clearDuck( )  -- Removes the ducking target from this bus, restoring the target bus
  Bus:getName( )  -> Name  -- Returns the unique name string assigned to this audio bus.
  Bus:getPeak( )  -> Peak  -- Returns the average peak amplitude of all sources currently on this bus.
  Bus:getPitch( )  -> Pitch  -- Returns the bus pitch multiplier.
  Bus:getVolume( )  -> Volume  -- Returns the current volume multiplier applied to all sources on this bus.
  Bus:isPaused( )  -- Returns true if this bus is paused.
  Bus:pause( )  -- Pauses all sources on this bus.
  Bus:resume( )  -- Resumes all sources on this bus.
  Bus:setDuckTarget( target_name, duck_vol )  -- Configures this bus to duck (lower the volume of) another bus when
  Bus:setPitch( pitch )  -- Sets the pitch multiplier for all sources on this bus.
  Bus:setVolume( vol )  -- Sets the volume for all sources on this bus.
  Bus:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Bus:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`Decoder`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for a streaming audio decoder.

```lua
  Decoder:decode( )  -- Decodes the next chunk of samples, or nil at EOF.
  Decoder:getBitDepth( )  -> BitDepth  -- Returns the per-sample bit depth of this decoded audio stream.
  Decoder:getChannelCount( )  -> ChannelCount  -- Returns the number of audio channels.
  Decoder:getDuration( )  -> Duration  -- Returns the total duration in seconds.
  Decoder:getSampleRate( )  -> SampleRate  -- Returns the sample rate in Hz.
  Decoder:isSeekable( )  -- Returns true if seeking is supported.
  Decoder:release( )  -- Releases the decoder (no-op).
  Decoder:rewind( )  -- Rewinds to the beginning.
  Decoder:seek( offset )  -- Seeks to a time offset in seconds.
  Decoder:tell( )  -- Returns the current position in seconds.
```

**`MidiPlayer`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for the MIDI player.

```lua
  MidiPlayer:getBus( )  -> Bus  -- Returns the assigned bus, or nil.
  MidiPlayer:getChannelCount( )  -> ChannelCount  -- Returns the number of MIDI channels.
  MidiPlayer:getChannelInstrument( ch )  -> GM  -- Returns the GM instrument for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:getChannelVolume( ch )  -> ChannelVolume  -- Returns the volume for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:getChannels( )  -> PCM  -- Returns the PCM output channel count (1 = mono, 2 = stereo).
  MidiPlayer:getDuration( )  -> Duration  -- Returns the total MIDI duration in seconds.
  MidiPlayer:getFilePath( )  -> FilePath  -- Returns the file path of the loaded MIDI, or nil.
  MidiPlayer:getNoteCount( )  -> NoteCount  -- Returns the total note count in the MIDI sequence.
  MidiPlayer:getOriginalTempo( )  -> OriginalTempo  -- Returns the original MIDI file tempo in BPM.
  MidiPlayer:getSampleRate( )  -> PCM  -- Returns the PCM output sample rate in Hz.
  MidiPlayer:getSoundFontPath( )  -> SoundFont  -- Returns the SoundFont file path, or nil (stub).
  MidiPlayer:getTempo( )  -> Tempo  -- Returns the current tempo in BPM.
  MidiPlayer:getTempoScale( )  -> TempoScale  -- Returns the current tempo scale factor.
  MidiPlayer:getTicksPerBeat( )  -> PPQ  -- Returns the PPQ resolution from the MIDI header.
  MidiPlayer:getTrackCount( )  -> TrackCount  -- Returns the number of tracks in the MIDI sequence.
  MidiPlayer:getTrackName( idx )  -> TrackName  -- Returns the name of a MIDI track (1-indexed), or nil.
  MidiPlayer:getVolume( )  -> Volume  -- Returns the current MIDI volume.
  MidiPlayer:isChannelMuted( ch )  -- Returns true if a MIDI channel is muted (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:isLoaded( )  -- Returns true if a MIDI sequence is loaded.
  MidiPlayer:isLooping( )  -- Returns true if looping is enabled.
  MidiPlayer:isPaused( )  -- Returns true if MIDI playback is paused.
  MidiPlayer:isPlaying( )  -- Returns true if MIDI is currently playing.
  MidiPlayer:isTrackMuted( idx )  -- Returns true if a track is muted (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:load( path )  -> MIDI  -- Loads a MIDI file from the given path.
  MidiPlayer:loadData( )  -> MIDI  -- Loads MIDI data from a Lua string.
  MidiPlayer:pause( )  -- Pauses the MIDI sequence at the current position; resume with `play()`.
  MidiPlayer:play( )  -- Starts or resumes MIDI sequence playback from the current position.
  MidiPlayer:seek( secs )  -- Seeks to a time position in seconds.
  MidiPlayer:setBus( bus_val )  -- Routes MIDI output through a bus (or nil to clear).
  MidiPlayer:setChannelInstrument( ch, inst )  -- Sets the GM instrument for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:setChannelMuted( ch, muted )  -- Mutes or unmutes a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:setChannelVolume( ch, vol )  -- Sets volume for a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:setChannels( channels )  -- Sets the PCM output channel count (clamped 1â€“2).
  MidiPlayer:setLooping( looping )  -- Enables or disables looping.
  MidiPlayer:setOnEnd( cb )  -- Registers a playback-end callback (stub).
  MidiPlayer:setOnNoteOff( cb )  -- Registers a note-off callback (stub).
  MidiPlayer:setOnNoteOn( cb )  -- Registers a note-on callback (stub).
  MidiPlayer:setSampleRate( rate )  -- Sets the PCM output sample rate in Hz (clamped 8000â€“192000).
  MidiPlayer:setSoundFont( path )  -> SoundFont  -- Loads a SoundFont file into this player (stub).
  MidiPlayer:setTempo( bpm )  -- Sets playback tempo in BPM.
  MidiPlayer:setTempoScale( scale )  -- Sets the tempo scale factor (1.0 = original speed).
  MidiPlayer:setTrackMuted( idx, muted )  -- Mutes or unmutes a track (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:setVolume( vol )  -- Sets MIDI playback volume.
  MidiPlayer:soloChannel( ch )  -- Solos a MIDI channel (1-indexed).
  MidiPlayer:stop( )  -- Stops MIDI playback and resets the playhead to the beginning.
  MidiPlayer:tell( )  -- Returns the current playback position in seconds.
  MidiPlayer:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  MidiPlayer:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  MidiPlayer:unsoloAll( )  -- Clears solo on all channels.
  MidiPlayer:useDefaultSoundFont( )  -- Reverts to the built-in default SoundFont (stub).
```

## lurek.timer {#timer}

> Frame timing: delta time, FPS, sleep, scheduled callbacks.

```lua
  lurek.timer.afterReal( delay, func )  -- Schedules a one-shot callback that fires after `delay` wall-clock seconds,
  lurek.timer.chain( steps )  -> Scheduler  -- Creates a new Scheduler loaded with a sequenced one-shot chain.
  lurek.timer.getAverageDelta( )  -> AverageDelta  -- Returns the rolling-average frame delta time in seconds.
  lurek.timer.getDelta( )  -> Delta  -- Returns the delta time in seconds for the current frame.
  lurek.timer.getFPS( )  -> FPS  -- Returns the current frames-per-second measurement.
  lurek.timer.getFrameCount( )  -> FrameCount  -- Returns the total number of frames rendered since engine start.
  lurek.timer.getMicroTime( )  -> MicroTime  -- Returns the high-resolution elapsed time since engine start in seconds.
  lurek.timer.getPhysicsDelta( )  -> PhysicsDelta  -- Returns the fixed timestep used by `process_physics` callbacks (seconds).
  lurek.timer.getPhysicsMaxSteps( )  -> PhysicsMaxSteps  -- Returns the maximum number of physics sub-steps allowed per frame.
  lurek.timer.getSmoothedDelta( )  -> SmoothedDelta  -- Returns the exponential moving-average of frame deltas in seconds.
  lurek.timer.getTime( )  -> Time  -- Returns the total elapsed time since engine start in seconds.
  lurek.timer.newScheduler( )  -> Scheduler  -- Creates a new independent Scheduler for managing timed callbacks.
  lurek.timer.setPhysicsDelta( dt )  -- Sets the fixed timestep for `process_physics` callbacks (seconds).
  lurek.timer.setPhysicsMaxSteps( n )  -- Sets the maximum number of physics sub-steps allowed per frame (clamped 1â€“64).
  lurek.timer.setSmoothingFactor( alpha )  -- Sets the smoothing factor (alpha) for `getSmoothedDelta`. Must be in [0.01, 1.0].
  lurek.timer.sleep( seconds )  -- Suspends execution for the given number of seconds.
  lurek.timer.step( )  -- Advances the timer by one frame, returning the delta time.
  lurek.timer.tickRealTimers( )  -- Advances all real-time timers by one tick; called automatically each frame.
  lurek.timer.tickWaits( )  -- Advances all `lurek.timer.wait()` coroutines by one tick; called each frame.
  lurek.timer.waitFrames( frames )  -- Yields the current Lua coroutine for at least `frames` engine frames.
  lurek.timer.waitSeconds( seconds )  -- Yields the current Lua coroutine for at least `seconds` wall-clock seconds.
```

**`Scheduler`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Scheduler`] with per-event callback storage.

```lua
  Scheduler:after( delay, func )  -- Schedules a callback to fire once after a delay.
  Scheduler:afterFrames( n, func )  -- Schedules a callback to fire once after `n` frames.
  Scheduler:afterNamed( name, delay, func )  -- Schedules a named one-shot callback, replacing any existing event with the same name.
  Scheduler:cancel( id )  -- Cancels a scheduled event by its numeric ID.
  Scheduler:cancelAll( )  -- Cancels all scheduled events and returns the count removed.
  Scheduler:cancelNamed( name )  -- Cancels a scheduled event by its string name.
  Scheduler:every( interval, func, [count] )  -- Schedules a callback to fire repeatedly at the given interval.
  Scheduler:everyFrames( n, func, [count] )  -- Schedules a callback to fire every `n` frames.
  Scheduler:everyNamed( name, interval, func, [count] )  -- Schedules a named repeating callback, replacing any existing event with the same name.
  Scheduler:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the number of active scheduled events.
  Scheduler:getInterval( id )  -> Interval  -- Returns the base interval in seconds for an event, or nil.
  Scheduler:getRemaining( id )  -> Remaining  -- Returns the seconds remaining until the next fire for an event, or nil.
  Scheduler:getRepeatCount( id )  -> RepeatCount  -- Returns the repeat count remaining for an event, or nil.
  Scheduler:getTimeScale( )  -> TimeScale  -- Returns the current time-scale multiplier.
  Scheduler:isEmpty( )  -- Returns whether the scheduler has no active events.
  Scheduler:isPaused( id )  -- Returns whether the given event is currently paused.
  Scheduler:isPausedNamed( name )  -- Returns whether the named event is currently paused.
  Scheduler:pause( id )  -- Pauses a scheduled event by its ID.
  Scheduler:pauseNamed( name )  -- Pauses a scheduled event by its string name.
  Scheduler:resetEvent( id )  -- Resets an event's remaining time back to its original interval.
  Scheduler:resume( id )  -- Resumes a paused event by its ID.
  Scheduler:resumeNamed( name )  -- Resumes a paused event by its string name.
  Scheduler:setInterval( id, interval )  -- Changes the repeat interval of an existing event.
  Scheduler:setTimeScale( scale )  -- Sets a global time-scale multiplier for this scheduler.
  Scheduler:update( dt )  -- Advances all timers by dt seconds, firing due callbacks.
  Scheduler:updateFrames( )  -- Advances frame-based events by one frame, firing due callbacks.
```

## lurek.math {#math}

> Core math: vectors, random, interpolation, geometry utilities.

```lua
  lurek.math.Vec2( x, y )  -- Compatibility alias for `vec2`.
  lurek.math.Vec3( x, y, z )  -- Compatibility alias for `vec3`.
  lurek.math.aabbTree( )  -- Creates a new empty AABB tree for efficient broad-phase overlap queries.
  lurek.math.abs( x )  -- Returns the absolute value of x.
  lurek.math.acos( x )  -- Returns the arccosine of x, in radians.
  lurek.math.angleBetween( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Returns the angle in radians from (x1, y1) to (x2, y2).
  lurek.math.applyEasing( name, t )  -- Applies a named easing function to progress value t.
  lurek.math.asin( x )  -- Returns the arcsine of x, in radians.
  lurek.math.atan( y, [x] )  -- Returns the arctangent of x (or atan2(y, x) when two args given).
  lurek.math.atan2( y, x )  -- Returns atan(y/x) using the signs of both args to determine the quadrant.
  lurek.math.bresenham( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Rasterizes a line from (x1,y1) to (x2,y2) using Bresenham's algorithm. Returns a table ...
  lurek.math.catmullRom( points )  -> Catmull  -- Creates a Catmull-Rom spline through the given control points.
  lurek.math.ceil( x )  -- Returns the smallest integer ≥ x.
  lurek.math.circleContainsPoint( cx, cy, r, px, py )  -- Returns true if the point (px, py) lies inside the circle.
  lurek.math.circleIntersectsCircle( x1, y1, r1, x2, y2, r2 )  -- Returns true if two circles overlap.
  lurek.math.circleIntersectsLine( cx, cy, r, lx1, ly1, lx2, ly2 )  -- Tests an infinite line against a circle. Returns hit, then two optional hit-point pairs.
  lurek.math.circleIntersectsSegment( cx, cy, r, sx1, sy1, sx2, sy2 )  -- Tests a line segment against a circle. Returns hit, then two optional hit-point pairs.
  lurek.math.clamp( v, min, max )  -- Clamps `v` between `min` and `max`.
  lurek.math.closestPointOnSegment( px, py, x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Returns the closest point on segment (x1,y1)-(x2,y2) to point (px,py).
  lurek.math.convexHull( pts )  -- Computes the convex hull of a flat {x1,y1,...} point list. Returns a flat table.
  lurek.math.cos( x )  -- Returns the cosine of x (radians).
  lurek.math.deg( rad )  -- Converts radians to degrees.
  lurek.math.delaunayTriangulate( pts )  -- Delaunay triangulation of a flat {x1,y1,...} point list. Returns a table of flat 6-numb...
  lurek.math.distance( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> Euclidean  -- Returns the Euclidean distance between (x1,y1) and (x2,y2).
  lurek.math.distanceSq( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Returns the squared Euclidean distance between (x1,y1) and (x2,y2) (avoids sqrt).
  lurek.math.exp( x )  -- Returns e raised to the power x.
  lurek.math.fbm( )  -- Returns fractal Brownian motion noise at (x, y).
  lurek.math.floor( x )  -- Returns the largest integer ≤ x.
  lurek.math.fmod( x, y )  -- Returns the remainder of x / y (fmod).
  lurek.math.fromHex( hex )  -- Parses a hex color string (#RRGGBB or #RRGGBBAA) into (r, g, b, a) floats.
  lurek.math.gammaToLinear( c )  -- Converts a gamma-encoded sRGB value to linear space.
  lurek.math.hermite( p0x, p0y, p1x, p1y, m0x, m0y, m1x, m1y )  -> Hermite  -- Creates a Hermite spline defined by two endpoints and tangents.
  lurek.math.hslToRgb( h, s, l )  -- Converts HSL (h: 0-360, s: 0-1, l: 0-1) to RGBA (r, g, b, a) floats.
  lurek.math.inBack( t )  -- Back ease-in — overshoots slightly before settling at the target.
  lurek.math.inBounce( t )  -- Bounce ease-in — reverse bounce effect that accelerates into the motion.
  lurek.math.inCubic( t )  -- Cubic ease-in — acceleration starts slowly then increases sharply.
  lurek.math.inElastic( t )  -- Elastic ease-in — spring-like overshoot at the beginning of the motion.
  lurek.math.inExpo( t )  -- Exponential ease-in — very slow start that accelerates sharply near the end.
  lurek.math.inOutBack( t )  -- Back ease-in-out — overshoot on both ends.
  lurek.math.inOutBounce( t )  -- Bounce ease-in-out — bouncing motion on both ends.
  lurek.math.inOutCubic( t )  -- Cubic ease-in-out — slow start and end with fast cubic middle.
  lurek.math.inOutElastic( t )  -- Elastic ease-in-out — spring-like oscillation on both ends.
  lurek.math.inOutExpo( t )  -- Exponential ease-in-out — very slow start and end with an exponential surge.
  lurek.math.inOutQuad( t )  -- Quadratic ease-in-out — slow start, fast middle, slow end.
  lurek.math.inOutQuart( t )  -- Quartic ease-in-out — very slow start and end with a sharp middle peak.
  lurek.math.inOutSine( t )  -- Sinusoidal ease-in-out — smooth S-curve based on cosine interpolation.
  lurek.math.inQuad( t )  -- Quadratic ease-in — acceleration that starts at zero and increases.
  lurek.math.inQuart( t )  -- Quartic ease-in — strongly delayed acceleration using a power-of-4 curve.
  lurek.math.inSine( t )  -- Sinusoidal ease-in — gentle acceleration based on a sine curve.
  lurek.math.inverseLerp( a, b, v )  -- Returns the interpolation parameter t for `v` in [a, b].
  lurek.math.isConvex( pts )  -- Returns true if the polygon (flat table {x1,y1,...}) is convex.
  lurek.math.lerp( a, b, t )  -- Linear interpolation between two numbers: a + (b - a) * t.
  lurek.math.lineIntersect( x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3, x4, y4 )  -- Infinite line intersection. Returns (x, y) or (nil, nil) if lines are parallel.
  lurek.math.linear( t )  -- Linear easing (identity).
  lurek.math.linearToGamma( c )  -- Converts a linear-space value to gamma-encoded sRGB.
  lurek.math.log( x, [b] )  -- Returns the natural log of x, or log base b if b is supplied.
  lurek.math.max( )  -- Returns the largest of the supplied numbers.
  lurek.math.min( )  -- Returns the smallest of the supplied numbers.
  lurek.math.newBezierCurve( points )  -> BezierCurve  -- Creates a new BezierCurve from a flat table of coordinates {x1,y1, x2,y2, ...}.
  lurek.math.newCircle( x, y, radius )  -> Circle  -- Creates a new Circle value type with the given centre and radius.
  lurek.math.newNoiseGenerator( [seed] )  -> NoiseGenerator  -- Creates a new seeded noise generator.
  lurek.math.newRandomGenerator( [seed] )  -> RandomGenerator  -- Creates a new random number generator with an optional seed.
  lurek.math.newSpatialHash( cell_size )  -> SpatialHash  -- Creates a new SpatialHash with the given cell size.
  lurek.math.newTransform( )  -> Transform  -- Creates a new Transform, optionally initialised from full parameters.
  lurek.math.newTween( duration, [easing_name] )  -> Tween  -- Creates a new Tween with the given duration and easing name.
  lurek.math.outBack( t )  -- Back ease-out — overshoots the target then snaps back into place.
  lurek.math.outBounce( t )  -- Bounce ease-out — simulates a ball bouncing against the target value.
  lurek.math.outCubic( t )  -- Cubic ease-out — rapid deceleration using a cubic power curve.
  lurek.math.outElastic( t )  -- Elastic ease-out — spring-like oscillation that settles at the target.
  lurek.math.outExpo( t )  -- Exponential ease-out — sharp initial speed that decelerates exponentially.
  lurek.math.outQuad( t )  -- Quadratic ease-out — deceleration that starts fast and ends at zero.
  lurek.math.outQuart( t )  -- Quartic ease-out — rapid deceleration using a power-of-4 curve.
  lurek.math.outSine( t )  -- Sinusoidal ease-out — gentle deceleration based on a cosine curve.
  lurek.math.perlin2d( x, y, [seed] )  -- Returns 2D Perlin noise at (x, y) with the given seed.
  lurek.math.perlin3d( x, y, z, [seed] )  -- Returns 3D Perlin noise at (x, y, z) with the given seed.
  lurek.math.pointInPolygon( pts, px, py )  -- Returns true if (px, py) is inside the polygon given as a flat {x1,y1,...} table.
  lurek.math.polygonArea( pts )  -- Returns the signed area of a polygon given as a flat {x1,y1,...} table.
  lurek.math.polygonCentroid( pts )  -- Returns the centroid (cx, cy) of a polygon given as a flat {x1,y1,...} table.
  lurek.math.polygonClip( pts, nx, ny, d )  -- Clips a polygon against a single half-plane using the Sutherland-Hodgman algorithm.
  lurek.math.polygonDifference( a, b )  -- Computes the approximate difference `A - B` (the part of A not covered by B).
  lurek.math.polygonIntersection( a, b )  -- Computes the intersection of two convex polygons using the Sutherland-Hodgman
  lurek.math.polygonUnion( a, b )  -- Computes the approximate union of two convex polygons as the convex hull of
  lurek.math.pow( x, y )  -- Returns x raised to the power y.
  lurek.math.rad( deg )  -- Converts degrees to radians.
  lurek.math.random( [a], [b] )  -- Returns a pseudo-random number in [0,1) with no args,
  lurek.math.randomInt( lo, hi )  -- Returns a pseudo-random integer in [lo, hi] (inclusive).
  lurek.math.rectFromCenter( cx, cy, w, h )  -- Creates a rectangle centered at (cx, cy) with the given width and height.
  lurek.math.rectUnion( x1, y1, w1, h1, x2, y2, w2, h2 )  -- Returns the union (bounding box) of two rectangles.
  lurek.math.remap( v, in_min, in_max, out_min, out_max )  -- Remaps `v` from [in_min, in_max] to [out_min, out_max].
  lurek.math.rgbToHsl( r, g, b )  -- Converts RGBA floats to HSL (h: 0-360, s: 0-1, l: 0-1).
  lurek.math.round( x )  -- Returns x rounded to the nearest integer (half-up).
  lurek.math.segmentIntersectsSegment( x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3, x4, y4 )  -- Tests if two line segments intersect. Returns (hit, ix?, iy?).
  lurek.math.sign( v )  -- Returns -1, 0, or 1 depending on the sign of `v`.
  lurek.math.simplex2d( x, y, [seed] )  -- Returns 2D Simplex noise at (x, y) with the given seed.
  lurek.math.simplexNoise( x, y, [z] )  -- Returns a simplex noise value in [-1, 1] for 2D or 3D coordinates.
  lurek.math.sin( x )  -- Returns the sine of x (radians).
  lurek.math.smoothstep( edge0, edge1, x )  -- Hermite smoothstep between `edge0` and `edge1`.
  lurek.math.sqrt( x )  -- Returns the square root of x.
  lurek.math.tan( x )  -- Returns the tangent of x (radians).
  lurek.math.triangulate( pts )  -- Triangulates a simple polygon given as a flat table {x1,y1, x2,y2, ...}.
  lurek.math.vec2( x, y )  -- Creates a 2D vector with x and y components.
  lurek.math.vec3( x, y, z )  -- Creates a 3D vector `{x, y, z}` table with numeric components.
  lurek.math.voronoi( points )  -- Computes the Voronoi diagram for a list of 2-D seed points.
```

**`AabbTree`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`AabbTree`].

```lua
  AabbTree:clear( )  -- Removes all entries from the tree.
  AabbTree:contains( id )  -- Returns true if an entry with the given id exists in the tree.
  AabbTree:insert( id, min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -- Inserts an entry with the given AABB into the tree.
  AabbTree:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the tree contains no entries.
  AabbTree:len( )  -- Returns the number of entries in the tree.
  AabbTree:query( min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -- Returns the ids of all entries whose AABBs overlap the query rectangle.
  AabbTree:queryPoint( x, y )  -- Returns the ids of all entries whose AABBs contain the given point.
  AabbTree:remove( id )  -- Removes the entry with the given id.
  AabbTree:update( id, min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -- Updates the AABB for an existing entry.
```

**`BezierCurve`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`BezierCurve`].

```lua
  BezierCurve:evaluate( t )  -- Evaluates the curve at parameter t, returning (x, y).
  BezierCurve:getControlPoint( index )  -> ControlPoint  -- Returns the control point at 1-based index as (x, y), or nil.
  BezierCurve:getControlPointCount( )  -> ControlPointCount  -- Returns the number of control points.
  BezierCurve:getDerivative( )  -> BezierCurve  -- Returns a new BezierCurve representing the first derivative.
  BezierCurve:insertControlPoint( x, y, [index] )  -- Inserts a control point. If index is given (1-based), inserts at that position.
  BezierCurve:length( )  -- Returns the approximate arc length of the curve.
  BezierCurve:removeControlPoint( index )  -- Removes a control point at 1-based index.
  BezierCurve:render( segments )  -- Renders the curve as a polyline with the given number of segments.
  BezierCurve:rotate( angle, ox, oy )  -- Rotates all control points around a pivot by angle radians.
  BezierCurve:scale( s, ox, oy )  -- Scales all control points around a pivot by factor s.
  BezierCurve:setControlPoint( index, x, y )  -- Sets the control point at 1-based index.
  BezierCurve:translate( dx, dy )  -- Translates all control points by (dx, dy).
```

**`CatmullRom`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`CatmullRomSpline`].

```lua
  CatmullRom:addPoint( x, y )  -- Appends a control point to the spline.
  CatmullRom:len( )  -- Number of control points.
  CatmullRom:removePoint( idx )  -- Removes the control point at `index` (0-based) and returns it.
  CatmullRom:sample( t )  -- Sample the spline at global t in [0, 1].
  CatmullRom:sampleSegment( seg, t )  -- Sample a specific segment at local t in [0, 1].
```

```lua
  NoiseGenerator:fbm( )  -- Returns fractal Brownian motion noise at (x, y).

  NoiseGenerator:perlin1d( x )  -- Returns 1D Perlin noise at x.

  NoiseGenerator:ridged( )  -- Returns ridged multi-fractal noise at (x, y).

  NoiseGenerator:simplex1d( x )  -- Returns 1D Simplex noise at x.
  NoiseGenerator:simplex2d( x, y )  -- Returns 2D Simplex noise at (x, y).
  NoiseGenerator:simplex3d( x, y, z )  -- Returns 3D Simplex noise at (x, y, z).
  NoiseGenerator:turbulence( )  -- Returns turbulence noise at (x, y).
  NoiseGenerator:warpDomain( x, y, strength )  -- Applies domain warping, returning offset (x, y).

```

```lua
  SpatialHash:clear( )  -- Removes all registered items from this spatial hash, leaving it empty.
```

```lua
  Transform:clone( )  -- Returns a copy of this transform.

  Transform:inverse( )  -> Transform  -- Returns a new Transform that undoes this transform.
  Transform:inverseTransformPoint( x, y )  -- Transforms a point from world space back to local space.
  Transform:reset( )  -- Resets the transform to identity.

  Transform:setTransformation( )  -- Replaces the transform with full transformation parameters.
  Transform:shear( kx, ky )  -- Applies horizontal and vertical shear factors to this transform matrix.
  Transform:transformPoint( x, y )  -- Transforms a point from local space to world space.
  Transform:translate( dx, dy )  -- Applies translation to the transform.
```

**`Tween`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Tween`].

```lua
  Tween:addValue( start, target )  -- Adds a start/target value pair. Returns the 1-based index.
  Tween:getAllValues( )  -> AllValues  -- Returns all interpolated values as a table.

  Tween:getDuration( )  -> Duration  -- Returns the tween duration in seconds.
  Tween:getEasingName( )  -> EasingName  -- Returns the easing function name.
  Tween:getTime( )  -> Time  -- Returns the current clock time.
  Tween:getValue( [index] )  -> Value  -- Returns the interpolated value at 1-based index, or all values as a
  Tween:getValueCount( )  -> ValueCount  -- Returns the number of values in this tween.
  Tween:isComplete( )  -- Returns true if the tween has finished.
  Tween:reset( )  -- Resets the tween elapsed time to zero, restarting the animation.
  Tween:set( t )  -- Alias for setTime(). Sets the clock to t, clamped to [0, duration].
  Tween:setTime( t )  -- Sets the clock to a specific time, clamped to [0, duration].
  Tween:update( dt )  -- Advances the clock by dt seconds. Returns true when complete.
```

**`Vec2`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Vec2`] value type.

```lua
  Vec2:angle( )  -- Returns the angle of this vector in radians (atan2(y, x)).
  Vec2:cross( other )  -- Returns the 2D cross product (scalar) with another vector.
  Vec2:distance( other )  -> Euclidean  -- Returns the Euclidean distance from this vector to another.
  Vec2:dot( other )  -- Returns the dot product with another vector.
  Vec2:length( )  -> Euclidean  -- Returns the Euclidean length of the vector.
  Vec2:lengthSquared( )  -- Returns the squared length of the vector (faster than length).
  Vec2:lerp( other, t )  -- Returns a linearly interpolated vector between this and other at parameter t.
  Vec2:normalize( )  -- Returns a unit-length copy of this vector. Returns zero if length is zero.
  Vec2:normalized( )  -- Compatibility alias for `normalize`.
  Vec2:perpendicular( )  -- Returns the perpendicular vector (-y, x).
  Vec2:reflect( normal )  -- Reflects this vector off a surface with the given normal.
  Vec2:rotate( angle )  -- Returns a new vector rotated by the given angle in radians.
  Vec2:x( )  -- Returns the horizontal component of the vector.
  Vec2:y( )  -- Returns the vertical component of the vector.
```

**`Vec3`** methods:

```lua
  Vec3:add( other )  -- Add another Vec3 and return the result.
  Vec3:cross( other )  -- Cross product with another Vec3.

  Vec3:dot( other )  -- Dot product with another Vec3.

  Vec3:lengthSquared( )  -- Returns the squared Euclidean length (avoids sqrt).
  Vec3:lerp( other, t )  -- Linear interpolation towards another Vec3.
  Vec3:normalize( )  -- Returns a unit-length version of this vector.
  Vec3:scale( s )  -- Scale this vector by a scalar and return the result.
  Vec3:sub( other )  -- Subtract another Vec3 and return the result.
```

## lurek.physics {#physics}

> 2D physics simulation via rapier2d: bodies, colliders, joints, sensors, raycasts.

```lua
  lurek.physics.attachShape( body_ud, shape_ud )  -- Attaches a standalone shape to a body as an additional fixture.
  lurek.physics.debugDraw( enable )  -- Enables or disables the physics debug overlay (AABB boxes and velocity vectors).
  lurek.physics.destroyWorld( world_ud )  -- Marks a physics world for destruction. Subsequent operations on the world
  lurek.physics.drawDebugGpu( world_ud, config_val )  -- Extracts collider geometry from a World and queues a GPU physics debug
  lurek.physics.getBody( world_ud, body_ud )  -> Body  -- Returns the position and velocity of a body (x, y, vx, vy).
  lurek.physics.getCollisions( world_ud )  -> Collisions  -- Returns all collision events from the last simulation step.
  lurek.physics.isSleepingAllowed( world_ud, body_ud )  -- Returns whether the body is allowed to sleep.
  lurek.physics.newBody( world_ud, x, y, bt )  -> Body  -- Creates a new rectangular body in the given world.
  lurek.physics.newCellular( width, height )  -> Cellular  -- Creates a falling-sand cellular automaton grid.
  lurek.physics.newChainShape( closed, coords )  -> ChainShape  -- Creates a chain shape userdata from flat variadic vertex pairs.
  lurek.physics.newCircleShape( r )  -> CircleShape  -- Creates a circle shape userdata.
  lurek.physics.newEdgeShape( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -> EdgeShape  -- Creates an edge (line segment) shape userdata.
  lurek.physics.newPolygonShape( )  -> PolygonShape  -- Creates a convex polygon shape userdata from flat variadic vertex pairs.
  lurek.physics.newRectangleShape( w, h )  -> RectangleShape  -- Creates a rectangle shape userdata.
  lurek.physics.newTerrain( width, height, cell_size, world_ud )  -> Terrain  -- Creates a destructible terrain grid.
  lurek.physics.newWorld( gx, gy )  -> World  -- Creates a new physics world with the given gravity vector.
  lurek.physics.setBodyVelocity( world_ud, body_ud, vx, vy )  -- Sets the velocity of a body.
  lurek.physics.setSleepingAllowed( world_ud, body_ud, allowed )  -- Sets whether the body is allowed to sleep.
  lurek.physics.step( world_ud, dt )  -- Advances the physics world by dt seconds.
  lurek.physics.testAABB( ax, ay, aw, ah, bx, by, bw, bh )  -- Returns true when two axis-aligned bounding boxes overlap.
  lurek.physics.testCircleAABB( cx, cy, cr, ax, ay, aw, ah )  -- Returns true when a circle overlaps an AABB.
  lurek.physics.testCircles( ax, ay, ar, bx, by, br )  -- Returns true when two circles overlap.
  lurek.physics.testPoint( px, py, ax, ay, aw, ah )  -- Returns true when point (px, py) lies inside the AABB.
```

**`Body`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a physics body accessed through its world.

```lua
  Body:applyAngularImpulse( impulse )  -- Applies an angular impulse.
  Body:applyForce( fx, fy )  -- Applies a continuous force to the body.
  Body:applyForceAtPoint( fx, fy, px, py )  -- Applies a force at a specific world-space point.
  Body:applyImpulse( ix, iy )  -- Applies a linear impulse to the body.
  Body:applyTorque( torque )  -- Applies a torque (rotational force).
  Body:destroy( )  -- Removes this body from the world.
  Body:getAngle( )  -> Angle  -- Returns the body angle in radians.
  Body:getAngularDamping( )  -> AngularDamping  -- Returns the angular damping coefficient.
  Body:getAngularVelocity( )  -> AngularVelocity  -- Returns the angular velocity in radians/s.
  Body:getFriction( )  -> Friction  -- Returns the body friction coefficient.
  Body:getGravityScale( )  -> GravityScale  -- Returns the per-body gravity multiplier.
  Body:getHeight( )  -> Height  -- Returns the height of this body's primary collider shape in world units.
  Body:getId( )  -> Id  -- Returns the body's integer ID.
  Body:getLayer( )  -> Layer  -- Returns the collision layer bitmask.
  Body:getLinearDamping( )  -> LinearDamping  -- Returns the linear damping coefficient.
  Body:getMask( )  -> Mask  -- Returns the collision mask bitmask.
  Body:getMass( )  -> Mass  -- Returns the body mass in kilograms used for force and impulse calculations.
  Body:getPosition( )  -> Position  -- Returns the body position (x, y).
  Body:getRestitution( )  -> Restitution  -- Returns the body restitution (bounciness).
  Body:getType( )  -> Type  -- Returns the body type as a string.
  Body:getVelocity( )  -> Velocity  -- Returns the body velocity (vx, vy).
  Body:getWidth( )  -> Width  -- Returns the width of this body's primary collider shape in world units.
  Body:getX( )  -- Returns the body X position.
  Body:getY( )  -- Returns the body Y position.
  Body:isBullet( )  -- Returns whether CCD is enabled.
  Body:isFixedRotation( )  -- Returns whether rotation is locked.
  Body:isSleeping( )  -- Returns true if this body is currently sleeping (inactive).
  Body:isSleepingAllowed( )  -- Returns whether the body can sleep.
  Body:setAngle( angle )  -- Sets the body angle in radians.
  Body:setAngularDamping( damping )  -- Sets the angular damping coefficient.
  Body:setAngularVelocity( omega )  -- Sets the angular velocity.
  Body:setBullet( bullet )  -- Enables or disables continuous collision detection (CCD) for fast-moving bodies.
  Body:setFixedRotation( fixed )  -- Locks or unlocks rotation.
  Body:setFriction( friction )  -- Sets the body friction coefficient.
  Body:setGravityScale( scale )  -- Sets the per-body gravity multiplier.
  Body:setLayer( layer )  -- Sets the collision layer bitmask.
  Body:setLinearDamping( damping )  -- Sets the linear damping coefficient.
  Body:setMask( mask )  -- Sets the collision mask bitmask.
  Body:setMass( mass )  -- Sets the body mass; affects how forces and impulses change velocity.
  Body:setPosition( x, y )  -- Teleports the body to the given world-space position, bypassing collision.
  Body:setRestitution( restitution )  -- Sets the body restitution (bounciness).
  Body:setSleepingAllowed( allowed )  -- Sets whether the body can sleep.
  Body:setType( bt )  -- Changes the body type: `"dynamic"`, `"static"`, or `"kinematic"`.
  Body:setVelocity( vx, vy )  -- Sets the body's linear velocity in world units per second.
  Body:sleep( )  -- Puts this body to sleep immediately.
  Body:wakeUp( )  -- Forcibly wakes up this body.
```

```lua
  Cellular:setCell( cx, cy, t )  -- Sets the material of a cell.

  Cellular:stepN( n )  -- Advances the simulation by `n` ticks.

```

**`PhysicsShape`** methods:

> Lua-side standalone shape object (circle, rectangle, edge, polygon, chain).

```lua
  PhysicsShape:destroy( )  -- Releases this shape handle (GC handles cleanup).
  PhysicsShape:getBoundingBox( )  -> BoundingBox  -- Returns the axis-aligned bounding box (x1, y1, x2, y2).
  PhysicsShape:getRadius( )  -> Radius  -- Returns the radius. Only valid for circle shapes.
  PhysicsShape:getType( )  -> Type  -- Returns the shape type string: "circle", "rectangle", "polygon", "edge", or "chain".
  PhysicsShape:setDensity( density )  -- Sets the density for this shape (used when attaching to a body).
  PhysicsShape:setFriction( friction )  -- Sets the friction coefficient.
  PhysicsShape:setRestitution( restitution )  -- Sets the restitution (bounciness) coefficient.
  PhysicsShape:setSensor( sensor )  -- Sets whether this shape is a sensor (non-colliding trigger).
```

**`Terrain`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a destructible [`TerrainMap`].

```lua
  Terrain:collapseColumns( )  -- Removes unsupported cells, returning the number of cells that fell.
  Terrain:fillAll( solid )  -- Sets every cell in the grid to `solid`.
  Terrain:fillCircle( wx, wy, radius, solid )  -- Fills a circle of cells centred at world position `(wx, wy)`.
  Terrain:fillRect( wx, wy, w, h, solid )  -- Fills a rectangular region of cells.
  Terrain:flush( )  -- Rebuilds physics bodies for all dirty chunks.
  Terrain:getCell( cx, cy )  -> Cell  -- Returns whether a cell is solid.
  Terrain:isDirty( )  -- Returns `true` when at least one chunk needs flushing.
  Terrain:loadFromBytes( data )  -- Loads terrain cell data from bytes produced by `toBytes`.
  Terrain:setCell( cx, cy, solid )  -- Sets a single terrain cell to solid or empty.
  Terrain:solidPositions( )  -- Returns the world-space centres of all solid cells as an array of `{x, y}` tables.
  Terrain:spawnDebris( positions, mass, restitution )  -- Spawns dynamic debris bodies at the given positions.
  Terrain:toBytes( )  -- Serialises the terrain grid to a byte string for save/load.
  Terrain:toImageData( sr, sg, sb, er, eg, eb )  -- Returns the terrain as an RGBA byte string.
```

**`World`** methods:

> Lua-side handle wrapping a physics World.

```lua
  World:addDistanceJoint( a, b, ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, len )  -- Creates a distance joint between two bodies.
  World:addFixture( )  -- Adds an extra fixture (collider) to a body.
  World:addFrictionJoint( a, b, ax, ay, max_f, max_t )  -- Creates a friction joint that resists relative motion.
  World:addGearJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -- Creates a gear joint (stub — falls back to weld joint).
  World:addMotorJoint( a, b, factor )  -- Creates a motor joint that drives body_b toward body_a.
  World:addMouseJoint( body_id, tx, ty, max_f )  -- Creates a mouse joint connecting a body to a target point.
  World:addPrismaticJoint( a, b, ax, ay, axis_x, axis_y )  -- Creates a prismatic (slider) joint between two bodies.
  World:addPulleyJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -- Creates a pulley joint (stub — falls back to weld joint).
  World:addRevoluteJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -- Creates a revolute (pin) joint between two bodies.
  World:addRopeJoint( a, b, ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, max )  -- Creates a rope joint with a maximum distance.
  World:addWeldJoint( a, b, ax, ay )  -- Creates a weld (rigid) joint between two bodies.
  World:addWheelJoint( a, b, ax, ay, axis_x, axis_y )  -- Creates a wheel joint (prismatic + rotation).
  World:addZone( x, y, w, h )  -- Creates a rectangular gravity/damping zone and returns a LuaZone handle.
  World:clear( )  -- Resets the world, removing all bodies and joints.
  World:clearBeginContact( )  -- Removes the begin-contact callback.
  World:clearBodyData( id )  -- Removes the Lua data attached to a body.
  World:clearBodyOneWay( id )  -- Removes the one-way platform flag from a body.
  World:clearEndContact( )  -- Removes the end-contact callback.
  World:destroyBody( id )  -- Removes a body from the world.
  World:destroyJoint( jid )  -- Removes a joint from the world.
  World:drawDebug( )  -- Draws physics objects for debugging
  World:fixtureCount( body_id )  -- Returns the number of fixtures on a body.
  World:getBeginContactEvents( )  -> BeginContactEvents  -- Returns begin-contact events from the last step.
  World:getBodyAtPoint( x, y )  -> BodyAtPoint  -- Returns the body ID at a world-space point, or nil.
  World:getBodyCCD( id )  -> BodyCCD  -- Returns whether CCD is enabled for a body.

  World:getBodyCount( )  -> BodyCount  -- Returns the total number of bodies in the world.
  World:getBodyData( id )  -> Lua  -- Returns the Lua data previously attached to a body, or nil if none is set.
  World:getBodyIds( )  -> BodyIds  -- Returns all body IDs in the world.
  World:getBodyOneWay( id )  -> BodyOneWay  -- Returns the one-way normal for a body, or nil if not configured.
  World:getBodyType( id )  -> BodyType  -- Returns the body type as a string.
  World:getCollisionEvents( )  -> CollisionEvents  -- Returns collision events from the last step.
  World:getContacts( )  -> Contacts  -- Returns all contact pairs from the narrow phase.
  World:getEndContactEvents( )  -> EndContactEvents  -- Returns end-contact events from the last step.
  World:getGravity( )  -> Gravity  -- Returns the gravity vector (gx, gy).
  World:getJointBodies( jid )  -> JointBodies  -- Returns the two body IDs connected by a joint.
  World:getJointBreakForce( jid )  -> JointBreakForce  -- Returns the break threshold for a joint, or nil if not set.
  World:getJointIds( )  -> JointIds  -- Returns a table of integer IDs for every joint attached to this world.
  World:getJointLimits( jid )  -> JointLimits  -- Returns the angular limits on a joint.
  World:getJointMotorSpeed( jid )  -> JointMotorSpeed  -- Returns the motor speed on a joint's angular axis.
  World:getJointType( jid )  -> JointType  -- Returns the type name of a joint.
  World:getMeter( )  -> Meter  -- Returns the pixels-per-meter scaling factor.
  World:getSolverIterations( )  -> SolverIterations  -- Returns the current number of solver iterations per step.
  World:getZoneEvents( )  -> ZoneEvents  -- Returns zone enter/leave events produced by the most recent step.
  World:isBodySleeping( id )  -- Returns true if a body is currently sleeping (inactive).
  World:jointCount( )  -- Returns the total number of joints.
  World:newBodies( specs )  -> Bodies  -- Creates multiple bodies in one call.
  World:newBody( x, y, bt )  -> Body  -- Creates a new rectangular body and adds it to the world.
  World:newChainBody( x, y, tbl, closed, bt )  -> ChainBody  -- Creates a new chain body from a flat vertex table and adds it to the world.
  World:newCircleBody( x, y, radius, bt )  -> CircleBody  -- Creates a new circular body and adds it to the world.
  World:newEdgeBody( x, y, x1, y1, x2, y2, bt )  -> EdgeBody  -- Creates a new edge (line segment) body and adds it to the world.
  World:newPolygonBody( x, y, tbl, bt )  -> PolygonBody  -- Creates a new polygon body from a flat vertex table and adds it to the world.
  World:queryAABB( x, y, w, h )  -- Returns body IDs within an axis-aligned bounding box.
  World:raycast( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Casts a ray and returns the nearest hit, or nil.

  World:raycastClosest( x1, y1, dx, dy, max_dist )  -- Casts a ray and returns the closest hit using the query pipeline.
  World:setBeginContact( f )  -- Registers a Lua function called with (bodyIdA, bodyIdB) when two
  World:setBodyCCD( id, enabled )  -- Enables or disables Continuous Collision Detection for a body.
  World:setBodyData( id, value )  -- Attaches arbitrary Lua data to a body for retrieval in collision callbacks.
  World:setBodyOneWay( id, nx, ny )  -- Marks a body as a one-way platform.  Bodies approaching from the
  World:setBodyType( id, bt )  -- Changes the simulation type of the body: `"dynamic"`, `"static"`, or `"kinematic"`.
  World:setEndContact( f )  -- Registers a Lua function called with (bodyIdA, bodyIdB) when two
  World:setFixtureFriction( body_id, fix_idx, friction )  -- Sets friction on a fixture by index.
  World:setFixtureRestitution( body_id, fix_idx, restitution )  -- Sets restitution on a fixture by index.
  World:setFixtureSensor( body_id, fix_idx, sensor )  -- Sets whether a fixture is a sensor.
  World:setGravity( gx, gy )  -- Sets the world gravity vector; default is `(0, 9.81)` (downward).
  World:setJointBreakForce( jid, f )  -- Sets the relative-velocity threshold above which a joint breaks.
  World:setJointLimits( jid, lower, upper )  -- Sets the angular limits on a joint.
  World:setJointLimitsEnabled( jid, enabled )  -- Enables or disables angular limits on a joint.
  World:setJointMotorSpeed( jid, speed )  -- Sets the motor speed on a joint's angular axis.
  World:setMeter( ppm )  -- Sets the pixels-per-meter scaling factor.
  World:setMouseJointTarget( jid, x, y )  -- Updates the target position of a mouse joint.
  World:setSolverIterations( n )  -- Sets the number of constraint solver iterations per step.
  World:sleepBody( id )  -- Puts a body to sleep immediately.
  World:step( dt )  -- Advances the physics simulation by dt seconds, firing onBeginContact /
  World:stepFixed( accum, step_dt, max_steps )  -- Steps the world using a fixed sub-step size to consume accumulated time.
  World:toPhysics( px )  -- Converts a pixel value to physics units.
  World:toPixels( m )  -- Converts a physics-unit value to pixels.
  World:wakeUpBody( id )  -- Forcibly wakes up a sleeping body.
```

**`Zone`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a [`PhysicsZone`] living inside a [`World`].

```lua
  Zone:destroy( )  -- Removes the zone from the world.
  Zone:getId( )  -> Id  -- Returns the zone's integer ID.
  Zone:setAngularDampingOverride( [value] )  -- Sets an optional angular damping override for bodies inside the zone.
  Zone:setCircle( cx, cy, radius )  -- Replaces the zone boundary with a circle.
  Zone:setEnabled( enabled )  -- Enables or disables the zone.
  Zone:setGravityDirectional( gx, gy )  -- Sets directional gravity inside the zone.
  Zone:setGravityPoint( cx, cy, strength )  -- Sets point-attractor gravity inside the zone.
  Zone:setGravityRepulsor( cx, cy, strength )  -- Sets point-repulsor gravity inside the zone.
  Zone:setGravityZero( )  -- Suppresses gravity inside the zone (zero-g pocket).
  Zone:setLayerMask( mask )  -- Sets the layer bitmask; only bodies whose `layer & mask != 0` are affected.
  Zone:setLinearDampingOverride( [value] )  -- Sets an optional linear damping override for bodies inside the zone.
  Zone:setPriority( priority )  -- Sets the zone priority; higher values win over lower when zones overlap.
```

```lua
  lurek.filesystem.pollWatchers( )  -- Polls all watched paths and returns an array of paths that changed since the
  lurek.filesystem.read( path )  -- Reads a text file and returns its contents as a string.
  lurek.filesystem.readAsync( path )  -- Starts loading a file in the background and returns an opaque handle.
  lurek.filesystem.remove( path )  -- Permanently deletes a file or empty directory from the save directory.
  lurek.filesystem.removeDir( path )  -- Recursively deletes a directory and all its contents within `save/`.
  lurek.filesystem.setIdentity( name )  -- Sets the identity string that names the game's sandboxed save-data directory.
  lurek.filesystem.stat( path )  -- Returns lightweight file statistics for the given path.
  lurek.filesystem.toAbsolutePath( path )  -- Resolves a path relative to the game root to an absolute OS path string.
  lurek.filesystem.unmount( mp )  -- Removes a virtual mount layer by mountpoint.

  lurek.filesystem.watchPath( path )  -- Adds `path` to the polled file-watch list.
  lurek.filesystem.write( path, data )  -- Writes a string to a file in the save directory.
```

**`FileData`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`FileData`] buffer.

```lua
  FileData:getFilename( )  -> Filename  -- Returns the virtual path this data was loaded from.
  FileData:getSize( )  -> Size  -- Returns the file size in bytes.
  FileData:getString( )  -> String  -- Returns the file content as a Lua string.
```

**`FileHandle`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`FileHandle`] with interior mutability.

```lua
  FileHandle:close( )  -- Flushes any pending writes and closes the file handle.
  FileHandle:flush( )  -- Flushes all buffered writes to disk without closing the handle.
  FileHandle:getMode( )  -> Mode  -- Returns the access mode the file was opened with.
  FileHandle:getSize( )  -> Size  -- Returns the size of the open file in bytes.
  FileHandle:isEOF( )  -- Returns whether the read cursor has reached the end of the file.
  FileHandle:read( [count] )  -- Reads bytes from the file, returning them as a string.
  FileHandle:readLine( )  -- Reads the next line from the file without the trailing newline.
  FileHandle:seek( pos )  -- Seeks the file position to the given byte offset from the start.
  FileHandle:tell( )  -- Returns the current read/write byte offset from the start of the file.
  FileHandle:write( data )  -- Writes a string to the file and returns the number of bytes written.
```

**`ZipMount`** methods:

> Lua userdata wrapper around a [`ZipMount`].

```lua
  ZipMount:contains( virtual_path )  -- Returns true if `virtual_path` exists inside this ZIP mount.
  ZipMount:listFiles( )  -- Returns a sorted array of all virtual paths exposed by this ZIP mount.
  ZipMount:prefix( )  -- Returns the virtual path prefix this archive was mounted under.
  ZipMount:readFile( virtual_path )  -- Reads a file from the ZIP and returns it as a string of bytes.
```
