## lurek.event {#event}

> Event queue: push/poll custom events between systems.

```lua
  lurek.event.clear( )  -- Discards all pending events in the queue.
  lurek.event.clearHistory( )  -- Clears all recorded event history.
  lurek.event.enableHistory( capacity )  -- Enables event history recording, keeping the last `capacity` pushed events.
  lurek.event.exit( [code] )  -- Pushes an exit event, requesting the engine to stop.
  lurek.event.flushDeferred( )  -- Moves all buffered deferred events into the main event queue and clears the buffer.
  lurek.event.getHistory( )  -> History  -- Returns an array of recent events as `{name, args}` tables.
  lurek.event.newSignal( )  -> Signal  -- Creates a new pub-sub Signal dispatcher.
  lurek.event.poll( )  -- Returns an iterator function that pops events from the queue.
  lurek.event.pump( )  -- Syncs OS-level events into the queue (no-op in Lurek2D push model).
  lurek.event.push( ... )  -- Adds an event item to the end of the event queue for processing.
  lurek.event.pushDeferred( ... )  -- Pushes a named event to the deferred buffer; it will not reach the main queue
  lurek.event.quit( )  -- Alias for `exit()` â€” requests the engine to stop at the end of the current frame.
  lurek.event.restart( )  -- Requests that the engine restart at the beginning of the next frame.
  lurek.event.wait( [timeout] )  -- Blocks until the next event arrives or the optional timeout elapses.
```

**`Signal`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Signal`] with registry-stored callbacks.

```lua
  Signal:clear( name )  -- Removes all callbacks for the named event.
  Signal:clearAll( )  -- Removes all callbacks across all events.
  Signal:connect( name, func )  -- Subscribes to an event name or wildcard pattern. When the pattern contains
  Signal:emit( ... )  -- Emits the named event, calling all registered callbacks with extra arguments.
  Signal:getCount( name )  -> Count  -- Returns the callback count for the named event.
  Signal:getTotalCount( )  -> TotalCount  -- Returns the total callback count across all events.
  Signal:once( name, callback )  -- Registers a one-shot callback that fires at most once then auto-removes itself.
  Signal:register( name, callback )  -- Registers a callback for the named event and returns its handle ID.
  Signal:registerWithFilter( name, callback, filter )  -- Registers a callback with a filter predicate. The callback only fires if the
  Signal:remove( handle )  -- Removes a subscription by handle ID.
  Signal:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Signal:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if the given type name matches this object's type or any parent type.
```

## lurek.system {#system}

> System info: OS, clipboard, locale, memory, Lurek2D version.

```lua
  lurek.system.errorSnapshot( msg )  -- Serialises an engine error message to a compact JSON string.
  lurek.system.getArch( )  -> CPU  -- Returns the CPU architecture string for the current machine.
  lurek.system.getArgs( )  -> Args  -- Returns the command-line arguments as a table.
  lurek.system.getBatchResults( results )  -> BatchResults  -- Returns the output table from the most recently completed runBatch call.
  lurek.system.getClipboardText( )  -> ClipboardText  -- Returns the current contents of the system clipboard.
  lurek.system.getDebugOverlay( )  -> DebugOverlay  -- Returns whether the debug overlay is currently visible.
  lurek.system.getEnv( name )  -> Env  -- Returns the value of an environment variable, or nil if not set.
  lurek.system.getInfo( )  -> Info  -- Returns a table of system information including OS name, CPU model, and installed RAM.
  lurek.system.getLastError( )  -> LastError  -- Returns the last unhandled error message, or nil.
  lurek.system.getLogLevel( )  -> LogLevel  -- Returns the name of the current minimum log level for runtime messages.
  lurek.system.getMemorySize( )  -> MemorySize  -- Returns the total amount of installed system RAM in megabytes.
  lurek.system.getMessage( id )  -> Message  -- Resolves a stable runtime message ID such as 'L001' to its human-readable text.
  lurek.system.getMessageCount( )  -> MessageCount  -- Returns the total number of message entries loaded into the runtime message catalog.
  lurek.system.getOS( )  -> OS  -- Returns the host operating system name ('Windows', 'Linux', 'macOS').
  lurek.system.getPowerInfo( )  -> PowerInfo  -- Returns battery state, percentage charged, and estimated time remaining.
  lurek.system.getPreferredLocales( )  -> PreferredLocales  -- Returns an ordered list of the user's preferred locale strings (e.g. 'en-US').
  lurek.system.getProcessorCount( )  -> ProcessorCount  -- Returns the number of logical CPU cores available.
  lurek.system.getVersion( )  -> Lurek2D  -- Returns the Lurek2D engine version string.
  lurek.system.hasMessage( id )  -- Returns true when the runtime message catalog contains the given stable message ID.
  lurek.system.log( level, message )  -- Emit a log message from Lua at the specified level.
  lurek.system.openURL( url )  -- Opens a URL in the system's default browser.
  lurek.system.parseArgs( [args] )  -- Parses a command-line argument string and returns a structured key/value table.
  lurek.system.runBatch( tasks, [opts] )  -- Runs a list of shell commands in parallel and returns immediately without blocking.
  lurek.system.setClipboardText( text )  -- Replaces the system clipboard contents with the given string.
  lurek.system.setDebugOverlay( enabled )  -- Shows or hides the FPS/draw-call debug overlay.
  lurek.system.setLogLevel( level )  -- Sets the minimum severity level for runtime log messages.
```

## lurek.thread {#thread}

> Background threads and inter-thread channels for Lua coroutines.

```lua
  lurek.thread.async( code, ... )  -- Starts a one-shot background computation and returns a Promise.
  lurek.thread.getChannel( name )  -> Channel  -- Gets or creates a named global channel shared across threads.
  lurek.thread.newChannel( )  -> Channel  -- Creates an unnamed thread-safe channel for inter-thread communication.
  lurek.thread.newPool( size, code )  -> Pool  -- Creates a thread pool of N workers all running the same Lua code.
  lurek.thread.newThread( code )  -> Thread  -- Creates a new background thread from a Lua code string.
```

**`Channel`** methods:

> A synchronized message queue for cross-VM communication.

```lua
  Channel:clear( )  -- Clears all items from the channel.
  Channel:demand( [timeout] )  -- Blocks until a value is available or the timeout expires, then removes and returns it.
  Channel:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the number of items in the channel.
  Channel:peek( )  -- Retrieves the value from the channel without removing it.
  Channel:pop( )  -- Retrieves and removes a value from the channel.
  Channel:popBytes( )  -- Pops a bytes value from the channel and returns it as a Lua string.
  Channel:popTable( )  -- Pops a value from the channel expecting a table.
  Channel:push( value )  -- Pushes a value to the channel.
  Channel:pushBytes( data )  -- Pushes raw binary data (a Lua string treated as a byte array) to the channel.
  Channel:pushTable( value )  -- Serializes a Lua table and pushes it to the channel.
  Channel:supply( value )  -- Blocks until the channel has space, then adds the value.
  Channel:type( )  -- Returns the type of the object.
  Channel:typeOf( name )  -- Checks if the object is of the specified type.
```

**`Promise`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a one-shot [`Promise`].

```lua
  Promise:getError( )  -> Error  -- Returns the worker error string if the promise failed, otherwise nil.
  Promise:isDone( )  -- Returns true if the promise has a result or has errored (non-blocking).
  Promise:result( )  -- Pops and returns the promise result, or nil if not yet ready.
  Promise:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Promise:typeOf( name )  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
```

**`ThreadHandle`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a background [`LuaThread`].

```lua
  ThreadHandle:getError( )  -> Error  -- Returns the error message if the thread failed, or nil.
  ThreadHandle:isRunning( )  -- Returns whether the thread is currently executing.
  ThreadHandle:start( ... )  -- Launches the background thread, passing optional arguments via varargs.
  ThreadHandle:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  ThreadHandle:typeOf( name )  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
  ThreadHandle:wait( )  -- Blocks the calling thread until the background thread finishes.
```

**`ThreadPool`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`ThreadPool`].

```lua
  ThreadPool:collect( )  -- Retrieves the next result from the pool's output channel (non-blocking).
  ThreadPool:getInputChannel( )  -> InputChannel  -- Returns the shared input Channel (main â†’ workers).
  ThreadPool:getOutputChannel( )  -> OutputChannel  -- Returns the shared output Channel (workers â†’ main).
  ThreadPool:join( )  -- Blocks until all workers in the pool have finished execution.
  ThreadPool:size( )  -- Returns the number of workers in this pool.
  ThreadPool:submit( value )  -- Submits a value to the pool's input channel for processing by a worker.
  ThreadPool:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  ThreadPool:typeOf( name )  -- Returns whether this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.particle {#particle}

> CPU particle system: emitters, modifiers, rendering.

```lua
  lurek.particle.fromTOML( path )  -- Creates a new particle system from a TOML config file.
  lurek.particle.newSystem( [config] )  -> System  -- Creates a new particle system and stores it in the engine pool.
  lurek.particle.newTrail( lifetime, start_width )  -> Trail  -- Creates a new trail ribbon effect.
```

**`ParticleSystem`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a particle system stored in SharedState.

```lua
  ParticleSystem:addAttractor( x, y, strength, radius )  -- Adds a gravity well that pulls (positive strength) or repels
  ParticleSystem:addSubEmitter( config_tbl, [burst_count] )  -- Attaches a sub-emitter that bursts when a particle dies.
  ParticleSystem:addSubSystem( config_tbl )  -- Adds a child emitter that updates and renders with this system.
  ParticleSystem:clearAttractors( )  -- Removes all attractors from this particle system.
  ParticleSystem:clearBounds( )  -- Removes the bounding rectangle so particles can move freely.
  ParticleSystem:clone( )  -- Creates a copy of this particle system (config only, no live particles).
  ParticleSystem:count( )  -- Returns the number of living particles.
  ParticleSystem:drawToImage( w, h )  -- Renders all live particles to a CPU ImageData.
  ParticleSystem:emit( count )  -- Emits a burst of the given number of particles.
  ParticleSystem:getAttractorCount( )  -> AttractorCount  -- Returns the number of attractors currently registered on this system.
  ParticleSystem:getBufferSize( )  -> BufferSize  -- Returns the maximum particle count.
  ParticleSystem:getColors( )  -> Colors  -- Returns color keyframes as a table of {r,g,b,a} tables.
  ParticleSystem:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the number of living particles (alias for count).
  ParticleSystem:getDirection( )  -> Direction  -- Returns emission direction in radians.
  ParticleSystem:getEmissionArea( )  -> EmissionArea  -- Returns emission area: dist-string, w, h.
  ParticleSystem:getEmissionRate( )  -> EmissionRate  -- Returns particles emitted per second.
  ParticleSystem:getEmitterLifetime( )  -> EmitterLifetime  -- Returns the emitter lifetime.
  ParticleSystem:getFlipbook( )  -> Flipbook  -- Returns the current flipbook configuration as `(cols, rows, fps)`, or `nil` if not set.
  ParticleSystem:getGravity( )  -> Gravity  -- Returns the gravity acceleration applied to particles as two numbers `gx, gy`.
  ParticleSystem:getInsertMode( )  -> InsertMode  -- Returns the insert mode as a string.
  ParticleSystem:getLinearAcceleration( )  -> LinearAcceleration  -- Returns linear acceleration range.
  ParticleSystem:getLinearDamping( )  -> LinearDamping  -- Returns linear damping range.
  ParticleSystem:getOffset( )  -> Offset  -- Returns the render origin offset.
  ParticleSystem:getParticleLifetime( )  -> ParticleLifetime  -- Returns min and max particle lifetime.
  ParticleSystem:getPosition( )  -> Position  -- Returns the emitter world position.
  ParticleSystem:getRadialAcceleration( )  -> RadialAcceleration  -- Returns radial acceleration range.
  ParticleSystem:getRotation( )  -> Rotation  -- Returns initial rotation range.
  ParticleSystem:getShape( )  -> Shape  -- Returns the particle draw shape as a string.
  ParticleSystem:getSizeVariation( )  -> SizeVariation  -- Returns the maximum random size variation applied to newly emitted particles.
  ParticleSystem:getSizes( )  -> Sizes  -- Returns size keyframes as a Lua table.
  ParticleSystem:getSpeed( )  -> Speed  -- Returns min/max initial speed.
  ParticleSystem:getSpin( )  -> Spin  -- Returns angular velocity range.
  ParticleSystem:getSpinVariation( )  -> SpinVariation  -- Returns the maximum random angular velocity variation for new particles.
  ParticleSystem:getSpread( )  -> Spread  -- Returns the half-angle spread in radians for the emission cone.
  ParticleSystem:getTangentialAcceleration( )  -> TangentialAcceleration  -- Returns tangential acceleration range.
  ParticleSystem:hasRelativeRotation( )  -- Returns whether relative rotation is enabled.
  ParticleSystem:isActive( )  -- Returns true if the emitter is currently emitting or has live particles.
  ParticleSystem:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if there are no live particles.
  ParticleSystem:isFull( )  -- Returns true if the system has reached max_particles.
  ParticleSystem:isPaused( )  -- Returns true if the emitter is paused.
  ParticleSystem:isStopped( )  -- Returns true if the emitter is stopped.
  ParticleSystem:moveTo( x, y )  -- Moves the emitter to the given world position.
  ParticleSystem:pause( )  -- Pauses particle emission; existing particles continue to simulate.
  ParticleSystem:release( )  -- Removes the particle system from the engine, freeing its slot.
  ParticleSystem:render( [ox], [oy] )  -- Renders all live particles to the GPU command queue.
  ParticleSystem:reset( )  -- Removes all particles and resets the emitter.
  ParticleSystem:resume( )  -- Resumes a paused emitter.
  ParticleSystem:setBounds( xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, restitution )  -- Constrains all particles to an axis-aligned bounding rectangle.
  ParticleSystem:setBufferSize( n )  -- Sets the maximum number of particles (resizes the pool).
  ParticleSystem:setColors( ... )  -- Sets color keyframes. Each arg is a table {r, g, b, a}.
  ParticleSystem:setCustomEmissionShape( cb )  -- Sets a Lua function that returns (offset_x, offset_y) for each newly spawned
  ParticleSystem:setDirection( dir )  -- Sets emission direction in radians.
  ParticleSystem:setEmissionArea( dist, w, h, [angle], [dir_rel] )  -- Sets emission area distribution and size.
  ParticleSystem:setEmissionRate( rate )  -- Sets particles emitted per second.
  ParticleSystem:setEmitterLifetime( t )  -- Sets how long the emitter runs before auto-stopping. Negative = infinite.
  ParticleSystem:setFlipbook( cols, rows, fps )  -- Configures sprite-sheet flipbook animation by dividing the texture into a grid.
  ParticleSystem:setGravity( gx, gy )  -- Sets the gravity acceleration applied to all active particles each frame.
  ParticleSystem:setInsertMode( mode )  -- Sets the insert mode: "top", "bottom", or "random".
  ParticleSystem:setLinearAcceleration( xmin, ymin, xmax, ymax )  -- Sets linear acceleration range.
  ParticleSystem:setLinearDamping( min, max )  -- Sets linear damping range.
  ParticleSystem:setOffset( ox, oy )  -- Sets the render origin offset.
  ParticleSystem:setOnDeathBatch( cb )  -- Sets a Lua function called after each update() with all particles that died
  ParticleSystem:setParticleLifetime( min, max )  -- Sets min and max particle lifetime in seconds.
  ParticleSystem:setPosition( x, y )  -- Sets the emitter world position.
  ParticleSystem:setRadialAcceleration( min, max )  -- Sets radial acceleration range.
  ParticleSystem:setRelativeRotation( v )  -- Sets whether particle rotation follows velocity direction.
  ParticleSystem:setRotation( min, max )  -- Sets initial rotation range in radians.
  ParticleSystem:setShape( shape )  -- Sets the particle draw shape.
  ParticleSystem:setSizeVariation( v )  -- Sets size variation (0â€“1).
  ParticleSystem:setSizes( ... )  -- Sets size keyframes (varargs: each number is one keyframe).
  ParticleSystem:setSpeed( min, max )  -- Sets min/max initial speed.
  ParticleSystem:setSpin( min, max )  -- Sets angular velocity range.
  ParticleSystem:setSpinVariation( v )  -- Sets spin variation (0â€“1).
  ParticleSystem:setSpread( spread )  -- Sets emission spread (half-angle cone) in radians.
  ParticleSystem:setTangentialAcceleration( min, max )  -- Sets tangential acceleration range.
  ParticleSystem:start( )  -- Starts or restarts particle emission.
  ParticleSystem:stop( )  -- Stops particle emission immediately.
  ParticleSystem:subSystemCount( )  -- Returns the number of direct child sub-systems attached to this emitter.
  ParticleSystem:toImage( w, h )  -- Alias for `drawToImage`. Renders all live particles to a CPU ImageData.
  ParticleSystem:type( )  -- Returns the type name "ParticleSystem".
  ParticleSystem:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this matches the given type name.
  ParticleSystem:update( dt )  -- Advances the particle simulation by dt seconds.
  ParticleSystem:warmUp( seconds )  -- Pre-simulates the particle system for `seconds` so it appears fully
```

**`Trail`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Trail`] ribbon effect.

```lua
  Trail:clear( )  -- Removes all trail points.
  Trail:drawToImage( w, h )  -- Renders the trail ribbon to a CPU ImageData.
  Trail:getLifetime( )  -> Lifetime  -- Returns the trail point lifetime in seconds.
  Trail:getPointCount( )  -> PointCount  -- Returns the number of active trail points.
  Trail:getWidth( )  -> Width  -- Returns the start and end width.
  Trail:pushPoint( x, y )  -- Appends a new point to the trail head.
  Trail:setHeadColor( r, g, b, a )  -- Sets the colour at the newest end of the trail.
  Trail:setLifetime( lifetime )  -- Sets how long each trail point persists in seconds.
  Trail:setMinDistance( distance )  -- Sets the minimum distance between trail points.
  Trail:setTailColor( r, g, b, a )  -- Sets the colour at the oldest end of the trail.
  Trail:setWidth( start, [end] )  -- Sets the start and end width of the trail ribbon.
  Trail:update( dt )  -- Ages trail points and removes expired ones.
```

## lurek.tilemap {#tilemap}

> Tile maps: chunk loading, tile queries, navigation grid.

```lua
  lurek.tilemap.fromLDtk( json_str, [level_name] )  -- Parses an LDtk JSON export string and returns a TileMap.
  lurek.tilemap.fromScreenHex( sx, sy, size )  -- Converts screen position back to axial hex coordinates (pointy-top layout).
  lurek.tilemap.fromScreenIso( sx, sy, tw, th )  -- Converts screen position back to tile coordinates for diamond isometric projection.
  lurek.tilemap.hexArea( q, r, radius )  -- Returns all hex cells within radius distance (filled hex circle) as a table.
  lurek.tilemap.hexDistance( q1, r1, q2, r2 )  -- Returns the hex distance between two axial coordinates.
  lurek.tilemap.hexLine( q1, r1, q2, r2 )  -- Returns all hex cells along a line between two axial coordinates as a table.
  lurek.tilemap.hexNeighbors( q, r )  -- Returns the six axial neighbor coordinates as a table of {q, r} pairs.
  lurek.tilemap.hexReflect( q, r, center_q, center_r, axis )  -- Reflects hex coordinates across an axis through the center.
  lurek.tilemap.hexRing( q, r, radius )  -- Returns all cells at exactly radius distance from (q, r) as a table.
  lurek.tilemap.hexRotate( q, r, center_q, center_r, steps )  -- Rotates hex coordinates around a center by steps x 60 degrees clockwise.
  lurek.tilemap.hexRound( q, r )  -- Rounds fractional axial coordinates to the nearest hex cell.
  lurek.tilemap.hexSpiral( q, r, radius )  -- Returns all hex cells from center outward to radius, ring by ring, as a table.
  lurek.tilemap.isoDirectionFromAngle( angle )  -- Snaps an angle (in radians) to the nearest isometric direction (1-4).
  lurek.tilemap.isoDirectionName( direction )  -- Returns the name of an isometric direction (1-4).
  lurek.tilemap.isoRotate( direction, steps )  -- Rotates an isometric direction (1-4) clockwise by steps.
  lurek.tilemap.loadTMX( xml )  -- Parses a TMX XML string and returns a table with map metadata and layers.
  lurek.tilemap.newAutoTileSheet( tile_w, tile_h, layout_str )  -> AutoTileSheet  -- Creates a new AutoTileSheet with the given tile dimensions and layout.
  lurek.tilemap.newChunkMap( [chunk_size] )  -> ChunkMap  -- Creates a new ChunkMap with the given chunk size.
  lurek.tilemap.newIsoMap( )  -> IsoMap  -- Creates a new IsoMap with no levels.
  lurek.tilemap.newLargeMapRenderer( tile_w, tile_h )  -> LargeMapRenderer  -- Creates a LargeMapRenderer for chunk-level occlusion culling on maps > 200Ă—200 tiles.
  lurek.tilemap.newMapBlock( width, height, [layers], [segment_size] )  -> MapBlock  -- Creates a new MapBlock with the given dimensions.
  lurek.tilemap.newMapGen( )  -> MapGen  -- Creates a MapGen from a MapGroup, a preset name or dimensions, and a segment size.
  lurek.tilemap.newMapGroup( name )  -> MapGroup  -- Creates a new empty MapGroup with the given name.
  lurek.tilemap.newMapScript( )  -> MapScript  -- Creates a new empty MapScript procedural generation script.
  lurek.tilemap.newTileMap( tile_width, tile_height, [chunk_size] )  -> TileMap  -- Creates a new TileMap with the given tile size and chunk size.
  lurek.tilemap.newTileSet( )  -> TileSet  -- Creates a new TileSet with the given atlas layout parameters.
  lurek.tilemap.toScreenHex( q, r, size )  -- Converts axial hex coordinates to screen position (pointy-top layout).
  lurek.tilemap.toScreenIso( tx, ty, tw, th )  -- Converts tile coordinates to screen position using diamond isometric projection.
```

**`AutoTileSheet`** methods:

```lua
  AutoTileSheet:applyToTileSet( ts_ud, type_name, [start_gid] )  -- Applies autotile rules from this sheet to a TileSet.

  AutoTileSheet:getLayout( )  -> Layout  -- Returns the layout variant as a string.
  AutoTileSheet:getQuad( tile_id )  -> Quad  -- Returns the atlas region rectangle for the 1-based tile ID.
  AutoTileSheet:getTileCount( )  -> TileCount  -- Returns the number of tiles in this sheet.
  AutoTileSheet:getTileForBitmask( bitmask )  -> TileForBitmask  -- Returns the 1-based tile ID for a given bitmask, or nil.
  AutoTileSheet:getTileHeight( )  -> TileHeight  -- Returns the tile height in pixels.
  AutoTileSheet:getTileWidth( )  -> TileWidth  -- Returns the tile width in pixels.
```

**`ChunkMap`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`ChunkMap`].

```lua
  ChunkMap:chunkTileRange( cx, cy )  -- Returns the tile coordinate range for chunk (cx, cy) as (x0, y0, x1, y1).
  ChunkMap:clearTile( x, y )  -- Clears the tile at (x, y) by setting its GID to 0.
  ChunkMap:fillRect( x0, y0, x1, y1, gid )  -- Fills the rectangular tile region with a GID.

  ChunkMap:setTile( x, y, gid )  -- Sets the GID at tile coordinate (x, y).
  ChunkMap:unloadChunk( cx, cy )  -- Removes the chunk at chunk coordinates (cx, cy) from memory.
```

**`IsoMap`** methods:

```lua
  IsoMap:addLevel( )  -- Appends a new empty Z-level and returns its 1-based index.
```

```lua
  LargeMapRenderer:setCamera( x, y, zoom )  -- Updates the camera position and zoom used for visibility culling.
  LargeMapRenderer:setChunkSize( size )  -- Sets the chunk size used for culling (default 16).
  LargeMapRenderer:setLodEnabled( enabled )  -- Enables or disables level-of-detail rendering for distant chunks.
  LargeMapRenderer:setLodThresholds( levels )  -- Sets the distance thresholds (in tile units) at which each LOD level activates.
```

**`TileMap`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`TileMap`].

```lua
  TileMap:addLayer( name, w, h )  -- Adds a new empty layer and returns its 1-based index.
  TileMap:addTileSet( ts_ud )  -- Adds a tileset to this map.
  TileMap:applyAutoTile( layer, type_name )  -- Applies 4-bit cardinal autotile rules to every tile on layer (1-based).
  TileMap:applyAutoTile8( layer, type_name )  -- Applies 8-bit directional autotile rules to every tile on layer (1-based).
  TileMap:applyAutoTile8At( layer, x, y, type_name )  -- Applies 8-bit directional autotile at a single cell and its 3x3 neighborhood (1-based).
  TileMap:applyAutoTileAt( layer, x, y, type_name )  -- Applies 4-bit cardinal autotile at a single cell and its 3x3 neighborhood (1-based).
  TileMap:checkEntities( layer, entities )  -- Checks a list of entity positions against registered tile callbacks and fires matches.
  TileMap:clearTile( layer, x, y )  -- Clears a tile (sets GID to 0) at (x, y) on the given layer (1-based).
  TileMap:drawToImage( tile_size )  -- Renders the tile map to a CPU ImageData using the given tile pixel size.
  TileMap:fill( layer, gid )  -- Fills an entire layer with the given GID (1-based layer).
  TileMap:fireTileExit( gid, entity, tx, ty )  -- Fire the tile exit callback for the given GID (call when entity leaves tile).
  TileMap:fireTileStep( gid, entity, tx, ty )  -- Fire the tile step callback for the given GID (call each frame while entity is on tile).
  TileMap:getChunkSize( )  -> ChunkSize  -- Returns the chunk size used for spatial partitioning.
  TileMap:getLayerColor( idx )  -> RGBA  -- Returns the RGBA tint color of a layer.
  TileMap:getLayerCount( )  -> LayerCount  -- Returns the number of layers.
  TileMap:getLayerName( idx )  -> LayerName  -- Returns the name of a layer by 1-based index.
  TileMap:getLayerOffset( idx )  -> LayerOffset  -- Returns the pixel offset of a layer.
  TileMap:getLayerParallax( idx )  -> LayerParallax  -- Returns the parallax factor of a layer.
  TileMap:getLayerVisible( idx )  -> LayerVisible  -- Returns layer visibility.
  TileMap:getOrientation( )  -> Orientation  -- Returns the map orientation as a string ("topdown", "sideview", "isometric", or "hexago...
  TileMap:getTile( layer, x, y )  -> GID  -- Returns the GID at (x, y) on the given layer (1-based).
  TileMap:getTileDimensions( )  -> TileDimensions  -- Returns tile dimensions as (width, height).
  TileMap:getTileHeight( )  -> TileHeight  -- Returns the tile height in pixels.
  TileMap:getTileSet( idx )  -> TileSet  -- Returns a tileset by 1-based index, or nil if out of range.
  TileMap:getTileSetCount( )  -> TileSetCount  -- Returns the number of tilesets attached to this map.
  TileMap:getTileWidth( )  -> TileWidth  -- Returns the tile width in pixels.
  TileMap:getViewport( )  -> Viewport  -- Returns the viewport as (x, y, w, h) or nil if not set.
  TileMap:isSolid( layer, x, y )  -- Returns true if the tile at (x, y) on layer is solid (1-based).
  TileMap:onTileEnter( gid, func )  -- Registers a callback fired when any entity's tile GID matches `gid`.
  TileMap:onTileExit( gid, func )  -- Register a callback for when an entity exits a tile with the given GID.
  TileMap:onTileStep( gid, func )  -- Register a callback for when an entity steps on a tile with the given GID.
  TileMap:rectOverlapsSolid( layer, x, y, w, h )  -- Returns true if any solid tile overlaps the given world-space rectangle on layer (1-bas...
  TileMap:render( [ox], [oy] )  -- Renders the tile map to the screen at the given offset.
  TileMap:setLayerColor( idx, r, g, b, a )  -- Sets the RGBA tint color for a layer.
  TileMap:setLayerOffset( idx, ox, oy )  -- Sets the pixel offset for a layer.
  TileMap:setLayerParallax( idx, px, py )  -- Sets the parallax scrolling factor for a layer.
  TileMap:setLayerVisible( idx, visible )  -- Shows or hides a tile layer by its 1-based index.
  TileMap:setOrientation( orientation )  -- Sets the map orientation from a string ("topdown", "sideview", "isometric", or "hexagon...
  TileMap:setTile( layer, x, y, gid )  -- Sets the GID of a tile at (x, y) on the given layer (1-based).
  TileMap:setTileTint( layer, x, y, r, g, b, a )  -- Sets a per-tile RGBA tint override (1-based layer, x, y).
  TileMap:setViewport( x, y, w, h )  -- Sets the viewport rectangle for rendering culling.
  TileMap:sweepRect( layer, x, y, w, h, dx, dy )  -- Performs a swept AABB collision test against solid tiles on layer (1-based).
  TileMap:tileToWorld( tx, ty )  -- Converts tile coordinates to world pixel coordinates (1-based input).
  TileMap:toNavGrid( layer, gids_tbl )  -- Converts the given layer into a 2D navigation grid.
  TileMap:update( dt )  -- Advances tile animation timers by dt seconds.
  TileMap:worldToTile( wx, wy )  -- Converts world pixel coordinates to tile coordinates.
```

```lua
  TileSet:getAutoTileId8( type_name, bitmask )  -> AutoTileId8  -- Looks up the 1-based local tile ID for an 8-bit directional autotile bitmask, or nil.
```

## lurek.scene {#scene}

> Depth-sorted scene management for 2D layers.

```lua
  lurek.scene.clear( )  -- Clears all scenes from the stack, calling leave on each.
  lurek.scene.define( [def] )  -- Creates a reusable scene class â€” returns a zero-argument constructor function.
  lurek.scene.depth( )  -- Returns the number of scenes on the stack.
  lurek.scene.deserializeScene( snapshot )  -- Restores scene data_refs from a snapshot produced by serializeScene().
  lurek.scene.draw( )  -- Draws all scenes in the stack from bottom to top (legacy name; prefer `render`).
  lurek.scene.fade( [duration] )  -- Returns a fade cross-dissolve transition config table.
  lurek.scene.getActiveScenes( )  -> ActiveScenes  -- Returns a table array of all active scene tables.
  lurek.scene.getCurrent( )  -> Current  -- Returns the current top scene table, or nil if the stack is empty.
  lurek.scene.getData( key )  -> Data  -- Returns a value from the inter-scene data store, or nil if not found.
  lurek.scene.getRegistered( name )  -> Registered  -- Returns a registered scene table by name, or nil if not found.
  lurek.scene.getRegisteredNames( )  -> RegisteredNames  -- Returns a list of all registered scene names.
  lurek.scene.getStackSize( )  -> StackSize  -- Returns the number of scenes on the stack.
  lurek.scene.getTransitionProgress( )  -> TransitionProgress  -- Returns the transition progress from 0.0 to 1.0.
  lurek.scene.getTransitionProgressEased( )  -> TransitionProgressEased  -- Returns the easing-adjusted transition progress from 0.0 to 1.0.
  lurek.scene.getTransitionTypes( )  -> TransitionTypes  -- Returns a table listing all supported transition type strings.
  lurek.scene.hasData( key )  -- Returns true if the given key exists in the data store.
  lurek.scene.hasRegistered( name )  -- Returns true if a scene is registered under the given name.
  lurek.scene.iris( [duration] )  -- Returns an iris in/out (circular reveal) transition config table.
  lurek.scene.isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the scene stack is empty.
  lurek.scene.isOverlay( )  -- Returns true if the current top scene was pushed as an overlay.
  lurek.scene.isPreloaded( name )  -- Returns true if the named scene has been preloaded.
  lurek.scene.isTransitioning( )  -- Returns true if a scene transition is currently active.
  lurek.scene.new( [def] )  -- Creates a scene instance directly from a methods table.
  lurek.scene.newDepthSorter( )  -> DepthSorter  -- Creates a new DepthSorter for z-ordered draw batching.
  lurek.scene.newScene( [def] )  -> Scene  -- Alias for `lurek.scene.new`. Creates a scene instance from a methods table.
  lurek.scene.pop( [transition], [duration], [easing] )  -- Pops the top scene from the stack with an optional transition and easing.
  lurek.scene.popTo( name )  -- Pops scenes until the named scene is on top, calling leave on each removed.
  lurek.scene.preload( name, loader )  -- Registers a loader function for a named scene. The loader is called
  lurek.scene.process( dt )  -- Calls `scene:ready(self)` once per scene on the first tick after enter,
  lurek.scene.processLate( dt )  -- Calls `scene:process_late(dt)` on all active scenes (after process, before render).
  lurek.scene.processPhysics( dt )  -- Calls `scene:process_physics(dt)` on all active scenes (fixed timestep).
  lurek.scene.push( )  -- Pushes a scene table onto the stack with an optional transition and easing.
  lurek.scene.pushOverlay( )  -- Pushes a scene as a non-pausing overlay over the current top scene.
  lurek.scene.pushPreloaded( )  -- Pushes a registered scene by name, running its loader if not yet preloaded.
  lurek.scene.registerScene( name, scene )  -- Registers a scene table by name for later retrieval.
  lurek.scene.removeData( key )  -- Removes a value from the inter-scene data store by key.
  lurek.scene.render( )  -- Draws all scenes in the stack from bottom to top.
  lurek.scene.renderUi( )  -- Draws UI overlay for all scenes in the stack from bottom to top.
  lurek.scene.serializeScene( )  -- Returns a snapshot of the scene stack as a Lua table: { stack=[name...], data={key=val} }.
  lurek.scene.setData( key, value )  -- Stores a value in the inter-scene data store under the given key.
  lurek.scene.slide( [direction], [duration] )  -- Returns a directional slide transition config table.
  lurek.scene.switchTo( )  -- Replaces the top scene with a new one, calling leave and enter callbacks.
  lurek.scene.unregisterScene( name )  -- Removes a scene from the registry by name.
  lurek.scene.update( dt )  -- Updates the top scene and any active transition (legacy name; prefer `process`).
  lurek.scene.wipe( [duration] )  -- Returns a wipe/curtain transition config table.
```

**`DepthSorter`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`DepthSorter`] with registry-stored callbacks.

```lua
  DepthSorter:add( callback, depth )  -- Registers a draw callback at the given depth layer.
  DepthSorter:addObject( obj )  -- Registers a table object with a draw method at the given depth.
  DepthSorter:clear( )  -- Removes all registered callbacks without calling them.
  DepthSorter:flush( )  -- Calls all draw callbacks in sorted depth order, then clears.
  DepthSorter:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the number of registered draw entries.
  DepthSorter:isStable( )  -- Returns true if stable sort mode is enabled.
  DepthSorter:setStable( stable )  -- Sets whether equal-depth entries preserve insertion order.
  DepthSorter:sort( )  -- Sorts all registered callbacks by depth ascending.
```

```lua
  lurek.ecs.newUniverse( )  -> Universe  -- Creates a new empty ECS universe.
```

**`Universe`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Universe`] ECS world.

```lua
  Universe:addRelation( from, name, to )  -- Adds a directed named relationship from entity `from` to entity `to`.
  Universe:addSystem( system, [opts] )  -- Adds a system table to the universe with an optional priority (lower = earlier).
  Universe:addTag( id, tag )  -- Attaches a string tag to an entity.
  Universe:bitmapTag( id, name )  -- Adds a bitmap tag to an entity.
  Universe:bitmapUntag( id, name )  -- Removes a bitmap tag from an entity.
  Universe:clear( )  -- Removes all entities, components, tags, layers, and systems. Blueprints are preserved.
  Universe:clearRelations( from, name )  -- Removes all directed named relationships of type `name` from entity `from`.
  Universe:defineBlueprint( name, components )  -- Defines a blueprint from a component table.
  Universe:defineTag( name )  -- Defines a bitmap tag name, returning its bit index.
  Universe:deserialize( snapshot )  -- Restores entity state from a snapshot produced by serialize().
  Universe:each( name, callback )  -- Calls callback(id, value) for every entity with the named component.
  Universe:emit( ... )  -- Emits a named event to all systems that implement the handler, in priority order.
  Universe:extendBlueprint( name, parent, overrides )  -- Defines a blueprint by extending a parent with overrides.
  Universe:flushObservers( )  -- Dispatches all pending component-add and component-remove events to registered callbacks.
  Universe:get( id, name )  -- Returns the component value for an entity, or nil if missing.
  Universe:getBitmapTagBit( name )  -> BitmapTagBit  -- Returns the bit index for a bitmap tag name, or nil if undefined.
  Universe:getBlueprintComponents( name )  -> BlueprintComponents  -- Returns a deep copy of a blueprint's component table, or nil.
  Universe:getChildren( parent_id )  -> Children  -- Returns all direct child entity IDs.
  Universe:getComponents( id )  -> Components  -- Returns all component names for an entity.
  Universe:getEntities( )  -> Entities  -- Returns all alive entity IDs.
  Universe:getEntitiesByLayer( layer )  -> EntitiesByLayer  -- Returns all alive entities on a specific layer.
  Universe:getEntitiesByTag( tag )  -> EntitiesByTag  -- Returns all alive entities with the given string tag.
  Universe:getEntitiesSorted( )  -> EntitiesSorted  -- Returns all alive entities sorted by layer then ID.
  Universe:getEntityCount( )  -> EntityCount  -- Returns the number of alive entities.
  Universe:getLayer( id )  -> Layer  -- Returns the layer for an entity, defaulting to zero.
  Universe:getParent( child_id )  -> Parent  -- Returns the parent entity ID, or nil if unparented.
  Universe:getRelated( from, name )  -> Related  -- Returns all entity IDs reachable from `from` via the named relationship.
  Universe:getSystemCount( )  -> SystemCount  -- Returns the number of registered systems.
  Universe:getTags( id )  -> Tags  -- Returns all string tags for an entity.
  Universe:has( id, name )  -- Returns true if the entity has the named component.
  Universe:hasBitmapTag( id, name )  -- Returns true if the entity has the given bitmap tag.
  Universe:hasBlueprint( name )  -- Returns true if a blueprint with the given name exists.
  Universe:hasRelation( from, name, to )  -- Returns true if a directed named relationship from `from` to `to` exists.
  Universe:hasTag( id, tag )  -- Returns true if the entity carries the given tag.
  Universe:isAlive( id )  -- Returns true if the entity ID is currently alive.
  Universe:kill( id )  -- Destroys the entity with the given ID, freeing its slot for reuse.
  Universe:killRecursive( id )  -- Kills an entity and all its descendants recursively.
  Universe:listBlueprints( )  -- Returns all defined blueprint names.
  Universe:onComponentAdded( name, cb )  -- Registers a callback to fire when a component is added to any entity.
  Universe:onComponentRemoved( name, cb )  -- Registers a callback to fire when a component is removed from any entity.
  Universe:query( ... )  -- Returns entity IDs that have all listed component names.
  Universe:queryBitmapAll( names )  -- Returns all alive entities with all of the listed bitmap tags.
  Universe:queryBitmapAny( names )  -- Returns all alive entities with any of the listed bitmap tags.
  Universe:queryBitmapTag( name )  -- Returns all alive entities with the given bitmap tag.
  Universe:queryNot( with_tbl, without_tbl )  -- Returns entity IDs that have all `with` components and none of the `without` components.
  Universe:release( )  -- Releases all universe state, equivalent to clear.
  Universe:remove( id, name )  -- Removes a component from an entity.
  Universe:removeBlueprint( name )  -- Removes a blueprint definition.
  Universe:removeRelation( from, name, to )  -- Removes the directed named relationship from entity `from` to entity `to`.
  Universe:removeSystem( system )  -- Removes a system table from the universe.
  Universe:removeTag( id, tag )  -- Removes a string tag from an entity.
  Universe:render( )  -- Calls render(system, world) on each registered system in priority order.
  Universe:serialize( )  -- Serializes all alive entities to a Lua table snapshot.
  Universe:set( id, name, value )  -- Sets a component value on an entity.
  Universe:setLayer( id, layer )  -- Sets the layer for an entity.
  Universe:setParent( child_id, [parent_id] )  -- Sets or clears the parent of an entity.
  Universe:spawn( )  -- Creates a new entity and returns its packed ID.

  Universe:spawnBulk( name, count, [overrides] )  -- Spawns `count` entities from a blueprint, returns an array of entity IDs.
  Universe:update( dt )  -- Calls update(system, world, dt) on each registered system in priority order.
```

## lurek.pathfind {#pathfind}

> Grid-based A* and flow-field pathfinding.

```lua
  lurek.pathfind.getThreadCount( )  -> ThreadCount  -- Returns the background pathfinding thread count (currently always 0).
  lurek.pathfind.newFlowField( grid_ud )  -> FlowField  -- Creates a new FlowField backed by a NavGrid.
  lurek.pathfind.newHexGrid( width, height, [layout_str] )  -> HexGrid  -- Creates a hex grid for pathfinding, LOS, FOV, and range queries.
  lurek.pathfind.newJpsGrid( width, height )  -> JpsGrid  -- Creates a uniform-cost grid optimised for Jump Point Search (orthogonal + diagonal).
  lurek.pathfind.newNavGrid( width, height )  -> NavGrid  -- Creates a new NavGrid with all cells walkable.
  lurek.pathfind.newNavGridFromTileMap( tm_ud, layer_index, blocked_table )  -> NavGridFromTileMap  -- Builds a NavGrid from a TileMap layer, treating specified GIDs as blocked (unwalkable).
  lurek.pathfind.newPathFlowField( grid_ud )  -> BFS  -- Creates a new BFS flow field from a PathGrid.
  lurek.pathfind.newPathGrid( w, h, cell_size )  -> PathGrid  -- Creates a new PathGrid with per-cell cost and walkability.
  lurek.pathfind.newPathfinder( grid_ud )  -> UnitPathfinder  -- Creates a new UnitPathfinder backed by a NavGrid.
  lurek.pathfind.rangeMap( opts )  -- Computes a Dijkstra range-of-movement map from an origin within a movement budget.
  lurek.pathfind.setThreadCount( count )  -- Sets the background pathfinding thread count (currently a no-op).
```

**`NavGrid`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`NavGrid`] with optional HPA★ abstract graph.

```lua
  NavGrid:clearDirty( )  -- Clears all pending dirty rectangles.
  NavGrid:fill( cost )  -- Sets every cell to the given cost.
  NavGrid:fillRect( x, y, w, h, cost )  -- Sets all cells in a rectangle to the given cost (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:getChunkSize( )  -> ChunkSize  -- Returns the current HPA★ chunk size.
  NavGrid:getCost( x, y )  -> Cost  -- Returns the traversal cost of a cell (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:getDiagonalMode( )  -> DiagonalMode  -- Returns the current diagonal movement mode as a string.
  NavGrid:getDimensions( )  -> Dimensions  -- Returns the grid dimensions as width, height.
  NavGrid:getHeight( )  -> Height  -- Returns the grid height in cells.
  NavGrid:getWidth( )  -> Width  -- Returns the grid width in cells.
  NavGrid:isBlocked( x, y )  -- Returns true if the cell is blocked (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:isWalkable( x, y, [unit_size] )  -- Returns true if a unit footprint is fully walkable (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:loadFromString( data )  -- Overwrites the grid from a raw byte string (row-major, one byte per cell).
  NavGrid:rebuildAbstract( )  -- Rebuilds the HPA★ abstract graph from the current grid state.
  NavGrid:saveToString( )  -- Exports the cost grid as a byte string (row-major, one byte per cell).
  NavGrid:setBlocked( x, y, blocked )  -- Marks a cell as blocked or unblocked (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:setChunkSize( size )  -- Sets the HPA★ chunk size.
  NavGrid:setCost( x, y, cost )  -- Sets the traversal cost of a cell (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:setDiagonalMode( mode )  -- Sets the diagonal movement mode.
  NavGrid:setDirty( x, y, w, h )  -- Records a dirty rectangle for incremental HPA★ updates (1-based coordinates).
  NavGrid:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  NavGrid:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```


**`UnitPathfinder`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`UnitPathfinder`].

```lua
  UnitPathfinder:clearCache( )  -- Removes all cached path results.
  UnitPathfinder:findNearestWalkable( x, y, max_radius, [unit_size] )  -- Finds the nearest walkable cell within a radius (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:findPartialPath( )  -- Finds a partial path with a node expansion limit (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:findPath( x1, y1, x2, y2, [unit_size] )  -- Finds an A★ path between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:findPathBidirectional( )  -- Finds a path using bidirectional A★, expanding from start and goal simultaneously
  UnitPathfinder:findPathSmooth( x1, y1, x2, y2, [unit_size] )  -- Finds a Theta★ smoothed path between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:getCacheSize( )  -> CacheSize  -- Returns the number of entries in the path cache.
  UnitPathfinder:getPathCost( path )  -> PathCost  -- Returns the sum of grid traversal costs along a path.
  UnitPathfinder:getPathLength( path )  -> PathLength  -- Returns the euclidean length of a path table.
  UnitPathfinder:heuristicDistance( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Returns the octile heuristic distance between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:isCacheEnabled( )  -- Returns true if path result caching is enabled.
  UnitPathfinder:isReachable( x1, y1, x2, y2, [unit_size] )  -- Returns true if a path exists between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:lineOfSight( x1, y1, x2, y2, [unit_size] )  -- Returns true if there is a clear line of sight between two cells (1-based coordinates).
  UnitPathfinder:setCacheEnabled( enabled )  -- Enables or disables path result caching.
  UnitPathfinder:setCacheMaxSize( n )  -- Sets the maximum number of cached path entries.
  UnitPathfinder:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  UnitPathfinder:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.ai {#ai}

> AI subsystems: FSM, behavior tree, steering, Q-learning, squad, utility AI, GOAP.

```lua
  lurek.ai.newAIDirector( )  -> AI  -- Creates a new AI pacing director with default config.
  lurek.ai.newAILod( )  -> AI  -- Creates a new AI LOD controller with default 3-tier config.
  lurek.ai.newAction( callback )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT action leaf with a Lua callback.
  lurek.ai.newBandit( arm_count, strategy, epsilon, seed )  -> Bandit  -- Creates a new multi-armed bandit.
  lurek.ai.newBehaviorTree( )  -> BehaviorTree  -- Creates a new behavior tree.
  lurek.ai.newBlackboard( )  -> Blackboard  -- Creates a new standalone blackboard.
  lurek.ai.newCommandQueue( )  -> RTS  -- Creates an RTS-style command queue.
  lurek.ai.newCondition( callback )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT condition leaf with a Lua predicate.
  lurek.ai.newContextSteering( slots )  -> ContextSteering  -- Creates a new context steering controller.
  lurek.ai.newEmotionModel( )  -> EmotionModel  -- Creates a new affective emotion model.
  lurek.ai.newGOAPPlanner( )  -> GOAP  -- Creates a new GOAP planning solver.
  lurek.ai.newGeneticAlgorithm( pop_size, gene_count, seed )  -> GeneticAlgorithm  -- Creates a new genetic algorithm.
  lurek.ai.newGuard( predicate, child_ud )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT Guard decorator. The predicate is evaluated before each tick;
  lurek.ai.newHTNDomain( )  -> Hierarchical  -- Creates a new Hierarchical Task Network domain.
  lurek.ai.newInfluenceMap( w, h, cs )  -> InfluenceMap  -- Creates a multi-layer influence map grid.
  lurek.ai.newInverter( )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT inverter decorator.
  lurek.ai.newMCTSEngine( iters, uct_c, depth, seed )  -> Monte  -- Creates a new Monte Carlo Tree Search engine.
  lurek.ai.newNeedSystem( )  -> NeedSystem  -- Creates a new motivational need system.
  lurek.ai.newNeuralNet( )  -> NeuralNet  -- Creates a new feedforward neural network (inference only).
  lurek.ai.newNeuroevolution( layer_spec, pop_size, seed )  -> Neuroevolution  -- Creates a neuroevolution trainer (GA for neural network weights).
  lurek.ai.newORCASolver( time_horizon )  -> ORCA  -- Creates a new ORCA crowd avoidance solver.
  lurek.ai.newParallel( [sp], [fp] )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT parallel node with optional policies.
  lurek.ai.newQLearner( sc, ac )  -> QLearner  -- Creates a tabular Q-learner.
  lurek.ai.newRepeater( [count] )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT repeater decorator.
  lurek.ai.newSelector( )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT selector node.
  lurek.ai.newSequence( )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT sequence node.
  lurek.ai.newSquad( name )  -> Squad  -- Creates a named squad for formation positioning.
  lurek.ai.newStateMachine( )  -> StateMachine  -- Creates a new finite state machine.
  lurek.ai.newSteeringManager( )  -> SteeringManager  -- Creates a new steering behavior manager.
  lurek.ai.newStimulusWorld( )  -> StimulusWorld  -- Creates a new stimulus perception world.
  lurek.ai.newStrategyAI( update_interval )  -> StrategyAI  -- Creates a new throttled strategy AI.
  lurek.ai.newSucceeder( )  -> BT  -- Creates a BT succeeder decorator.
  lurek.ai.newTraitProfile( )  -> TraitProfile  -- Creates a new personality trait profile.
  lurek.ai.newUtilityAI( )  -> UtilityAI  -- Creates a new utility AI evaluator.
  lurek.ai.newWorld( )  -> AI  -- Creates a new AI world container.
```

**`SteeringManager`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`SteeringManager`].

```lua
  SteeringManager:addArrive( tx, ty, [slowing], [weight] )  -- Adds an Arrive behavior with deceleration.
  SteeringManager:addCustomBehavior( func, [weight] )  -- Registers a Lua callback as a custom steering behavior.
  SteeringManager:addEvade( [threat_name], [weight] )  -- Adds an Evade behavior fleeing from a named agent.
  SteeringManager:addFlee( tx, ty, [panic_dist], [weight] )  -- Adds a Flee behavior away from the target.
  SteeringManager:addFlock( )  -- Adds a Flock behavior for group movement.
  SteeringManager:addPursue( [target_name], [weight] )  -- Adds a Pursue behavior targeting a named agent.
  SteeringManager:addSeek( tx, ty, [weight] )  -- Adds a Seek behavior toward the target.
  SteeringManager:addWander( )  -- Adds a Wander behavior for random meandering.
  SteeringManager:applyCustomSteering( agent_ud, dt )  -- Invokes all registered custom steering callbacks and returns the combined force.
  SteeringManager:calculate( px, py, vx, vy, max_speed, max_force, dt )  -- Computes the combined steering force for the given agent state.
  SteeringManager:enableSpatialHash( enabled )  -- Enables or disables spatial-hash bucketing for neighbourhood queries.
  SteeringManager:getBehaviorCount( )  -> BehaviorCount  -- Returns the number of active behaviors.
  SteeringManager:getCombineMode( )  -> CombineMode  -- Returns the current combination mode.
  SteeringManager:getLastSteering( )  -> LastSteering  -- Returns the last computed steering force.
  SteeringManager:setCombineMode( mode )  -- Sets the force combination mode.
  SteeringManager:setSpatialHashCellSize( size )  -- Sets the cell size used by the spatial-hash neighbourhood search.
```

## lurek.data {#data}

> Data utilities: TOML/JSON parsing, encoding, hashing, compression.

```lua
  lurek.data.compress( format_str, raw_data, [level] )  -- Compresses data using the given algorithm (deflate, gzip, lz4).
  lurek.data.crc32( raw_data )  -> CRC  -- Returns the CRC-32 checksum of the input data as an integer.
  lurek.data.decode( format_str, encoded )  -- Decodes encoded text back to binary (base64, hex).
  lurek.data.decompress( format_str, compressed )  -- Decompresses data using the given algorithm (deflate, gzip, lz4).
  lurek.data.encode( format_str, raw_data )  -- Encodes binary data using the given format (base64, hex).
  lurek.data.encodeToml( tbl )  -- Encodes a Lua table into a TOML string.
  lurek.data.fromMsgPack( bytes )  -- Deserializes a MessagePack binary string back into a Lua value.
  lurek.data.getPackedSize( fmt, ... )  -> PackedSize  -- Returns the number of bytes the given format and values would occupy.
  lurek.data.hash( algo_str, raw_data )  -- Returns the cryptographic hash of the input (md5, sha1, sha256, sha512).
  lurek.data.newByteData( value )  -> ByteData  -- Instantiates a raw byte data container object.
  lurek.data.newDataView( raw, [offset], [size] )  -> DataView  -- Creates a read-only windowed view into a byte string.
  lurek.data.newRingBuffer( capacity )  -> RingBuffer  -- Creates a fixed-capacity ring buffer that can store any Lua value.
  lurek.data.newWriter( )  -> Writer  -- Creates a new write-cursor for building binary data.
  lurek.data.pack( fmt, ... )  -- Packs values into a binary byte string using the format string.
  lurek.data.parseToml( text )  -- Parses a TOML string into a Lua table.
  lurek.data.read( fmt, raw, [offset] )  -- Reads values using the Lurek2D Binary Pack Format.
  lurek.data.size( fmt )  -- Returns the byte size of a Lurek2D Binary Pack Format string.
  lurek.data.toMsgPack( value )  -- Serializes a Lua value (table, string, number, boolean, or nil) to MessagePack binary.
  lurek.data.unpack( fmt, raw, [offset] )  -- Unpacks values from a binary byte string, returning values followed by next offset.
  lurek.data.write( fmt, ... )  -- Writes values using the Lurek2D Binary Pack Format.
```

**`ByteData`** methods:

```lua
  ByteData:clone( )  -- Clone the ByteData.
  ByteData:getBit( byte_offset, bit_offset )  -> Bit  -- Returns the value of a single bit within the buffer.
  ByteData:getByte( offset )  -> Byte  -- Get a byte at the specified offset.
  ByteData:getSize( )  -> Size  -- Get the size.
  ByteData:getString( )  -> String  -- Get the string representation.
  ByteData:readBits( byte_offset, bit_offset, count )  -- Reads `count` consecutive bits starting at `byte_offset`/`bit_offset`
  ByteData:setBit( byte_offset, bit_offset, value )  -- Sets or clears a single bit within the buffer.
  ByteData:setByte( offset, value )  -- Set a byte at the specified offset.
```

**`DataView`** methods:

> Access structured binary data efficiently without copying.

```lua
  DataView:getDouble( offset )  -> Double  -- Reads a 64-bit float at the given offset.
  DataView:getFloat( offset )  -> Float  -- Reads a 32-bit float at the given offset.
  DataView:getInt16( offset )  -> Int16  -- Reads a signed 16-bit integer at the given offset.
  DataView:getInt32( offset )  -> Int32  -- Reads a signed 32-bit integer at the given offset.
  DataView:getInt8( offset )  -> Int8  -- Reads a signed 8-bit integer at the given offset.
  DataView:getSize( )  -> Size  -- Returns the size of this view in bytes.
  DataView:getUInt16( offset )  -> UInt16  -- Reads an unsigned 16-bit integer at the given offset.
  DataView:getUInt32( offset )  -> UInt32  -- Reads an unsigned 32-bit integer at the given offset.
  DataView:getUInt8( offset )  -> UInt8  -- Reads an unsigned 8-bit integer at the given offset.
```

**`DataWriter`** methods:

```lua
  DataWriter:len( )  -- Returns the total buffer length.
  DataWriter:seek( pos )  -- Moves the write cursor to the given position.
  DataWriter:tell( )  -- Returns the current write cursor position.
  DataWriter:toBytes( )  -- Returns the buffer contents as a Lua string.
  DataWriter:writeBytes( )  -- Writes raw bytes from a Lua string.
  DataWriter:writeF32LE( v )  -- Writes a 32-bit LE float.
  DataWriter:writeF64LE( v )  -- Writes a 64-bit LE float.
  DataWriter:writeI16LE( v )  -- Writes a signed 16-bit LE integer.
  DataWriter:writeI32LE( v )  -- Writes a signed 32-bit LE integer.
  DataWriter:writeI8( v )  -- Writes a signed 8-bit integer.
  DataWriter:writeString( s )  -- Writes a length-prefixed UTF-8 string (4-byte LE length + bytes).
  DataWriter:writeU16BE( v )  -- Writes an unsigned 16-bit BE integer.
  DataWriter:writeU16LE( v )  -- Writes an unsigned 16-bit LE integer.
  DataWriter:writeU32LE( v )  -- Writes an unsigned 32-bit LE integer.
  DataWriter:writeU8( v )  -- Writes an unsigned 8-bit integer.
```

**`RingBuffer`** methods:

> Lua-side fixed-capacity ring buffer that holds any Lua value.

```lua
  RingBuffer:capacity( )  -- Returns the maximum number of elements the buffer can hold.
  RingBuffer:clear( )  -- Removes all elements from the buffer, releasing their registry entries.
  RingBuffer:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the buffer contains no elements.
  RingBuffer:isFull( )  -- Returns true if the buffer has reached its capacity.
  RingBuffer:len( )  -- Returns the number of elements currently in the buffer.
  RingBuffer:peek( )  -- Returns the oldest element without removing it, or nil if empty.
  RingBuffer:peekNewest( )  -- Returns the newest element without removing it, or nil if empty.
  RingBuffer:pop( )  -- Removes and returns the oldest element, or nil if the buffer is empty.
  RingBuffer:push( value )  -- Pushes a value onto the ring buffer.
  RingBuffer:toTable( )  -- Returns all elements as an array table ordered oldest-first.
```
