**`DataFrame`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a shared [`DataFrame`].

```lua
  DataFrame:addColumn( name, [default] )  -- Adds a new column with an optional default value.
  DataFrame:addRow( [row_tbl] )  -- Adds a row from an optional table of name-value pairs, returns 1-based index.
  DataFrame:addRowBatch( rows )  -- Add multiple rows at once from a table of row tables.
  DataFrame:apply( col_val, func )  -- Applies a function to each value in a column, replacing cells with results.
  DataFrame:clone( )  -- Returns a deep copy of this DataFrame.
  DataFrame:columns( )  -- Returns a table of column names.
  DataFrame:corr( col_a, col_b )  -- Pearson correlation coefficient between two numeric columns.
  DataFrame:correlationMatrix( )  -- Compute a correlation matrix for all numeric columns.
  DataFrame:count( )  -- Returns the row count (alias for nrows).
  DataFrame:countBy( col )  -- Counts distinct values in a column, returns a DataFrame with value and count columns.
  DataFrame:describe( )  -- Returns descriptive statistics for all numeric columns.
  DataFrame:dropNil( col )  -- Removes rows where the given column is nil, returns a new DataFrame.
  DataFrame:entropy( col )  -- Shannon entropy (bits) of the value distribution in a column.
  DataFrame:fillNil( col, val )  -- Replaces nil values in a column with the given value.
  DataFrame:filter( col, op, val )  -- Filters rows where column matches a condition, returns a new DataFrame.
  DataFrame:getColumn( col )  -> Column  -- Returns all values in a column as a table.
  DataFrame:getColumnAsF64( col )  -> ColumnAsF64  -- Return a numeric column as a Lua array of numbers (nils → 0/nan).
  DataFrame:getRow( row )  -> Row  -- Returns a row as a table of name-value pairs.
  DataFrame:getValue( row, col )  -> Value  -- Returns a single cell value.
  DataFrame:groupAgg( group_col, agg_col, fn_name )  -- Aggregate agg_col grouped by group_col using the named function.
  DataFrame:groupBy( col )  -- Groups rows by column value, returns a table of DataFrames keyed by value.
  DataFrame:groupByObj( col )  -- Groups rows by column value, returns a GroupedFrame object supporting aggregate().
  DataFrame:head( [n] )  -- Returns the first n rows (default 5).
  DataFrame:join( )  -- Joins with another DataFrame on matching columns.
  DataFrame:max( col )  -- Returns the maximum numeric value in a column.
  DataFrame:mean( col )  -- Returns the mean of numeric values in a column.
  DataFrame:median( col )  -- Returns the median of numeric values in a column.
  DataFrame:merge( other )  -- Appends rows from another DataFrame in-place.
  DataFrame:min( col )  -- Returns the minimum numeric value in a column.
  DataFrame:modeVal( col )  -- Return the most frequent value in a column (nil if empty).
  DataFrame:ncols( )  -- Returns the number of columns.
  DataFrame:normalizeCol( col, out_min, out_max, name )  -- Add a min-max normalized column scaled to [out_min, out_max].
  DataFrame:nrows( )  -- Returns the number of rows.
  DataFrame:outliers( col, [threshold] )  -> DataFrame  -- Return a new DataFrame with only outlier rows (|z-score| > threshold).
  DataFrame:pivot( row_col, col_col, val_col )  -- Creates a wide pivot table by reshaping rows into columns.
  DataFrame:pivotTable( )  -- Reshapes a long-format DataFrame into wide format.
  DataFrame:query( sql_str )  -- Executes a SQL query against this DataFrame.
  DataFrame:rank( col, [order], [result_col] )  -> DataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with a dense-rank column appended.
  DataFrame:removeColumn( col )  -- Removes a column by name or index.
  DataFrame:removeRow( row )  -- Removes a row by 1-based index.
  DataFrame:rename( col, new_name )  -- Renames the column `old_name` to `new_name` in this DataFrame.
  DataFrame:rollingMean( col, window, [result_col] )  -> DataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with a rolling mean column appended.
  DataFrame:rollingSum( col, window, [result_col] )  -> DataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with a rolling sum column appended.
  DataFrame:sample( n, [seed] )  -- Returns a random sample of n rows.
  DataFrame:select( ... )  -- Selects a subset of columns, returns a new DataFrame.
  DataFrame:setColumnFromF64( col, values )  -- Set a numeric column from a Lua array of numbers.
  DataFrame:setValue( row, col, val )  -- Sets a single cell value.
  DataFrame:slice( start, end )  -- Returns rows from start to end (1-based, inclusive).
  DataFrame:sort( col, [ascending] )  -- Sorts by column, returns a new DataFrame.
  DataFrame:stddev( col )  -- Returns the population standard deviation of numeric values in a column.
  DataFrame:sum( col )  -- Returns the sum of numeric values in a column.
  DataFrame:tail( [n] )  -- Returns the last n rows (default 5).
  DataFrame:toBinary( )  -- Serializes this DataFrame to a binary LVDF string.
  DataFrame:toCSV( )  -- Serializes this DataFrame to a CSV string.
  DataFrame:toJSON( )  -- Serializes this DataFrame to a JSON string.
  DataFrame:toString( )  -- Returns a formatted string table representation.
  DataFrame:toTable( )  -- Converts this DataFrame to a Lua table of row tables.
  DataFrame:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  DataFrame:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  DataFrame:unique( col )  -- Returns unique values in a column as a table.
  DataFrame:variance( col )  -- Returns the population variance of numeric values in a column.
  DataFrame:withCumsum( col, name )  -- Add a cumulative-sum column.
  DataFrame:withEval( col_name, expr )  -> DataFrame  -- Returns a new DataFrame with an additional computed column named `col_name`.
  DataFrame:withPctChange( col, name )  -- Add a percent-change-from-previous-row column.
  DataFrame:withRank( col, [asc], name )  -- Add a rank column (1-based, ties averaged).
  DataFrame:withRollingMax( col, window, name )  -- Add a rolling maximum column.
  DataFrame:withRollingMean( col, window, name )  -- Add a rolling mean column. Rows with insufficient history get nil.
  DataFrame:withRollingMin( col, window, name )  -- Add a rolling minimum column.
  DataFrame:withRollingSum( col, window, name )  -- Add a rolling sum column.
  DataFrame:zscoreCol( col, name )  -- Add a z-score column for the given numeric column.
```

**`Database`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a shared [`Database`].

```lua
  Database:addTable( name, df_ud )  -- Adds or replaces a table by cloning the given DataFrame.
  Database:clear( )  -- Drops every table from this in-memory database, leaving it empty.
  Database:getTable( name )  -> Table  -- Returns a copy of a table by name, or nil if not found.
  Database:hasTable( name )  -- Returns true if a table with the given name exists.
  Database:listTables( )  -- Returns a table of all table names.
  Database:merge( other )  -- Merges all tables from another Database into this one.
  Database:query( sql_str )  -- Executes a SQL query against the database tables.
  Database:removeTable( name )  -- Drops the named table from this in-memory database if it exists.
  Database:tableCount( )  -- Returns the number of tables.
  Database:toJSON( )  -- Serializes all tables to a JSON object string.
  Database:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Database:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`GroupedFrame`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a grouped result from [`DataFrame::group_by`].

```lua
  GroupedFrame:aggregate( col_name, func )  -- Apply a Lua function to aggregate a column's values per group.
```

**`VecFrame`** methods:

> Thin Lua wrapper around a [`VecFrame`]: typed-column vectorized DataFrame.

```lua
  VecFrame:applyMask( mask_tbl )  -> VecFrame  -- Return a new VecFrame containing only the rows where mask[i] is true.
  VecFrame:colAbs( col )  -- Apply absolute value to every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colAdd( col, val )  -- Add a scalar to every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colCast( col, dtype )  -- Cast a column to a new dtype: "float64", "int64", or "text".
  VecFrame:colCeil( col )  -- Apply ceiling to every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colClamp( col, min_val, max_val )  -- Clamp every element of a Float64 column to [min, max].
  VecFrame:colDiv( col, val )  -- Divide every element of a Float64 column by a scalar.
  VecFrame:colFloor( col )  -- Apply floor to every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colMul( col, val )  -- Multiply every element of a Float64 column by a scalar.
  VecFrame:colNeg( col )  -- Negate every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colOp( out_col, left_col, op, right_col )  -- Compute out[i] = left[i] op right[i] for every row.
  VecFrame:colSqrt( col )  -- Apply square root to every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colSub( col, val )  -- Subtract a scalar from every element of a Float64 column.
  VecFrame:colType( col )  -- Return the dtype name of a column: "float64", "int64", "bool", or "text".
  VecFrame:columns( )  -- Return a table of column names.
  VecFrame:filterMask( col, cmp_op, val )  -- Build a boolean row mask: mask[i] = col[i] cmp_op val.
  VecFrame:ncols( )  -- Return the number of columns.
  VecFrame:nrows( )  -- Return the number of rows.
  VecFrame:parReduce( cols_tbl, op )  -- Reduce multiple columns in parallel, returning {col → value} table.
  VecFrame:parScalarOp( cols_tbl, op, val )  -- Apply a scalar op in parallel to multiple Float64 columns.
  VecFrame:reduce( col, op )  -- Reduce an entire numeric column to a single value.
  VecFrame:toDataFrame( )  -- Convert this VecFrame back to a DataFrame.
  VecFrame:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  VecFrame:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

## lurek.graph {#graph}

> Directed graph: nodes, edges, item flow, Dijkstra pathfinding.

```lua
  lurek.graph.newGraph( )  -> Graph  -- Creates a new empty directed graph for item flow simulation.
```

**`Edge`** methods:

> Lua handle for an edge inside a `Graph`.

```lua
  Edge:addAllowedType( t )  -- Adds an item type to the edge allow-list.
  Edge:clearAllowedTypes( )  -- Clears the edge allow-list so all item types are permitted.
  Edge:getCapacity( )  -> Capacity  -- Returns the edge capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  Edge:getCooldown( )  -> Cooldown  -- Returns the cooldown duration in seconds.
  Edge:getFrom( )  -> From  -- Returns the source node handle.
  Edge:getItemsInTransit( )  -> ItemsInTransit  -- Returns a table of GraphItem handles currently in transit on this edge.
  Edge:getSpeedModifier( )  -> SpeedModifier  -- Returns the speed modifier applied to items in transit.
  Edge:getThroughput( )  -> Throughput  -- Returns items per second this edge can transfer.
  Edge:getTo( )  -> To  -- Returns the destination node handle.
  Edge:getTravelTime( )  -> TravelTime  -- Returns the travel time in seconds for items on this edge.
  Edge:getType( )  -> Type  -- Returns the edge type string.
  Edge:getWeight( )  -> Weight  -- Returns the pathfinding weight of this edge.
  Edge:isActive( )  -- Returns true if the edge is active.
  Edge:isBidirectional( )  -- Returns true if items can travel the edge in either direction.
  Edge:isItemTypeAllowed( t )  -- Returns true if the given item type is allowed on this edge.
  Edge:isOnCooldown( )  -- Returns true if the edge is currently on cooldown.
  Edge:removeAllowedType( t )  -- Removes an item type from the edge allow-list.
  Edge:setActive( a )  -- Sets the active state of this edge.
  Edge:setBidirectional( b )  -- Sets whether items can travel the edge in either direction.
  Edge:setCapacity( c )  -- Sets the edge capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  Edge:setCooldown( c )  -- Sets the cooldown duration in seconds.
  Edge:setSpeedModifier( m )  -- Sets the speed modifier applied to items in transit.
  Edge:setThroughput( t )  -- Sets items per second this edge can transfer.
  Edge:setTravelTime( t )  -- Sets the travel time in seconds for items on this edge.
  Edge:setType( t )  -- Sets the edge type string.
  Edge:setWeight( w )  -- Sets the pathfinding weight of this edge.
  Edge:type( )  -- Returns the type name "GraphEdge".
  Edge:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true when the given name matches "GraphEdge" or a parent type.
```

**`Graph`** methods:

> Lua wrapper around a directed `Graph` with event callback registry.

```lua
  Graph:addEdge( from_ud, to_ud, [edge_type] )  -- Adds a directed edge between two nodes and returns its handle.
  Graph:addItem( item_ud, node_ud )  -- Places an item at a node.
  Graph:addNode( [node_type], [capacity] )  -- Adds a node and returns its handle.
  Graph:astar( from_node, to_node )  -- Finds the shortest path between two nodes using A*.
  Graph:colorGraph( )  -- Assigns each node the smallest non-negative integer colour not shared with any
  Graph:createItem( [item_type], [decay_time] )  -> Item  -- Creates a new unplaced item and returns its handle.
  Graph:findPath( from_ud, to_ud )  -- Finds the shortest path between two nodes using Dijkstra.
  Graph:findPathForItem( item_ud, from_ud, to_ud )  -- Finds the shortest path for a specific item, filtering by item type.
  Graph:getComponents( )  -> Components  -- Returns weakly connected components as a table of tables of Node handles.
  Graph:getDistance( from_ud, to_ud )  -> Distance  -- Returns the shortest path distance, or nil if unreachable.
  Graph:getEdgeBetween( from_ud, to_ud )  -> EdgeBetween  -- Returns the edge between two nodes, or nil if none exists.
  Graph:getEdgeCount( )  -> EdgeCount  -- Returns the number of edges in the graph.
  Graph:getEdges( )  -> Edges  -- Returns a table of all Edge handles.
  Graph:getItemCount( )  -> ItemCount  -- Returns the number of items in the graph.
  Graph:getItems( )  -> Items  -- Returns a table of all GraphItem handles.
  Graph:getNeighbors( node_ud )  -> Neighbors  -- Returns a table of direct neighbor Node handles.
  Graph:getNodeCount( )  -> NodeCount  -- Returns the number of nodes in the graph.
  Graph:getNodes( )  -> Nodes  -- Returns a table of all Node handles.
  Graph:getReachable( from_ud, [max_dist] )  -> Reachable  -- Returns a table of Node handles reachable from the given node.
  Graph:getStats( )  -> Stats  -- Returns a statistics snapshot table.
  Graph:hasCycle( )  -- Returns true if the graph contains a directed cycle.
  Graph:hasEdge( edge_ud )  -- Returns true if the edge exists in the graph.
  Graph:hasItem( item_ud )  -- Returns true if the item exists in the graph.
  Graph:hasNode( node_ud )  -- Returns true if the node exists in the graph.
  Graph:isBipartite( )  -- Returns `true` when the graph can be 2-coloured (bipartite check via BFS).
  Graph:mst( )  -- Returns edge IDs forming a minimum spanning tree (Kruskal, undirected view).
  Graph:on( event_name, func )  -- Registers a callback for a graph simulation event.
  Graph:processDemand( )  -- Processes all supply/demand declarations and fires event callbacks.
  Graph:removeEdge( edge_ud )  -- Removes an edge from the graph.
  Graph:removeItem( item_ud )  -- Removes an item from the graph entirely.
  Graph:removeNode( node_ud )  -- Removes a node from the graph.
  Graph:sendItem( item_ud, edge_ud )  -- Sends an item onto an edge to begin transit.
  Graph:step( )  -- Runs one discrete simulation step and fires event callbacks.
  Graph:tickParallel( dt )  -- Advances simulation by dt seconds using a parallelised decay phase.
  Graph:topologicalSort( )  -- Returns a topologically sorted table of Node handles, or nil if a cycle exists.
  Graph:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Graph:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  Graph:update( dt )  -- Advances simulation by dt seconds and fires event callbacks.
```

**`GraphItem`** methods:

> Lua handle for an item inside a `Graph`.

```lua
  GraphItem:getDecayTime( )  -> DecayTime  -- Returns the decay time in seconds (-1 = immortal).
  GraphItem:getPosition( )  -> Position  -- Returns the item position: node userdata if at a node, (edge, progress)
  GraphItem:getPriority( )  -> Priority  -- Returns the item priority.
  GraphItem:getRemainingLife( )  -> RemainingLife  -- Returns the remaining life in seconds.
  GraphItem:getType( )  -> Type  -- Returns the item type string.
  GraphItem:isAlive( )  -- Returns true if the item is alive.
  GraphItem:kill( )  -- Marks this graph item as dead so it is removed on the next cleanup pass.
  GraphItem:setDecayTime( t )  -- Sets the decay time in seconds (-1 = immortal).
  GraphItem:setPriority( p )  -- Sets the scheduling priority; higher values are processed before lower ones.
  GraphItem:setType( t )  -- Sets the item type string.
  GraphItem:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  GraphItem:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
```

**`Node`** methods:

> Lua handle for a node inside a `Graph`.

```lua
  Node:addDemand( item_type, quantity, [priority] )  -- Declares a demand for the given item type, quantity, and priority.
  Node:addSupply( item_type, quantity )  -- Declares a supply of the given item type and quantity at this node.
  Node:addTag( tag )  -- Attaches a string tag to this node for fast group queries.
  Node:clearAllConversions( )  -- Removes all conversion rules from this node.
  Node:clearConversion( in_type )  -- Removes the conversion rule for the given input type.
  Node:clearDemands( )  -- Removes all demand declarations from this node.
  Node:clearSupplies( )  -- Removes all supply declarations from this node.
  Node:clearTags( )  -- Removes all tags from this node.
  Node:dequeue( )  -- Pops the next item from the node queue, or nil if empty.
  Node:enqueue( item_ud )  -- Pushes an item into the node queue.
  Node:getCapacity( )  -> Capacity  -- Returns the node capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  Node:getEdges( [dir] )  -> Edges  -- Returns a table of Edge handles connected to this node.
  Node:getFlowMode( )  -> FlowMode  -- Returns the flow mode as a string.
  Node:getItemCount( )  -> ItemCount  -- Returns the number of items currently at this node.
  Node:getItems( )  -> Items  -- Returns a table of GraphItem handles at this node.
  Node:getOverflowPolicy( )  -> OverflowPolicy  -- Returns the overflow policy as a string.
  Node:getProcessTime( )  -> ProcessTime  -- Returns the processing time in seconds.
  Node:getPullFilter( )  -> PullFilter  -- Returns the pull filter string, or nil if unset.
  Node:getPullRate( )  -> PullRate  -- Returns items per second this node pulls.
  Node:getPushFilter( )  -> PushFilter  -- Returns the push filter string, or nil if unset.
  Node:getPushRate( )  -> PushRate  -- Returns items per second this node pushes.
  Node:getQueueCapacity( )  -> QueueCapacity  -- Returns the queue capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  Node:getQueueSize( )  -> QueueSize  -- Returns the number of items currently in the queue.
  Node:getTags( )  -> Tags  -- Returns a table of tag strings on this node.
  Node:getType( )  -> Type  -- Returns the node type string.
  Node:hasTag( tag )  -- Returns true if this node has the given tag.
  Node:isActive( )  -- Returns true if the node is active.
  Node:isFull( )  -- Returns true if the node has reached its capacity.
  Node:isQueueEnabled( )  -- Returns true if the node queue is enabled.
  Node:removeDemand( item_type )  -- Removes the demand declaration for the given item type.
  Node:removeSupply( item_type )  -- Removes the supply declaration for the given item type.
  Node:removeTag( tag )  -- Removes a tag from this node.
  Node:setActive( a )  -- Sets the active state of this node.
  Node:setCapacity( c )  -- Sets the node capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  Node:setConversion( )  -- Adds or replaces a conversion rule on this node.
  Node:setFlowMode( m )  -- Sets the flow mode from a string.
  Node:setOverflowPolicy( p )  -- Sets the overflow policy from a string.
  Node:setProcessTime( t )  -- Sets the processing time in seconds.
  Node:setPullFilter( [f] )  -- Sets the pull filter string, or nil to clear.
  Node:setPullRate( r )  -- Sets items per second this node pulls.
  Node:setPushFilter( [f] )  -- Sets the push filter string, or nil to clear.
  Node:setPushRate( r )  -- Sets items per second this node pushes.
  Node:setQueueCapacity( c )  -- Sets the queue capacity (-1 = unlimited).
  Node:setQueueEnabled( e )  -- Enables or disables the node queue.
  Node:setType( t )  -- Sets the node type string.
  Node:type( )  -- Returns the type name "GraphNode".
  Node:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true when the given name matches "GraphNode" or a parent type.
```

## lurek.minimap {#minimap}

> Minimap rendering from tile data.

```lua
  lurek.minimap.newMinimap( grid_w, grid_h, [display_w], [display_h] )  -> Minimap  -- Creates a new grid-based minimap.
```

**`Minimap`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Minimap`].

```lua
  Minimap:addMarker( )  -- Adds a persistent marker and returns its auto-assigned ID.
  Minimap:addObjectType( name, r, g, b, [a] )  -- Registers a new object type and returns its 1-based index.
  Minimap:addPing( )  -- Adds an animated ping at grid coordinates with a duration and optional color.
  Minimap:clearMarkerAnimation( id )  -- Removes the animation from a marker, reverting it to static.
  Minimap:clearObjects( )  -- Removes all tracked objects.
  Minimap:clearOverlay( )  -- Removes all custom geometry from the minimap overlay.
  Minimap:clearPath( [id] )  -- Removes a displayed path. If id is nil, all paths are removed.
  Minimap:clearViewportRect( )  -- Clears the viewport rectangle overlay.
  Minimap:drawLine( x1, y1, x2, y2, color_tbl )  -- Draws a custom line segment on the minimap overlay.
  Minimap:drawRect( x, y, w, h, color_tbl )  -- Draws a custom rectangle on the minimap overlay.
  Minimap:drawToImage( pixel_size )  -- Renders the minimap grid to a CPU ImageData.
  Minimap:getCenter( )  -> Center  -- Returns the center coordinates as x, y.
  Minimap:getCenterX( )  -> CenterX  -- Returns the center X coordinate.
  Minimap:getCenterY( )  -> CenterY  -- Returns the center Y coordinate.
  Minimap:getColorMode( )  -> ColorMode  -- Returns the current color mode as a string.
  Minimap:getDisplayHeight( )  -> DisplayHeight  -- Returns the display height in pixels.
  Minimap:getDisplaySize( )  -> DisplaySize  -- Returns the display width and height as two values.
  Minimap:getDisplayWidth( )  -> DisplayWidth  -- Returns the display width in pixels.
  Minimap:getFogColor( )  -> FogColor  -- Returns the fog overlay color as r, g, b, a.
  Minimap:getFogLevel( x, y )  -> FogLevel  -- Returns the fog level at a 1-based grid position (0=hidden, 1=explored, 2=visible).
  Minimap:getGridHeight( )  -> GridHeight  -- Returns the grid height in cells.
  Minimap:getGridSize( )  -> GridSize  -- Returns the grid width and height as two values.
  Minimap:getGridWidth( )  -> GridWidth  -- Returns the grid width in cells.
  Minimap:getHoverInfo( sx, sy, mx, my )  -> HoverInfo  -- Returns hover tooltip text for the element under screen coordinates, or nil.
  Minimap:getLayer( )  -> Layer  -- Returns the index of the currently active render layer.
  Minimap:getMarkerCount( )  -> MarkerCount  -- Returns the number of markers.
  Minimap:getMarkerDescription( id )  -> MarkerDescription  -- Returns the description of a marker, or nil.
  Minimap:getObjectCount( )  -> ObjectCount  -- Returns the number of tracked objects.
  Minimap:getObjectTypeCount( )  -> ObjectTypeCount  -- Returns the number of registered object types.
  Minimap:getOwnerColor( owner )  -> OwnerColor  -- Returns the display color for an owner/faction as r, g, b, a.
  Minimap:getPingCount( )  -> PingCount  -- Returns the number of active pings.
  Minimap:getTerrain( x, y )  -> Terrain  -- Returns the terrain type at a 1-based grid position.
  Minimap:getTerrainColor( terrain_type )  -> TerrainColor  -- Returns the display color for a terrain type as r, g, b, a.
  Minimap:getTileDescription( type_id )  -> TileDescription  -- Returns the hover tooltip string for a terrain type ID, or nil.
  Minimap:getViewportColor( )  -> ViewportColor  -- Returns the viewport rectangle color as r, g, b, a.
  Minimap:getViewportRect( )  -> ViewportRect  -- Returns the viewport rectangle as x, y, w, h or nil if not set.
  Minimap:getZoom( )  -> Zoom  -- Returns the current zoom level.
  Minimap:gridToScreen( gx, gy, mx, my )  -- Converts grid coordinates to screen coordinates.
  Minimap:hasMarker( id )  -- Returns whether a marker with the given ID exists.
  Minimap:isAntiAlias( )  -- Returns whether anti-aliasing is enabled.
  Minimap:isClickable( )  -- Returns whether this minimap responds to click hit-testing.
  Minimap:isFogEnabled( )  -- Returns whether fog of war is enabled.
  Minimap:isObjectTypeVisible( type_idx )  -- Returns whether an object type (1-based index) is visible.
  Minimap:isViewportVisible( )  -- Returns whether the viewport rectangle is visible.
  Minimap:removeMarker( id )  -- Removes the minimap marker with the given integer ID, if present.
  Minimap:removeObject( id )  -- Removes a tracked object by ID.
  Minimap:render( [x], [y] )  -- Renders the minimap to the screen at the given position.
  Minimap:screenToGrid( sx, sy, mx, my )  -- Converts screen coordinates to grid coordinates.
  Minimap:setAntiAlias( enabled )  -- Sets whether anti-aliasing is enabled.
  Minimap:setCenter( x, y )  -- Sets the center of the minimap view in grid coordinates.
  Minimap:setClickable( enabled )  -- Sets whether this minimap responds to click hit-testing.
  Minimap:setColorMode( mode )  -- Sets the color mode ("terrain" or "political").
  Minimap:setDisplaySize( w, h )  -- Sets the display size in pixels.
  Minimap:setFogColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the fog overlay color.
  Minimap:setFogData( data )  -- Sets the entire fog grid from a flat 1-based table (0=hidden, 1=explored, 2=visible).
  Minimap:setFogEnabled( enabled )  -- Enables or disables fog of war.
  Minimap:setFogLevel( x, y, level )  -- Sets the fog level at a 1-based grid position (0=hidden, 1=explored, 2=visible).
  Minimap:setLayer( layer )  -- Switches the minimap's active render layer (0-based index).
  Minimap:setLayerData( layer, data_tbl )  -- Stores tile data for a specific layer index.
  Minimap:setMarkerAnimation( id, anim_type, speed )  -- Attaches an animation to a marker. Does nothing if the ID does not exist.
  Minimap:setObject( id, x, y, type_idx, [owner] )  -- Sets or updates a tracked object on the minimap.
  Minimap:setObjectTypeVisible( type_idx, visible )  -- Sets whether an object type (1-based index) is visible.
  Minimap:setOwnerColor( owner, r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the display color for an owner/faction.
  Minimap:setTerrain( x, y, terrain_type )  -- Sets the terrain type at a 1-based grid position.
  Minimap:setTerrainColor( terrain_type, r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the display color for a terrain type.
  Minimap:setTerrainData( data )  -- Sets terrain types from a flat 1-based Lua table of integers (row-major).
  Minimap:setTileDescription( type_id, desc )  -- Sets a hover tooltip string for a terrain type ID.
  Minimap:setViewportColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the viewport rectangle color.
  Minimap:setViewportRect( x, y, w, h )  -- Sets the viewport rectangle overlay in grid coordinates.
  Minimap:setViewportVisible( visible )  -- Sets whether the viewport rectangle is visible.
  Minimap:setZoom( zoom )  -- Sets the zoom level (minimum 0.1).
  Minimap:showPath( points_tbl, color_tbl )  -- Displays a pathfinding route on the minimap and returns its path ID.
  Minimap:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Minimap:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true if this object is of the given type.
  Minimap:update( dt )  -- Advances time-based effects by dt seconds (expires pings).
```

## lurek.save {#save}

> Save/load game state: named slots, versioned tables, autosave.

```lua
  lurek.save.newSaveManager( )  -> SaveManager  -- Creates a new SaveManager for slot-based save/load operations.
```

**`SaveManager`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`SaveManager`] with per-module callback storage.

```lua
  SaveManager:addMigration( from_ver, func )  -- Registers a migration function for upgrading from a schema version
  SaveManager:collect( )  -- Collects data from all registered collectors into a table with metadata
  SaveManager:delete( slot )  -- Deletes a save file for the given slot.
  SaveManager:disableAutoSave( )  -- Disables automatic periodic saving; manual `write()` calls still work.
  SaveManager:enableAutoSave( interval, slot )  -- Enables auto-save with a given interval and target slot
  SaveManager:exists( slot )  -- Returns whether a save file exists for the given slot.
  SaveManager:getSchemaVersion( )  -> SchemaVersion  -- Returns the current schema version
  SaveManager:getSlotInfo( slot )  -> SlotInfo  -- Returns metadata for a single slot, or nil if not found.
  SaveManager:getSlots( )  -> Slots  -- Returns a list of all save slots with metadata.
  SaveManager:getSummary( )  -> Summary  -- Returns the current summary string
  SaveManager:isCompressed( )  -- Returns whether compression is currently enabled.
  SaveManager:isDirty( )  -- Returns whether data has been modified since the last save or load
  SaveManager:load( slot )  -- Loads data from a slot file, applies migrations, and restores.
  SaveManager:markDirty( )  -- Marks data as modified since the last save or load
  SaveManager:onAfterLoad( func )  -- Registers a callback that fires after every successful load operation.
  SaveManager:onBeforeSave( func )  -- Registers a callback that fires before every save operation.
  SaveManager:register( name, collect_fn, restore_fn )  -- Registers a named module with collector and restorer callbacks
  SaveManager:reset( )  -- Resets all state, removing callbacks and clearing the manager
  SaveManager:restore( data )  -- Restores data from a table, applying migrations and calling restorers
  SaveManager:save( slot )  -- Collects data and writes it to a slot file.
  SaveManager:setCompress( enabled )  -- Enables or disables LZ4 compression for saved data
  SaveManager:setSchemaVersion( version )  -- Sets the current schema version for new saves
  SaveManager:setSummary( summary )  -- Sets the summary string included in save metadata
  SaveManager:unregister( name )  -- Removes a named module and its callbacks
  SaveManager:update( dt )  -- Advances the auto-save timer, returning the slot name if a save should trigger
```

## lurek.log {#log}

```lua
  lurek.log.addSink( config )  -- Registers a new output sink. Returns its numeric id.
  lurek.log.clearSinks( )  -- Removes all registered sinks (the default stderr channel is unaffected).
  lurek.log.debug( message, [tag] )  -- Emits a debug-severity log message. Also dispatches to configured sinks.
  lurek.log.debug_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -- Emits a debug structured log message. Shorthand for `struct("debug", ...)`.
  lurek.log.error( message, [tag] )  -- Emits an error-severity log message. Also dispatches to configured sinks.
  lurek.log.error_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -- Emits an error structured log message. Shorthand for `struct("error", ...)`.
  lurek.log.flushFile( id )  -- Flushes the OS write buffer for a file sink.
  lurek.log.getLevel( )  -> Level  -- Returns the name of the currently active minimum log level.
  lurek.log.info( message, [tag] )  -- Emits an info-severity log message. Also dispatches to configured sinks.
  lurek.log.info_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -- Emits an info structured log message. Shorthand for `struct("info", ...)`.
  lurek.log.listSinks( )  -- Returns a table describing all registered sinks.
  lurek.log.print( level, message, [tag] )  -- Emits a log message at the specified level. Also dispatches to sinks.
  lurek.log.readMemory( id, [drain] )  -- Reads entries from a memory sink. If drain=true the buffer is cleared.
  lurek.log.removeSink( id )  -- Removes a sink by id. Returns true if one was removed.
  lurek.log.setLevel( level )  -- Sets the minimum severity level for the default log channel.
  lurek.log.struct( level_str, message, fields_tbl )  -- Emits a structured log message with key-value fields.
  lurek.log.warn( message, [tag] )  -- Emits a warn-severity log message. Also dispatches to configured sinks.
  lurek.log.warn_fields( message, fields_tbl )  -- Emits a warn structured log message. Shorthand for `struct("warn", ...)`.
```

## lurek.mods {#mods}

```lua
  lurek.mods.newMod( info )  -> Mod  -- Creates a new Mod from an info table with at least an `id` field.

```

**`ContentRegistry`** methods:

> A typed content registry for mod-contributed assets and objects.

```lua
  ContentRegistry:get( type_name, id )  -- Retrieve a content entry.
  ContentRegistry:getAll( type_name )  -> All  -- Get all entries for a type.
  ContentRegistry:getTypes( )  -> Types  -- Get all registered type names.
  ContentRegistry:register( type_name, id, obj )  -- Register a content entry.
  ContentRegistry:registerType( type_name )  -- Register a new content type.
```

**`Mod`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`ModInfo`] with per-mod hook and config storage.

```lua
  Mod:getApiVersion( )  -> ApiVersion  -- Returns the required engine API version string, or nil if not set
  Mod:getAuthor( )  -> Author  -- Returns the author name string from this mod's metadata manifest
  Mod:getCapabilities( )  -> Capabilities  -- Returns an array of declared capability flags
  Mod:getConfig( )  -> Config  -- Returns the stored config value, or nil
  Mod:getConfigSchema( )  -> ConfigSchema  -- Returns the config schema as an array of `{key, type, default}` tables.
  Mod:getDependencies( )  -> Dependencies  -- Returns the list of required mod IDs
  Mod:getDescription( )  -> Description  -- Returns the mod description
  Mod:getHook( name )  -> Hook  -- Returns the hook function for the given name, or nil
  Mod:getHookNames( )  -> HookNames  -- Returns an array of registered hook names
  Mod:getId( )  -> Id  -- Returns the unique mod identifier
  Mod:getName( )  -> Name  -- Returns the localized or human-readable display name of the mod.
  Mod:getPriority( )  -> Priority  -- Returns the load-order priority
  Mod:getVersion( )  -> Version  -- Returns the version string
  Mod:hasHook( name )  -- Returns whether a hook with the given name exists
  Mod:isEnabled( )  -- Returns whether the mod is enabled
  Mod:isLoaded( )  -- Returns whether the mod has been loaded
  Mod:releaseRefs( )  -- Releases all hook and config registry references
  Mod:setApiVersion( api_version )  -- Sets the required engine API version string
  Mod:setCapabilities( caps )  -- Replaces the capability list with the given array of strings
  Mod:setConfig( value )  -- Stores an arbitrary config value for this mod
  Mod:setConfigSchema( schema )  -- Replaces the config schema with the given array of `{key, type, default}` tables.
  Mod:setEnabled( enabled )  -- Enables or disables this mod; disabled mods are skipped during loading
  Mod:setHook( name, func )  -- Registers a named hook callback, replacing any existing one
```

**`ModManager`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`ModManager`].

```lua
  ModManager:clearLoadOrder( )  -- Clears the custom load order, reverting to priority-based sorting
  ModManager:clearReloadQueue( )  -- Clears the reload queue without reloading
  ModManager:getAllMods( )  -> AllMods  -- Returns an array of info tables for all registered mods
  ModManager:getLoadOrder( )  -> LoadOrder  -- Returns an array of info tables in effective load order
  ModManager:getModCount( )  -> ModCount  -- Returns the number of registered mods
  ModManager:getModPath( mod_id )  -> ModPath  -- Returns the filesystem path of a registered mod, or nil
  ModManager:getReloadQueue( )  -> ReloadQueue  -- Returns the array of mod IDs pending hot-reload
  ModManager:hasCircularDependencies( )  -- Returns whether any circular dependency cycles exist
  ModManager:hasMod( mod_id )  -- Returns whether a mod with the given ID is registered
  ModManager:markForReload( mod_id )  -- Marks a registered mod for hot-reload
  ModManager:registerMod( ud )  -- Registers a mod from its Mod userdata
  ModManager:scanFolder( path )  -- Scans a directory for mods with mod.toml and registers them
  ModManager:setLoadOrder( order_table )  -- Sets an explicit load order from an array of mod ID strings
  ModManager:unregisterMod( mod_id )  -- Removes a mod by ID and returns whether it was found
  ModManager:validateDependencies( )  -- Returns an array of mod IDs with missing dependencies
```

## lurek.i18n {#i18n}

> Localisation: string lookup, locale switching, plural forms.

```lua
  lurek.i18n.buildIndex( )  -- Builds an inverted word index for the active locale. Returns index as {word â†’ {keys}}.
  lurek.i18n.categories( )  -- Returns unique first-path-segment category prefixes for all active locale keys.

  lurek.i18n.getAvailableLanguages( )  -> AvailableLanguages  -- Returns all loaded locale codes (alias for getLanguages).
  lurek.i18n.getBase( )  -> Base  -- Returns the base/fallback language.
  lurek.i18n.getFallbacks( )  -> Fallbacks  -- Returns the current fallback locale array.
  lurek.i18n.getKeys( )  -> Keys  -- Returns all known keys for the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.getLanguage( )  -> Language  -- Returns the currently active locale code, or nil if unset.
  lurek.i18n.getLanguages( )  -> Languages  -- Returns all loaded locale codes.
  lurek.i18n.getLoadedLocales( )  -> LoadedLocales  -- Returns an array of all currently loaded locale codes.
  lurek.i18n.hasKey( key )  -- Returns whether a key exists in the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.hasLanguage( locale )  -- Returns whether a locale has been loaded.
  lurek.i18n.interpolate( template, vars )  -- Interpolates {name} placeholders in a template string.
  lurek.i18n.keyCount( )  -- Returns the number of keys loaded in the active locale.
  lurek.i18n.keysInCategory( category )  -- Returns all keys in the active locale whose first path segment matches category.
  lurek.i18n.loadTable( locale, tbl )  -- Loads a language table under the given locale code.
  lurek.i18n.mergeLocale( locale, entries )  -- Merges a flat keyâ†’value table into an existing locale without replacing the whole table.
  lurek.i18n.offChange( )  -- Unregisters all onChange callbacks (cb arg is ignored; all callbacks are cleared).
  lurek.i18n.onChange( cb )  -- Registers a callback invoked when setLanguage() is called (alias: onChange).
  lurek.i18n.onLanguageChange( cb )  -- Registers a callback invoked when setLanguage() is called.
  lurek.i18n.pluralFor( n )  -> CLDR  -- Returns the CLDR plural category for a number ("one" or "other", etc.).
  lurek.i18n.search( query, [limit] )  -- Searches active locale values for a substring query (case-insensitive). Returns {key, v...
  lurek.i18n.searchIndexed( index, query, [limit] )  -- Searches the provided pre-built index for entries matching all words in query.
  lurek.i18n.setBase( locale )  -- Sets the base/fallback language (adds it as first fallback).
  lurek.i18n.setFallbacks( locales )  -- Sets the ordered list of fallback locale codes tried when a key is missing.
  lurek.i18n.setKey( locale, key, value )  -- Inserts or overwrites a single key in the given locale.
  lurek.i18n.setLanguage( locale )  -- Sets the active translation language.
  lurek.i18n.t( key, [vars], [count] )  -- Translates a key against the active locale with optional variable
  lurek.i18n.tGender( key, gender, [vars] )  -- Looks up a translation key augmented with a gender suffix.
  lurek.i18n.unloadTable( locale )  -- Unloads a locale from the catalog.
```

## lurek.input {#input}

```lua

  lurek.input.getY( )  -- Returns the current mouse Y position in window coordinates.
  lurek.input.hasKeyRepeat( )  -- Returns whether key-repeat is currently enabled.
  lurek.input.hasTextInput( )  -- Returns whether text input mode is currently active.
  lurek.input.isActionDown( action )  -- Returns true if any key bound to the action is currently held down.
  lurek.input.isConnected( id )  -- Returns whether the gamepad with the given ID is connected.
  lurek.input.isCursorSupported( )  -- Returns whether cursor customisation is supported on this platform.
  lurek.input.isDown( args )  -- Returns true if any of the given keys is currently held down.
  lurek.input.isDown( button )  -- Returns whether the given mouse button is currently held down.
  lurek.input.isDown( id, button )  -- Returns whether the given button on the gamepad is currently held.
  lurek.input.isGamepad( id )  -- Returns whether the joystick at the given slot is a recognized gamepad.
  lurek.input.isGrabbed( )  -- Returns whether the mouse cursor is locked to the window.
  lurek.input.isModifierActive( modifier )  -- Returns whether the named modifier key is currently held.
  lurek.input.isPlayingBack( )  -- Returns true if input playback is currently active.
  lurek.input.isRecording( )  -- Returns true if input recording is currently active.
  lurek.input.isScancodeDown( scancode )  -- Returns whether the key with the given scancode is held.
  lurek.input.isVibrationSupported( id )  -- Returns whether the gamepad supports haptic vibration.
  lurek.input.isVisible( )  -- Returns whether the mouse cursor is currently visible.

  lurek.input.loadRecording( json )  -> JSON  -- Loads a JSON-encoded recording string for playback.
  lurek.input.newCombo( steps_val, [opts] )  -> Combo  -- Creates a new combo detector from an ordered list of steps.
  lurek.input.newCursor( )  -> Cursor  -- Creates a custom mouse cursor from RGBA pixel data.
  lurek.input.saveGamepadMappings( path )  -- Saves all stored gamepad mappings to a plain-text file.

  lurek.input.setGamepadMapping( guid, mapping )  -- Stores or replaces the SDL2 GameControllerDB mapping string for the given GUID.
  lurek.input.setGrabbed( grabbed )  -- Locks or unlocks the mouse cursor to the window.
  lurek.input.setKeyRepeat( enabled )  -- Enables or disables key-repeat events.
  lurek.input.setPosition( x, y )  -- Moves the mouse cursor to the given window-space position.
  lurek.input.setRelativeMode( relative )  -- Enables or disables raw relative mouse motion mode.
  lurek.input.setTextInput( enabled )  -- Enables or disables Unicode text input mode.
  lurek.input.setVibration( ... )  -- Triggers haptic rumble (currently a no-op stub).
  lurek.input.setVisible( visible )  -- Shows or hides the operating-system mouse cursor.
  lurek.input.startPlayback( )  -- Starts playback from the beginning of the loaded recording.
  lurek.input.startRecording( )  -- Starts capturing input events frame-by-frame.  Clears any previous recording.
  lurek.input.stopPlayback( )  -- Stops playback immediately.
  lurek.input.stopRecording( )  -- Stops recording and returns an `InputRecording` userdata, or nil if not recording.
  lurek.input.unbind( action )  -- Removes all key bindings for the given action name.
  lurek.input.vibrate( id, low_freq, high_freq, duration_ms )  -- Requests haptic vibration on a gamepad.
  lurek.input.wasActionPressed( action )  -- Returns true if any key bound to the action was pressed this frame.
  lurek.input.wasActionPressedWithin( action, frames )  -- Was action pressed within.
  lurek.input.wasActionReleased( action )  -- Returns true if any key bound to the action was released this frame.
```

**`Combo`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper for a [`ComboDetector`] with an integrated millisecond clock.

```lua
  Combo:feed( key )  -- Feed a key-press event into the combo detector.
  Combo:getStep( index )  -> Step  -- Returns the step at the given 1-based index as `{key=..., gap_ms=...}`.
  Combo:isInProgress( )  -- Returns true if the detector is currently mid-sequence.
  Combo:progress( )  -- Returns the number of steps matched so far (0 when idle).
  Combo:reset( )  -- Reset the detector to its initial idle state, cancelling any in-progress sequence.
  Combo:tick( dt )  -- Advance the internal clock by `dt` seconds and check for timeouts.
  Combo:totalSteps( )  -- Returns the total number of steps in the combo sequence.
```

**`Cursor`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a mouse cursor handle.

```lua
  Cursor:getType( )  -> Type  -- Returns the cursor type as "system" or "custom".
  Cursor:release( )  -- Releases the cursor resource (no-op on desktop).
```

**`InputRecording`** methods:

> Lua userdata wrapper for a completed [`crate::input::recorder::InputRecording`].

```lua
  InputRecording:frameCount( )  -- Returns the number of sparse event frames stored in this recording.
  InputRecording:toJson( )  -- Serializes this recording to a JSON string for saving to disk.
  InputRecording:totalFrames( )  -- Returns the total frame count when recording was stopped.
```

```lua
  AnimStateMachine:addTransition( from_state, to_state, condition )  -- Adds a conditional transition between two states.
```

**`Animation`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around an [`Animation`] controller.

```lua
  Animation:addClip( name, indices_tbl, fps, looping )  -- Adds a named clip from explicit frame indices.
  Animation:addClipFromGrid( )  -- Adds a named clip sliced from a sprite-sheet grid.
  Animation:addFrame( x, y, w, h )  -- Adds a single frame to the frame pool by source rectangle.
  Animation:addFramesFromGrid( tw, th, fw, fh, start, count )  -- Slices a sprite-sheet grid into frames and appends them.
  Animation:crossfade( clip_name, duration )  -- Begins a smooth crossfade from the current clip to a new named clip.
  Animation:drawToImage( w, h )  -- Renders the current animation frame into a new ImageData (white bg, blue frame rect).
  Animation:getBlendState( )  -> BlendState  -- Returns the two quads and blend factor during a crossfade, or nil when not blending.
  Animation:getClip( )  -> Clip  -- Returns the name of the currently playing clip, or nil.
  Animation:getClipCount( )  -> ClipCount  -- Returns the number of registered clips.
  Animation:getCurrentFrame( )  -> CurrentFrame  -- Returns the current position within the active clip (0-based).
  Animation:getFrameCount( )  -> FrameCount  -- Returns the total number of frames in the frame pool.
  Animation:getQuad( )  -> Quad  -- Returns the source quad (x, y, w, h) for the current frame, or nil.
  Animation:getSpeed( )  -> Speed  -- Returns the playback speed multiplier.
  Animation:isLooping( )  -- Returns true if the current clip is set to loop.
  Animation:isPlaying( )  -- Returns true if a clip is currently playing.
  Animation:pause( )  -- Pauses playback at the current frame.
  Animation:play( name )  -- Starts playback of the named clip.
  Animation:pollEvents( )  -- Drains and returns all pending animation events as a table.
  Animation:resume( )  -- Resumes playback from the current frame.
  Animation:setFrame( index )  -- Sets the playback position within the current clip.
  Animation:setSpeed( speed )  -- Sets the playback speed multiplier.
  Animation:stop( )  -- Stops playback and resets to frame 0.
  Animation:update( dt )  -- Advances the animation by dt seconds.
```

**`BlendLayerSet`** methods:

## lurek.automation {#automation}

> `lurek.automation` â€” Automated input simulation via timed step scripts.

```lua
  lurek.automation.getCurrentScript( )  -> CurrentScript  -- Returns the name of the active script, or nil if idle.
  lurek.automation.getCurrentStep( )  -> CurrentStep  -- Returns the index of the next step to be dispatched.
  lurek.automation.getElapsedTime( )  -> ElapsedTime  -- Returns seconds elapsed since playback started.
  lurek.automation.getPlaybackSpeed( )  -> PlaybackSpeed  -- Returns the current playback speed multiplier (default 1.0).
  lurek.automation.getScripts( )  -> Scripts  -- Returns an array of all registered script names.
  lurek.automation.getStepCount( )  -> StepCount  -- Returns the total number of steps in the active script.
  lurek.automation.getStepLimit( name )  -> StepLimit  -- Returns the step limit for the named script, or nil if not found.
  lurek.automation.hasMacro( name )  -- Returns true if a macro with the given name has been saved.
  lurek.automation.hasScript( name )  -- Returns true if a script with the given name is registered.
  lurek.automation.isComplete( )  -- Returns true if all steps in the active script have been dispatched.
  lurek.automation.isHighlightMode( )  -- Returns whether the highlight overlay hint is active.
  lurek.automation.isPaused( )  -- Returns true if playback is currently paused.
  lurek.automation.isRunning( )  -- Returns true if the simulator is actively playing a script.
  lurek.automation.listMacros( )  -- Returns an array of all saved macro names.
  lurek.automation.load( name, data )  -- Loads a named script from a Lua data table containing a steps array.
  lurek.automation.loadFromToml( name, toml_str )  -- Parses a TOML string and registers it as a named script.
  lurek.automation.pause( )  -- Pauses playback at the current step position.
  lurek.automation.playMacro( name )  -- Loads and starts playback of a previously saved macro.
  lurek.automation.resume( )  -- Resumes playback from a paused position.
  lurek.automation.saveMacro( macro_name, script_name )  -- Saves a currently-loaded script under a macro name for fast replay.
  lurek.automation.setHighlightMode( enable )  -- Enables or disables the highlight overlay hint.
  lurek.automation.setPlaybackSpeed( factor )  -- Sets the dt multiplier for script playback (0.5 = half speed, 2.0 = double).
  lurek.automation.setStepLimit( name, n )  -- Sets the step limit for the named script (clamped to 1..MAX_STEPS).
  lurek.automation.start( name )  -- Starts playback of the named script from the beginning.
  lurek.automation.stop( )  -- Stops playback and resets the simulator to idle.
  lurek.automation.unload( name )  -- Removes a loaded script by name, returning true if it existed.
  lurek.automation.update( dt )  -- Advances the playback clock by `dt` seconds, dispatching due steps.
  lurek.automation.waitUntil( predicate, timeout )  -- Pauses playback advancement until predicate() returns true or timeout seconds elapse.
```

```lua
  lurek.debugbridge.broadcast( event, json_data )  -- Broadcasts a JSON event to all connected clients.

  lurek.debugbridge.clearPrintHistory( )  -- Clears the print history.
  lurek.debugbridge.getClientCount( )  -> ClientCount  -- Returns the number of connected TCP clients.
  lurek.debugbridge.getPerformance( )  -> Performance  -- Returns performance statistics.
  lurek.debugbridge.getPort( )  -> Port  -- Returns the server port (0 if not running).
  lurek.debugbridge.getPrintHistory( [count] )  -> PrintHistory  -- Returns the print history.
  lurek.debugbridge.isRunning( )  -- Returns whether the server is currently running.
  lurek.debugbridge.isScreenshotRequested( )  -- Returns whether a screenshot is currently requested.
  lurek.debugbridge.poll( )  -- Poll for pending Lua-dependent requests from TCP clients.
  lurek.debugbridge.requestScreenshot( [scale] )  -- Flags a screenshot request for the next frame.
  lurek.debugbridge.setMaxPrintHistory( max )  -- Sets the maximum print history size.
  lurek.debugbridge.start( [port] )  -- Start the TCP debug server on 127.0.0.1:port.
  lurek.debugbridge.stop( )  -- Stop the TCP debug server and close all connections.
```

```lua
  lurek.devtools.getWatches( )  -> Watches  -- Calls all registered watch getters and returns a table of {name, category, value} records.
  lurek.devtools.info( message )  -- Logs a message at INFO level.
  lurek.devtools.isConsoleOpen( )  -- Returns whether the console is considered open.
  lurek.devtools.isProfilingEnabled( )  -- Returns whether the profiler is enabled.
  lurek.devtools.log( level, message )  -- Logs a message at the given level.

  lurek.devtools.newRepl( [max_history] )  -> Repl  -- Creates an interactive Lua REPL console with a bounded history buffer.
  lurek.devtools.openConsole( )  -- Opens the console window (updates the console flag; returns true).

  lurek.devtools.profilePop( [] )  -- Closes the most recent profiling zone.

  lurek.devtools.profilerReport( )  -- Returns a flat summary table of all recorded profiler zones across all stored
  lurek.devtools.recordFrameTime( dt_val )  -- Records a frame-time sample (call each frame with delta time in seconds).
  lurek.devtools.removeWatch( id )  -- Removes a watch by the id returned from exposeWatch. Returns true if removed.
  lurek.devtools.resetProfile( )  -- Clears all profiling data and resets the zone stack.
  lurek.devtools.scan( )  -- Polls all watched paths and returns paths whose mtime changed.
  lurek.devtools.setFrameHistorySize( size )  -- Sets the frame-history buffer capacity (clamped 10-10000).
  lurek.devtools.setLogConsole( enabled )  -- Enables or disables console log output.

  lurek.devtools.setLogLevel( level )  -- Sets the minimum log level.
  lurek.devtools.setProfilingEnabled( enabled )  -- Enables or disables the profiler.
  lurek.devtools.setWatchInterval( interval )  -- Sets the file watch poll interval in seconds.
  lurek.devtools.snapshot( )  -- Takes a structured snapshot of all watches + frame stats + last profile frame.
  lurek.devtools.trace( message )  -- Logs a message at TRACE level.
  lurek.devtools.unwatch( path )  -- Removes a file path from the watch list.
  lurek.devtools.warn( message )  -- Logs a message at WARN level.
  lurek.devtools.watch( path )  -- Adds a file path to the watch list. Returns false if already watched.
```

```lua
  FileWatcher:getPath( )  -> Path  -- Returns the watched path string.
```

**`ApiCatalog`** methods:

> Wraps a catalog snapshot of API entries for Lua access.

```lua
  ApiCatalog:entryCount( [module] )  -- Returns the number of entries, optionally scoped to a module.
  ApiCatalog:filter( predicate )  -- Returns a new catalog containing only entries for which predicate returns true.
  ApiCatalog:getEntries( [module] )  -> Entries  -- Returns all entries, optionally filtered to a single module.
  ApiCatalog:getEntry( qualified_name )  -> Entry  -- Returns a single entry by qualified name, or nil.
  ApiCatalog:getModules( )  -> Modules  -- Returns a sorted list of module names present in the catalog.
  ApiCatalog:getTypeMethods( qualified_name )  -> TypeMethods  -- Returns entries that are methods of the given type qualified name.
  ApiCatalog:getTypes( module_name )  -> Types  -- Returns the names of all entries with kind "type" in the given module.
  ApiCatalog:merge( other )  -- Returns a new catalog that is the union of this and another catalog, with other overrid...
  ApiCatalog:search( query )  -- Returns a table of entries whose name, qualified name, or description contains query.
  ApiCatalog:toJSON( )  -- Serialises the catalog to a pretty-printed JSON string.
  ApiCatalog:toTable( )  -- Converts the catalog to a plain Lua table array.
```

```lua

  Overlay:getFilmGrainIntensity( )  -> FilmGrainIntensity  -- Returns the current film-grain intensity.
  Overlay:getFlashAlpha( )  -> FlashAlpha  -- Returns the current flash overlay alpha value.
  Overlay:getFogColor( )  -> FogColor  -- Returns the current fog tint as r, g, b, a components.
  Overlay:getFogDensity( )  -> FogDensity  -- Returns the current fog density.
  Overlay:getHeatHazeIntensity( )  -> HeatHazeIntensity  -- Returns the current heat-haze distortion intensity.
```

## lurek.globe {#globe}

> `lurek.globe` — XCOM-style Geoscape province sphere API.

```lua
  lurek.globe.get( name )  -- Get an existing globe by name, or nil.
  lurek.globe.greatCircleDistance( la, lo, lb, lo2 )  -- Great-circle distance between two lat/lon points (in unit-sphere radians).
  lurek.globe.greatCirclePath( la, lo, lb, lo2, n )  -- Great-circle path as a table of {lat, lon} pairs.
  lurek.globe.latLonToUnit( lat, lon )  -- Convert lat/lon (degrees) to a unit-sphere Cartesian vector {x, y, z}.

  lurek.globe.new( name, [spec_tbl] )  -- Creates a new globe instance with default settings and empty collections.
```

```lua
  Globe:removeMarker( id )  -- Removes a marker from the globe map by its unique string identifier.

  Globe:revealProvince( viewer, id )  -- Reveal a province for a viewer.

  Globe:update( dt )  -- Advance globe simulation by dt seconds.

```
