## lurek.network {#network}

> Provides ENet UDP, HTTP, TCP, WebSocket, and MessagePack serialization

```lua
  lurek.network.createLobby( name, port, [player_count], [max_players] )  -> LobbyInfo  -- Creates a LobbyInfo record and broadcasts it once on the local network.
  lurek.network.discoverLobbies( [timeout_ms] )  -- Listens for LAN lobby announcements for `timeout_ms` milliseconds (default 500).
  lurek.network.newClient( opts )  -> Client  -- Creates a client host that connects to a remote server.
  lurek.network.newHost( opts )  -> Host  -- Creates a new network host bound to the given address.
  lurek.network.newRuntime( )  -> Runtime  -- Creates a background network runtime for async HTTP, TCP, and WebSocket.
  lurek.network.newServer( opts )  -> Server  -- Creates a server host that binds to a port and accepts connections.
  lurek.network.pack( value )  -- Serializes a Lua value to a binary MessagePack string.
  lurek.network.syncEntity( )  -- Convenience helper: packs an entity snapshot and broadcasts it to all peers.
  lurek.network.unpack( data )  -- Deserializes a MessagePack binary string back to a Lua value.
```

**`NetworkHost`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`NetworkHost`].

```lua
  NetworkHost:broadcast( channel_id, data, [reliable] )  -- Broadcasts data to all connected peers on a channel.
  NetworkHost:connect( addr_str, [channels], [data] )  -- Initiates a connection to a remote host, returning the peer ID.
  NetworkHost:destroy( )  -- Destroys the host, closing the underlying socket.
  NetworkHost:disconnect( peer_id, [data] )  -- Gracefully disconnects a peer.
  NetworkHost:disconnectLater( peer_id, [data] )  -- Disconnects a peer after all queued packets have been sent.
  NetworkHost:disconnectNow( peer_id, [data] )  -- Immediately disconnects a peer without handshake.
  NetworkHost:flush( )  -- Flushes all pending sends immediately.
  NetworkHost:getAddress( )  -> Address  -- Returns the local bind address as a string.
  NetworkHost:getBandwidthLimit( )  -> BandwidthLimit  -- Returns the bandwidth limits as a table with incoming and outgoing fields.
  NetworkHost:getChannelLimit( )  -> ChannelLimit  -- Returns the maximum number of channels per connection.
  NetworkHost:getConnectedPeerCount( )  -> ConnectedPeerCount  -- Returns the number of currently connected peers.
  NetworkHost:getConnectedPeerIds( )  -> ConnectedPeerIds  -- Returns a table of connected peer IDs.
  NetworkHost:getPeerAddress( peer_id )  -> PeerAddress  -- Returns the remote address of a peer, or nil if unavailable.
  NetworkHost:getPeerLimit( )  -> PeerLimit  -- Returns the maximum number of peer slots.
  NetworkHost:getPeerState( peer_id )  -> PeerState  -- Returns the connection state of a peer as a string.
  NetworkHost:getPeerStats( peer_id )  -> PeerStats  -- Returns a statistics table for a peer.
  NetworkHost:getRole( )  -> Role  -- Returns the multiplayer role of this host ("server", "client", or "host").
  NetworkHost:getRoundTripTime( peer_id )  -> RoundTripTime  -- Returns the round-trip time estimate for a peer in milliseconds.
  NetworkHost:isClient( )  -- Returns true if this host was created as a client.
  NetworkHost:isDestroyed( )  -- Returns true if the host has been destroyed.
  NetworkHost:isServer( )  -- Returns true if this host was created as a server.
  NetworkHost:ping( peer_id )  -- Sends a ping to a peer to measure round-trip time.
  NetworkHost:resetPeer( peer_id )  -- Resets a peer connection immediately without notifying the remote side.
  NetworkHost:send( peer_id, channel_id, data, [reliable] )  -- Sends data to a specific peer on a channel.
  NetworkHost:service( )  -- Polls the network for one event, returning an event table or nil.
  NetworkHost:setBandwidthLimit( [incoming], [outgoing] )  -- Sets the bandwidth limits in bytes per second.
  NetworkHost:setChannelLimit( limit )  -- Sets the channel limit for future connections.
```

**`NetworkRuntime`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around [`NetworkRuntime`] for async HTTP/TCP/WebSocket.

```lua
  NetworkRuntime:httpGet( url, [headers] )  -- Convenience: sends an HTTP GET request.
  NetworkRuntime:httpPost( url, body, [headers] )  -- Convenience: sends an HTTP POST request.
  NetworkRuntime:httpRequest( opts )  -- Sends an HTTP request asynchronously. Poll with `poll()` for the response.
  NetworkRuntime:poll( )  -- Polls for completed async responses (HTTP, TCP events, WebSocket events).
  NetworkRuntime:shutdown( )  -- Shuts down the background network thread.
  NetworkRuntime:tcpClose( id )  -- Closes the TCP connection identified by the given connection handle.
  NetworkRuntime:tcpConnect( addr )  -- Opens a TCP connection to a remote address.
  NetworkRuntime:tcpSend( id, data )  -- Sends data over a TCP connection.
  NetworkRuntime:wsClose( id )  -- Closes a WebSocket connection.
  NetworkRuntime:wsConnect( url )  -- Opens a WebSocket connection.
  NetworkRuntime:wsSend( id, data )  -- Sends a text message over a WebSocket connection.
```

## lurek.parallax {#parallax}

> `lurek.parallax` â€” multi-layer scrolling background system.

```lua
  lurek.parallax.newLayer( opts )  -> Layer  -- Creates a new parallax background layer from an options table.
  lurek.parallax.newSet( name )  -> Set  -- Creates a new empty parallax set with the given name.
```

**`ParallaxLayer`** methods:

> Lua-side handle to a single parallax background layer.

```lua
  ParallaxLayer:clearClamp( )  -- Removes scroll clamping so the layer scrolls freely.
  ParallaxLayer:getAutoscroll( )  -> Autoscroll  -- Returns the autoscroll velocity as `(vx, vy)`.
  ParallaxLayer:getBlendMode( )  -> BlendMode  -- Returns the current blend mode as a string.
  ParallaxLayer:getDepth( )  -> Depth  -- Returns the current floating-point depth.
  ParallaxLayer:getOffset( )  -> Offset  -- Returns the static offset as `(x, y)`.
  ParallaxLayer:getOpacity( )  -> Opacity  -- Returns the current opacity.
  ParallaxLayer:getScrollFactor( )  -> ScrollFactor  -- Returns the scroll factor as `(x, y)`.
  ParallaxLayer:getTiling( )  -> Tiling  -- Returns `true` if seamless infinite tiling is enabled.
  ParallaxLayer:getTint( )  -> Tint  -- Returns the current tint as `(r, g, b, a)`.
  ParallaxLayer:getZ( )  -- Returns the draw-order depth.
  ParallaxLayer:isVisible( )  -- Returns `true` if the layer is currently visible.
  ParallaxLayer:render( cam_x, cam_y )  -- Draws the layer using an explicit camera world position.
  ParallaxLayer:renderAuto( )  -- Draws the layer using the engine active camera position automatically.
  ParallaxLayer:resetAutoscroll( )  -- Resets the autonomous scroll accumulator to zero.
  ParallaxLayer:setAutoscroll( vx, vy )  -- Sets the autonomous scroll velocity in world-pixels per second.
  ParallaxLayer:setBlendMode( mode )  -- Sets the GPU blend mode for this layer.
  ParallaxLayer:setClamp( min_x, min_y, max_x, max_y )  -- Clamps the scroll offset to a world-pixel range on each axis.
  ParallaxLayer:setDepth( z )  -- Sets the floating-point draw depth for fine-grained layer ordering.
  ParallaxLayer:setOffset( x, y )  -- Sets the static world-pixel position bias added on top of camera scroll.
  ParallaxLayer:setOpacity( a )  -- Sets the layer-wide opacity override in `[0.0, 1.0]`.
  ParallaxLayer:setRepeat( rx, ry )  -- Sets whether the layer tiles on the X and Y axes.
  ParallaxLayer:setScale( sx, sy )  -- Sets the texture display scale factor on each axis.
  ParallaxLayer:setScrollFactor( x, y )  -- Sets the scroll factor relative to camera movement on each axis.
  ParallaxLayer:setTileSize( w, h )  -- Sets explicit tile dimensions in logical pixels, overriding the default
  ParallaxLayer:setTiling( enabled )  -- Enables or disables seamless infinite tiling on both axes simultaneously.
  ParallaxLayer:setTint( r, g, b, a )  -- Sets the multiplicative RGBA tint applied to all pixels of this layer.
  ParallaxLayer:setVisible( v )  -- Shows or hides this layer.
  ParallaxLayer:setZ( z )  -- Sets the draw-order depth. Lower values render first (further back).
  ParallaxLayer:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  ParallaxLayer:update( dt )  -- Advances the autonomous scroll accumulator by `dt` seconds.
```

**`ParallaxSet`** methods:

> Lua-side container that groups `LuaParallaxLayer` objects for scene-level management.

```lua
  ParallaxSet:addLayer( layer )  -- Adds a layer to this set.
  ParallaxSet:getName( )  -> Name  -- Returns the name of this set.
  ParallaxSet:isVisible( )  -- Returns `true` if the set is currently visible.
  ParallaxSet:layerCount( )  -- Returns the number of layers in this set.
  ParallaxSet:removeLayerAt( index )  -- Removes the layer at the given 1-based index.
  ParallaxSet:render( cam_x, cam_y )  -- Draws all visible layers in ascending `z` order using an explicit camera position.
  ParallaxSet:renderAuto( )  -- Draws all visible layers using the engine active camera position.
  ParallaxSet:setName( name )  -- Sets the name of this set.
  ParallaxSet:setVisible( v )  -- Shows or hides all layers in this set.
  ParallaxSet:sortByZ( )  -- Re-sorts all layers by ascending `z` value.
  ParallaxSet:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  ParallaxSet:update( dt )  -- Advances the autoscroll accumulator of every layer by `dt` seconds.
```

## lurek.patterns {#patterns}

> Registers the `lurek.patterns.*` software design patterns API.

```lua
  lurek.patterns.newBlackboard( [name] )  -> Blackboard  -- Creates a new Blackboard shared key-value store.
  lurek.patterns.newCommandStack( [max_size] )  -> CommandStack  -- Creates a new CommandStack instance.
  lurek.patterns.newDebounce( wait )  -> Debounce  -- Creates a trailing-edge debounce that fires after the input stream is idle for wait sec...
  lurek.patterns.newEventBus( [name] )  -> EventBus  -- Creates a new EventBus instance.
  lurek.patterns.newFactory( )  -> Factory  -- Creates a new Factory instance.
  lurek.patterns.newFunnel( window, [max_entries], [name] )  -> Funnel  -- Creates a time-windowed event aggregator. window=0 means flush on every push.
  lurek.patterns.newList( )  -> List  -- Creates an ordered, resizable list.
  lurek.patterns.newMediator( )  -> Mediator  -- Creates a new named-channel message broker.
  lurek.patterns.newObjectPool( )  -> ObjectPool  -- Creates a new ObjectPool instance.
  lurek.patterns.newObserver( [name] )  -> Observer  -- Creates a new reactive property Observer.
  lurek.patterns.newPriorityQueue( [name] )  -> PriorityQueue  -- Creates a stable priority-ordered task queue.
  lurek.patterns.newQueue( [capacity] )  -> FIFO  -- Creates a FIFO queue. capacity=0 means unlimited.
  lurek.patterns.newRelationshipManager( )  -> RelationshipManager  -- Creates a new entity relationship manager.
  lurek.patterns.newRing( capacity, [name] )  -> Ring  -- Creates a fixed-capacity circular history buffer.
  lurek.patterns.newServiceLocator( )  -> ServiceLocator  -- Creates a new ServiceLocator instance.
  lurek.patterns.newSet( )  -> Set  -- Creates an unordered set that rejects duplicate values (by string key).
  lurek.patterns.newSimpleState( )  -> SimpleState  -- Creates a new SimpleState finite state machine instance.
  lurek.patterns.newStack( [capacity] )  -> LIFO  -- Creates a LIFO stack. capacity=0 means unlimited.
  lurek.patterns.newStrategy( )  -> Strategy  -- Creates a new strategy registry.
  lurek.patterns.newThrottle( interval )  -> Throttle  -- Creates a leading-edge rate limiter that fires at most once per interval seconds.
```

**`Blackboard`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Blackboard pattern.

```lua
  Blackboard:clear( key )  -- Removes a fact from the blackboard.
  Blackboard:clearAll( )  -- Clears all facts from the blackboard.
  Blackboard:get( key )  -- Gets a fact from the blackboard. Returns nil if not set.
  Blackboard:getRevision( )  -> Revision  -- Returns the monotonic revision counter (incremented on every write).
  Blackboard:has( key )  -- Returns true when the key has a non-nil value.
  Blackboard:keys( )  -- Returns all set fact keys as a table.
  Blackboard:set( key, value )  -- Sets a fact on the blackboard. Accepts boolean, number, or string values.
  Blackboard:snapshot( )  -- Returns all facts as a flat keyâ†’value table.
  Blackboard:unwatch( id )  -- Removes a watcher subscription by id.
  Blackboard:watch( key, callback )  -- Subscribes to changes on a specific key (or "*" for all changes).
```

**`CommandStack`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the CommandStack pattern.

```lua
  CommandStack:canRedo( )  -- Returns true if there is a command available to redo.
  CommandStack:canUndo( )  -- Returns true if the most recent command can be undone.
  CommandStack:clearAll( )  -- Clears all command history, releasing Lua registry values.
  CommandStack:execute( name, exec_fn, [undo_fn] )  -- Executes a named command and records it in undo/redo history.
  CommandStack:getCurrentName( )  -> CurrentName  -- Returns the name of the most recently executed command, or nil.
  CommandStack:getHistorySize( )  -> HistorySize  -- Returns the total number of recorded commands (undo + redo).
  CommandStack:redo( )  -- Re-executes the next undone command. Returns true if successful.
  CommandStack:undo( )  -- Undoes the most recent command. Returns true if successful.
```

**`Debounce`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Debounce pattern.

```lua
  Debounce:cancel( )  -- Cancels the pending trigger without firing.
  Debounce:getFireCount( )  -> FireCount  -- Returns the total number of times this debounce has fired.
  Debounce:isPending( )  -- Returns true when a trigger is pending.
  Debounce:onFire( f )  -- Sets the callback invoked when the debounce fires.
  Debounce:trigger( )  -- Records an input event, resetting the idle timer.
  Debounce:update( dt )  -- Advances the idle timer by dt seconds; fires the callback if idle wait expired.
```

**`EventBus`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the EventBus pattern.

```lua
  EventBus:clear( event )  -- Removes all listeners for a specific event.
  EventBus:clearAll( )  -- Removes all listeners on this EventBus.
  EventBus:emit( ... )  -- Dispatches an event, calling all registered listeners in priority order.
  EventBus:getEvents( )  -> Events  -- Returns all event names that have at least one listener.
  EventBus:getListenerCount( event )  -> ListenerCount  -- Returns the number of listeners registered for an event.
  EventBus:off( id )  -- Removes a previously registered event listener by subscription ID.
  EventBus:on( event, callback, [priority] )  -- Registers a listener callback for an event.
```

**`Factory`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Factory pattern.

```lua
  Factory:alias( alias, canonical )  -- Registers an alias pointing to an existing canonical type name.
  Factory:clearAll( )  -- Removes all registered type constructors and aliases.
  Factory:create( ... )  -- Creates an instance of the named type by invoking its constructor.
  Factory:getTypes( )  -> Types  -- Returns a table of all registered type names.
  Factory:has( type_name )  -- Returns true if the named type (or alias) is registered.
  Factory:register( type_name, ctor )  -- Registers a named type constructor function.
  Factory:remove( type_name )  -- Unregisters a type constructor (and any aliases pointing to it).
```

**`Funnel`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Funnel (event aggregator) pattern.

```lua
  Funnel:discard( )  -- Discards all buffered entries without flushing.
  Funnel:flush( )  -- Manually flushes all pending entries, invoking the onFlush callback.
  Funnel:getFlushCount( )  -> FlushCount  -- Returns the total number of flushes performed.
  Funnel:onFlush( f )  -- Sets a callback invoked when the funnel flushes. Receives a table of {tag, value} entries.
  Funnel:pendingCount( )  -- Returns the number of buffered entries not yet flushed.
  Funnel:push( tag, [value] )  -- Adds an event to the funnel. Immediately flushes if max_entries reached or window is 0.
  Funnel:update( dt )  -- Advances the window timer by dt seconds; flushes when window expires.
```

**`List`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for an ordered, resizable list.

```lua
  List:add( value )  -- Appends a value to the end of the list.
  List:clear( )  -- Removes all values from the list.
  List:contains( value )  -- Returns true if the list contains a value equal to the given Lua value (string/number/b...
  List:get( index )  -- Returns the value at a 1-based index, or nil.
  List:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the list is empty.
  List:len( )  -- Returns the number of items in the list.
  List:remove( index )  -- Removes and returns the value at a 1-based index.
  List:set( index, value )  -- Replaces the value at a 1-based index.
  List:toArray( )  -- Returns all items as a Lua table.
```

**`Mediator`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Mediator pattern.

```lua
  Mediator:broadcast( ... )  -- Dispatches a message to all handlers across all channels.
  Mediator:channels( )  -- Returns all registered channel names.
  Mediator:clear( )  -- Removes all channels and handlers.
  Mediator:handlerCount( channel )  -- Returns the number of handlers on a channel.
  Mediator:off( channel, id )  -- Unregisters a handler by ID.
  Mediator:on( channel, callback )  -- Registers a handler callback on a channel; returns handler ID.
  Mediator:removeChannel( channel )  -- Removes a channel and all its handlers.
  Mediator:send( ... )  -- Dispatches a message to all handlers on a channel.
```

**`ObjectPool`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the ObjectPool pattern.

```lua
  ObjectPool:acquire( )  -- Acquires an available object from the pool; returns nil if empty.
  ObjectPool:add( value )  -- Inserts a pre-built object into the available pool.
  ObjectPool:clearAll( )  -- Clears all objects from the pool, releasing Lua registry values.
  ObjectPool:getActiveCount( )  -> ActiveCount  -- Returns the number of currently active (acquired) objects.
  ObjectPool:getAvailableCount( )  -> AvailableCount  -- Returns the number of available (idle) objects in the pool.
  ObjectPool:getTotalCount( )  -> TotalCount  -- Returns the total number of tracked objects (active + available).
  ObjectPool:release( value )  -- Returns an object to the available pool.
```

**`Observer`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Observer pattern.

```lua
  Observer:get( key )  -- Gets a property value, or nil if not set.
  Observer:getCount( )  -> Count  -- Returns the total number of active subscriptions.
  Observer:set( key, new_val )  -- Sets a property value and fires subscribed watchers.
  Observer:subscribe( key, callback, [once] )  -- Subscribes to changes on a property key (or "*" for all).
  Observer:unsubscribe( id )  -- Removes a subscription by id.
```

**`PriorityQueue`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the PriorityQueue pattern.

```lua
  PriorityQueue:clearAll( )  -- Removes all items from the queue.
  PriorityQueue:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true when the queue has no items.
  PriorityQueue:len( )  -- Returns the number of items in the queue.
  PriorityQueue:peek( )  -- Returns the highest-priority item without removing it, or nil if empty.
  PriorityQueue:pop( )  -- Removes and returns the highest-priority item, or nil if empty.
  PriorityQueue:push( priority, value, [label] )  -- Inserts an item with a priority. Higher priorities are dequeued first.
```

**`Queue`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for a FIFO queue.

```lua
  Queue:clear( )  -- Removes all values from the queue.
  Queue:dequeue( )  -- Removes and returns the front value, or nil if empty.
  Queue:enqueue( value )  -- Adds a value to the back of the queue. Returns false if capacity is full.
  Queue:front( )  -- Returns the front value without removing it, or nil if empty.
  Queue:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the queue is empty.
  Queue:isFull( )  -- Returns true if the queue is at its capacity limit.
  Queue:len( )  -- Returns the number of items in the queue.
  Queue:toArray( )  -- Returns all items as a Lua table (front to back).
```

**`RelationshipManager`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the RelationshipManager pattern.

```lua
  RelationshipManager:adjustValue( a, b, delta )  -- Adjusts the numeric relationship value by a delta.
  RelationshipManager:defineType( name, levels, [default_level] )  -- Defines a relationship type with ordered levels.
  RelationshipManager:getLevel( a, b, type_name )  -> Level  -- Returns the named level for a typed relationship, or nil.
  RelationshipManager:getValue( a, b )  -> Value  -- Returns the numeric relationship value between two entities (default 0.0).
  RelationshipManager:pairCount( )  -- Returns the total number of stored relationship pairs.
  RelationshipManager:removePair( a, b )  -- Removes all relationship data between two entities.
  RelationshipManager:removeType( name )  -- Removes a relationship type definition.
  RelationshipManager:setLevel( a, b, type_name, level )  -- Sets a named level for a typed relationship between two entities.
  RelationshipManager:setValue( a, b, value )  -- Sets the numeric relationship value between two entities.
  RelationshipManager:typeNames( )  -- Returns all defined relationship type names.
```

**`Ring`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Ring (circular buffer) pattern.

```lua
  Ring:average( )  -- Returns the average of all numeric values, or 0 if empty.
  Ring:clear( )  -- Removes all entries from the ring.
  Ring:isFull( )  -- Returns true when the ring is at capacity.
  Ring:latest( )  -- Returns the most recently pushed entry, or nil.
  Ring:len( )  -- Returns the number of entries currently in the ring.
  Ring:push( value, [tag] )  -- Pushes a value (number or string) with an optional tag. Overwrites oldest on overflow.
  Ring:sum( )  -- Returns the sum of all numeric values in the ring.
  Ring:toArray( )  -- Returns all entries (oldest first) as an array of {id, tag, value?, text?} tables.
```

**`ServiceLocator`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the ServiceLocator pattern.

```lua
  ServiceLocator:clearAll( )  -- Removes all registered services.
  ServiceLocator:getServices( )  -> Services  -- Returns a table of all registered service names.
  ServiceLocator:has( name )  -- Returns true if a service with the given name is registered.
  ServiceLocator:locate( name )  -- Retrieves a registered service by name; returns nil if not found.
  ServiceLocator:provide( name, value )  -- Registers a named service with an associated Lua value.
  ServiceLocator:remove( name )  -- Unregisters and removes a named service.
```

**`Set`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for an unordered set. Values are keyed by their string representation.

```lua
  Set:add( key )  -- Adds a string key to the set. Returns true if it was not already present.
  Set:clear( )  -- Removes all keys from the set.
  Set:has( key )  -- Returns true if the key is in the set.
  Set:intersection( other )  -- Returns the intersection of this set and another as a new Set.
  Set:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the set is empty.
  Set:len( )  -- Returns the number of distinct keys in the set.
  Set:remove( key )  -- Removes a key from the set. Returns true if it was present.
  Set:toArray( )  -- Returns all keys as a Lua table (unordered).
  Set:union( other )  -- Returns the union of this set and another as a new Set.
```

**`SimpleState`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the SimpleState finite state machine pattern.

```lua
  SimpleState:addState( name, [callbacks] )  -- Registers a named state with optional enter, exit, and update callbacks.
  SimpleState:clearAll( )  -- Removes all states and callbacks from this state machine.
  SimpleState:getCurrent( )  -> Current  -- Returns the name of the current state, or nil if none is active.
  SimpleState:getStates( )  -> States  -- Returns a table of all registered state names.
  SimpleState:hasState( name )  -- Returns true if a state with the given name is registered.
  SimpleState:transitionTo( name )  -- Transitions to a named state, calling exit/enter callbacks as needed.
  SimpleState:update( dt )  -- Calls the update callback of the current state with the given delta time.
```

**`Stack`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for a LIFO stack.

```lua
  Stack:clear( )  -- Removes all values from the stack.
  Stack:isEmpty( )  -- Returns true if the stack is empty.
  Stack:isFull( )  -- Returns true if the stack is at its capacity limit.
  Stack:len( )  -- Returns the number of items on the stack.
  Stack:peek( )  -- Returns the top value without removing it, or nil if empty.
  Stack:pop( )  -- Removes and returns the top value, or nil if empty.
  Stack:push( value )  -- Pushes a value onto the stack. Returns false if capacity is full.
  Stack:toArray( )  -- Returns all items as a Lua table (bottom to top).
```

**`Strategy`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Strategy pattern.

```lua
  Strategy:clear( )  -- Removes all strategies and clears the active selection.
  Strategy:execute( ... )  -- Calls the currently active strategy function with the given arguments.
  Strategy:getCurrent( )  -> Current  -- Returns the name of the active strategy, or nil.
  Strategy:has( name )  -- Returns true if a strategy with this name is registered.
  Strategy:names( )  -- Returns all registered strategy names.
  Strategy:register( name, callback )  -- Registers a named strategy function.
  Strategy:remove( name )  -- Removes a strategy by name.
  Strategy:set( name )  -- Sets the active strategy by name. Returns false if not registered.
```

**`Throttle`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for the Throttle pattern.

```lua
  Throttle:getFireCount( )  -> FireCount  -- Returns the total number of times this throttle has fired.
  Throttle:getProgress( )  -> Progress  -- Returns the normalised progress through the current interval [0, 1].
  Throttle:onFire( f )  -- Sets the callback invoked when the throttle fires.
  Throttle:reset( )  -- Resets the elapsed counter without firing.
  Throttle:setEnabled( v )  -- Enables or disables the throttle.
  Throttle:update( dt )  -- Advances the timer by dt seconds; fires the callback if the interval elapsed.
```

## lurek.pipeline {#pipeline}

> `lurek.pipeline` â€” DAG-based pipeline orchestrator for composing multi-step workflows.

```lua
  lurek.pipeline.fromTable( def )  -- Deserialises a pipeline from a definition table.
  lurek.pipeline.newPipeline( [name] )  -> Pipeline  -- Creates a new empty pipeline with the given name (defaults to "pipeline").
  lurek.pipeline.newStep( name, [callback] )  -> Step  -- Creates a new pipeline step with the given name and optional callback.
```

**`Pipeline`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Pipeline`] DAG with scheduler and Lua callback registry.

```lua
  Pipeline:addConditional( name, deps_tbl, cb, cond )  -- Adds a step with a runtime condition guard: the step is skipped when `when_fn()` return...
  Pipeline:addStep( step_ud )  -- Adds a step to the pipeline. Returns self for chaining.
  Pipeline:addSubPipeline( sub_ud, alias, [deps_tbl] )  -- Inlines all steps from `sub_pipeline` into this pipeline, prefixing
  Pipeline:cancel( )  -- Cancels all pending and waiting steps.
  Pipeline:clear( )  -- Clears all steps from the pipeline.
  Pipeline:getContext( )  -> Context  -- Returns the stored async context table, or nil.
  Pipeline:getErrorMode( )  -> ErrorMode  -- Returns the current error mode as a string.
  Pipeline:getExecutionOrder( )  -> ExecutionOrder  -- Returns the topological execution order as an array of step names.
  Pipeline:getName( )  -> Name  -- Returns the pipeline's name.
  Pipeline:getParallelGroups( )  -> ParallelGroups  -- Returns parallel execution groups as a nested array of step name arrays.
  Pipeline:getResult( )  -> Result  -- Returns the current result table built from step states, or nil.
  Pipeline:getStep( name )  -> LuaStep  -- Returns the LuaStep wrapper for the named step, or nil.
  Pipeline:getStepCount( )  -> StepCount  -- Returns the total number of steps.
  Pipeline:getSteps( )  -> Lua  -- Returns a Lua array of all step wrappers in the pipeline.
  Pipeline:getStepsByTag( tag )  -> Lua  -- Returns a Lua array of all steps whose tag matches the given string.
  Pipeline:isComplete( )  -- Returns true if all steps have reached a terminal state.
  Pipeline:isRunning( )  -- Returns true if the pipeline is currently running asynchronously.
  Pipeline:onProgress( cb )  -- Registers a callback invoked after every step with `(step_name, status)`.
  Pipeline:removeStep( name )  -- Removes a step from the pipeline by name.
  Pipeline:reset( )  -- Resets all step states and clears the async context.
  Pipeline:run( [context] )  -- Executes the pipeline synchronously in topological order.
  Pipeline:runAsync( [context] )  -- Starts an async pipeline run. Steps are executed one-per-frame via update(dt).
  Pipeline:setErrorMode( mode )  -- Sets the pipeline error mode: "abort" or "continue".
  Pipeline:setName( name )  -- Sets the pipeline's name.
  Pipeline:setOnComplete( [cb] )  -- Sets the callback to invoke when the pipeline completes.
  Pipeline:setOnStepComplete( [cb] )  -- Sets the callback to invoke each time a step completes successfully.
  Pipeline:setOnStepError( [cb] )  -- Sets the callback to invoke each time a step fails.
  Pipeline:toAscii( )  -- Returns a multi-line ASCII string visualising the pipeline DAG.
  Pipeline:toTable( )  -- Serialises the pipeline definition to a Lua table (no callbacks).
  Pipeline:type( )  -- Returns the type name of this object.
  Pipeline:typeOf( name )  -- Returns the type identifier string of this pipeline stage object.
  Pipeline:update( dt )  -- Advances the async pipeline by one tick. Returns true when all steps are done.
  Pipeline:validate( )  -- Validates the pipeline DAG. Returns (ok, error_array).
```

**`Step`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a single [`PipelineStep`], plus Lua callback registry keys.

```lua
  Step:dependsOn( dep )  -- Adds a dependency on another step by name or PipelineStep. Returns self for chaining
  Step:getAttempt( )  -> Attempt  -- Returns the number of execution attempts so far
  Step:getData( key )  -> Data  -- Retrieves a metadata value by key, returning nil if not found
  Step:getDelay( )  -> Delay  -- Returns the configured delay in seconds
  Step:getDependencies( )  -> Dependencies  -- Returns the list of dependency step names
  Step:getDependencyCount( )  -> DependencyCount  -- Returns the number of declared dependencies
  Step:getDuration( )  -> Duration  -- Returns total seconds spent executing this step
  Step:getError( )  -> Error  -- Returns the error message from the last failed attempt, or nil
  Step:getName( )  -> Name  -- Returns the unique name of this step
  Step:getRetryCount( )  -> RetryCount  -- Returns the configured retry count
  Step:getStatus( )  -> Status  -- Returns the current execution status as a string
  Step:getTag( )  -> Tag  -- Returns the tag on this step, or nil if unset
  Step:getTimeout( )  -> Timeout  -- Returns the timeout stored in metadata, or 0.0 if unset
  Step:isOptional( )  -- Returns whether this step is marked as optional
  Step:setCallback( cb )  -- Stores a Lua function as the execute callback for this step
  Step:setCondition( [cond] )  -- Stores a Lua function (or nil) as the run-condition for this step
  Step:setData( key, value )  -- Stores an arbitrary string value under the given key in step metadata
  Step:setDelay( seconds )  -- Sets the delay in seconds to wait after dependencies finish
  Step:setOnError( [cb] )  -- Stores a Lua function (or nil) to call if this step fails
  Step:setOptional( optional )  -- Marks whether this step is optional (downstream steps continue on failure)
  Step:setRetryCount( count )  -- Sets the maximum number of retry attempts on failure
  Step:setRetryDelay( seconds )  -- Sets the delay in seconds between retry attempts
  Step:setTag( tag )  -- Sets the tag on this step for grouping and filtering
  Step:setTimeout( seconds )  -- Stores a timeout in seconds in the step's metadata
  Step:type( )  -- Returns the type name "PipelineStep"
  Step:typeOf( name )  -- Returns true when the given name matches "PipelineStep" or a parent type
```

## lurek.procgen {#procgen}

> `lurek.procgen` — Stateless procedural generation utilities.

```lua
  lurek.procgen.bspDungeon( [opts] )  -- Generates a dungeon using Binary Space Partitioning.
  lurek.procgen.cellularAutomata( w, h, [opts] )  -- Generates a cave-like map using cellular automata.
  lurek.procgen.floodFill( )  -- BFS flood fill on a flat grid of bytes.
  lurek.procgen.generateName( )  -- Generates a single procedural name using a Markov chain.
  lurek.procgen.generateNames( )  -- Generates N procedural names using a Markov chain.
  lurek.procgen.heightmap( [opts] )  -- Generates a heightmap using fractal noise.
  lurek.procgen.lsystem( opts )  -- Generates an L-system string.
  lurek.procgen.lsystemSegments( opts, [angle_deg], [step] )  -- Generates L-system line segments for rendering.
  lurek.procgen.noiseMap( width, height, [opts] )  -- Generates a noise map using the configurable NoiseGenerator.
  lurek.procgen.noiseMapParallel( width, height, [opts] )  -- Generates a noise map using rayon parallel processing.
  lurek.procgen.perlinNoise( x, y, px, py )  -- Evaluates periodic Perlin noise at a point.
  lurek.procgen.poissonDisk( w, h, min_dist, [max_attempts], [seed] )  -- Generates Poisson disk sample points using Bridson's algorithm.
  lurek.procgen.roomsDungeon( [opts] )  -- Generates a rooms-and-corridors dungeon.
  lurek.procgen.simplex2d( x, y )  -- Returns a single Simplex noise value at the given 2-D coordinate.
  lurek.procgen.simplex3d( x, y, z )  -- Returns a single Simplex noise value at the given 3-D coordinate.
  lurek.procgen.voronoi( w, h, pts_tbl, [opts_tbl] )  -- Generates a Voronoi diagram for a set of seed points.
  lurek.procgen.wfcGenerate( opts )  -- Generates a tile grid using Wave Function Collapse.
  lurek.procgen.worldGraph( width, height, region_count, [seed] )  -- Generates a world graph with scattered regions and edges.
```

**`Raycaster`** methods:

```lua
  Raycaster:buildScene( )  -- Builds a raycaster scene and stores it in SharedState for GPU rendering.
  Raycaster:castFloorRow( )  -- Computes floor (or ceiling) texture UV coordinates for one horizontal screen row.
  Raycaster:castRay( ox, oy, angle, max_dist )  -- Casts a single ray and returns a hit table, or nil if nothing was hit.
  Raycaster:castRayMulti( ox, oy, angle, max_dist, [max_hits] )  -- Casts a ray collecting up to max_hits wall layers, continuing through
  Raycaster:castRays( ox, oy, angle, fov, count, max_dist )  -- Casts multiple rays across a field of view, returns an array of hit tables.
  Raycaster:castRaysFlat( ox, oy, angle, fov, count, max_dist )  -- Casts multiple rays and returns a flat array of 5 floats per ray.
  Raycaster:drawCameraSweep( x, y, fov, max_dist, num_frames, fw, fh )  -- Renders a mosaic of first-person views from evenly spaced angles to an ImageData.
  Raycaster:drawDepthMap( )  -- Renders a depth-map column view to an ImageData.

  Raycaster:isBlocked( x, y )  -- Returns true when the cell at (x, y) is a wall (value > 0).
  Raycaster:lineOfSight( x1, y1, x2, y2 )  -- Checks line of sight between two points using DDA traversal.
  Raycaster:projectSprite( sx, sy, px, py, pa, fov, screen_w )  -- Projects a world-space sprite onto screen space.
  Raycaster:setCell( x, y, val )  -- Sets the cell value at grid position (x, y).
  Raycaster:setCells( cells_tbl )  -- Replaces all grid cells from a flat array of values in row-major order.
  Raycaster:setWallAlpha( tile_type, alpha )  -- Sets the opacity for a wall tile type. Alpha is clamped to [0, 1].
```

## lurek.terminal {#terminal}

> `lurek.terminal` — Grid-based character-cell terminal emulator and widget toolkit.

```lua
  lurek.terminal.addCompletion( candidate )  -- Adds a candidate string to the tab-completion engine.
  lurek.terminal.applyTheme( term_ud, theme )  -- Applies a named colour theme to a terminal, recolouring all existing cells.
  lurek.terminal.clearCmdHistory( term_ud )  -- Clears all entries from this terminal's command history.
  lurek.terminal.clearCompletions( )  -- Clears all completion candidates.
  lurek.terminal.cmdHistoryLen( term_ud )  -- Returns the total number of entries in this terminal's command history.
  lurek.terminal.getCompletions( prefix )  -> Completions  -- Returns all registered candidates that start with `prefix`, as a sorted array.
  lurek.terminal.getMaxCols( )  -> MaxCols  -- Returns the maximum number of columns a Terminal can be constructed with.
  lurek.terminal.getMaxRows( )  -> MaxRows  -- Returns the maximum number of rows a Terminal can be constructed with.
  lurek.terminal.getScrollback( term_ud, offset, count )  -> Scrollback  -- Returns a table of lines from the scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.newBorder( col, row, width, height )  -> Border  -- Creates a new decorative border widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newButton( )  -> Button  -- Creates a new button widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newLabel( col, row, [text] )  -> Label  -- Creates a new label widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newList( col, row, width, height )  -> List  -- Creates a new scrollable list widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newPanel( col, row, [width], [height] )  -> Panel  -- Creates a new container panel widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.newTerminal( [cols], [rows] )  -> Terminal  -- Creates a new terminal grid with the given dimensions.
  lurek.terminal.newTextBox( col, row, width )  -> TextBox  -- Creates a new single-line text box widget at 1-based coordinates.
  lurek.terminal.nextCmd( term_ud )  -- Steps one entry forward in command history (toward newer commands).
  lurek.terminal.nextCompletion( prefix )  -- Returns the next candidate for `prefix`, cycling on repeated calls.
  lurek.terminal.parseAnsi( text )  -- Parses `text` into coloured spans.  Returns an array of tables, each with
  lurek.terminal.prevCmd( term_ud )  -- Steps one entry back in command history (toward older commands).
  lurek.terminal.printAnsi( t_ud, col, row, text )  -- Prints ANSI-escaped `text` onto terminal `t` starting at `(col, row)`.
  lurek.terminal.printHighlighted( )  -- Prints text at 1-based `(col, row)` with per-keyword colour highlighting.
  lurek.terminal.pushCmdHistory( term_ud, cmd )  -- Appends a command string to this terminal's history.
  lurek.terminal.pushScrollback( term_ud, line )  -- Appends a line to this terminal's scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.removeCompletion( candidate )  -- Removes a candidate string from the tab-completion engine.
  lurek.terminal.resetCompletion( )  -- Resets the cycling cursor without clearing the candidate list.
  lurek.terminal.scrollbackLen( term_ud )  -- Returns the number of lines currently in this terminal's scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.setScrollbackCap( term_ud, cap )  -- Sets the maximum number of lines retained in the scrollback buffer.
  lurek.terminal.stripAnsi( text )  -- Strips all ANSI escape codes from `text` and returns the plain string.
```

**`Terminal`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Terminal`] with widget binding management.

```lua
  Terminal:addWidget( widget_ud )  -- Attaches a widget to this terminal.
  Terminal:autoResize( )  -- Resizes the window to exactly fit the terminal grid at the current font size.
  Terminal:clear( )  -- Clears all cells to defaults.
  Terminal:clearWidgets( )  -- Detaches all widgets from this terminal.
  Terminal:get( col, row )  -- Returns the cell data at 1-based coordinates.
  Terminal:getCellSize( )  -> CellSize  -- Returns the active cell size override as `{w, h}`, or `nil` if none is set.
  Terminal:getDimensions( )  -> Dimensions  -- Returns the terminal grid dimensions.
  Terminal:getFocused( )  -> Focused  -- Returns the currently focused widget, or nil.
  Terminal:getWidgetCount( )  -> WidgetCount  -- Returns the number of attached widgets.
  Terminal:keypressed( key )  -- Routes a key press to the focused widget and fires callbacks.
  Terminal:mousepressed( px, py, [button] )  -- Routes a mouse press to widgets using pixel coordinates.
  Terminal:removeWidget( widget_ud )  -- Detaches a widget from this terminal.
  Terminal:render( [x], [y] )  -- Renders the terminal grid and widgets as render commands.
  Terminal:resetCellSize( )  -- Removes the cell size override, restoring font-derived cell dimensions.
  Terminal:set( ... )  -- Sets a cell at 1-based coordinates with character FG and BG colours.
  Terminal:setCellSize( w, h )  -- Sets a per-terminal cell pixel size override, bypassing the font-derived size.
  Terminal:setFocus( value )  -- Sets the focused widget, or clears focus if nil is passed.
  Terminal:setFont( height )  -- Sets the terminal font by pixel height, snapping to the nearest built-in size.
  Terminal:textinput( text )  -- Routes text input to the focused widget and fires callbacks.
```

**`Widget`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around a [`Widget`] with attachment and callback state.

```lua
  Widget:addChild( child_ud )  -- Adds a child widget to a panel widget.
  Widget:addItem( item )  -- Adds an item to a list widget.
  Widget:clearChildren( )  -- Removes all children from a panel widget.
  Widget:clearItems( )  -- Removes all items from a list widget.
  Widget:getChild( index )  -> Child  -- Returns a child widget from a panel by 1-based index, or nil.
  Widget:getChildCount( )  -> ChildCount  -- Returns the number of children in a panel widget.
  Widget:getColor( )  -> Color  -- Returns the colour of a label or border widget.
  Widget:getItem( index )  -> Item  -- Returns a list item by 1-based index.
  Widget:getItemCount( )  -> ItemCount  -- Returns the number of items in a list widget.
  Widget:getMaxLength( )  -> MaxLength  -- Returns the maximum character length of a text box widget.
  Widget:getPosition( )  -> Position  -- Returns the widget position as 1-based coordinates.
  Widget:getSelected( )  -> Selected  -- Returns the selected item index (1-based) in a list widget, or nil.
  Widget:getSize( )  -> Size  -- Returns the widget size in cells.
  Widget:getStyle( )  -> Style  -- Returns the border style name of a border widget.
  Widget:getTag( )  -> Tag  -- Returns the free-form identification tag.
  Widget:getText( )  -> Text  -- Returns the text content of a label, button, or text box widget.
  Widget:getTitle( )  -> Title  -- Returns the title of a border widget.
  Widget:isEnabled( )  -- Returns whether the widget accepts input.
  Widget:isVisible( )  -- Returns whether the widget is visible.
  Widget:removeChild( child_ud )  -- Removes a child widget from a panel widget.
  Widget:removeItem( index )  -- Removes an item from a list widget by 1-based index.
  Widget:setColor( r, g, b, [a] )  -- Sets the colour of a label or border widget.
  Widget:setEnabled( enabled )  -- Sets whether the widget accepts input.
  Widget:setMaxLength( max_length )  -- Sets the maximum character length of a text box widget.
  Widget:setOnChange( [callback] )  -- Registers a text change callback for a text box widget.
  Widget:setOnClick( [callback] )  -- Registers a click callback for a button widget.
  Widget:setOnSelect( [callback] )  -- Registers a selection change callback for a list widget.
  Widget:setPosition( col, row )  -- Sets the widget position from 1-based coordinates.
  Widget:setSelected( [index] )  -- Sets the selected item in a list widget by 1-based index.
  Widget:setSize( width, height )  -- Sets the widget size in cells.
  Widget:setStyle( style_name )  -- Sets the border style of a border widget.
  Widget:setTag( tag )  -- Sets the free-form identification tag.
  Widget:setText( text )  -- Sets the text content of a label, button, or text box widget.
  Widget:setTitle( title )  -- Sets the title of a border widget.
  Widget:setVisible( visible )  -- Sets the widget visibility.
```

## lurek.tween {#tween}

> `lurek.tween` â€” thin Lua registration wrapper for the property tween system.

```lua
  lurek.tween.cancelAll( )  -- Cancels all active tweens, sequences, parallels, and springs immediately.
  lurek.tween.delay( seconds, [cb] )  -- Creates a no-op tween that waits `seconds`, then optionally calls `callback`.
  lurek.tween.getActiveCount( )  -> ActiveCount  -- Returns the number of currently active tween objects (tweens + seqs + pars).
  lurek.tween.getEasingNames( )  -> EasingNames  -- Returns a list of all available easing names (built-in + custom).
  lurek.tween.newState( duration, [easing] )  -> State  -- Creates a standalone tween timing state without registering it with the engine.
  lurek.tween.parallel( )  -- Creates an empty TweenParallel. Add entries with :tween() or :add(tween),
  lurek.tween.registerEasing( name, f )  -- Registers a custom easing function under `name`. `fn(t)` receives 0..1, returns 0..1.
  lurek.tween.sequence( )  -- Creates an empty TweenSequence. Add steps with :tween(), :delay(), :callback(),
  lurek.tween.spring( target_tbl, fields_tbl, [opts] )  -- Creates a physics-based spring animation that drives named fields on `target_table`
  lurek.tween.to( )  -- Sugar for `tween()` with `target` first â€” natural read order.
  lurek.tween.tween( )  -- Creates a new property tween and registers it for automatic updating.
  lurek.tween.update( dt )  -- Advances all active tweens, sequences, and parallels by `dt` seconds.
```

**`Spring`** methods:

> Lua-side spring handle: wraps [`SpringSystem`] and a registry reference to the target table.

```lua
  Spring:cancel( )  -- Stops the spring. The engine will drop it on the next `update(dt)` call.
  Spring:getPosition( field )  -> Position  -- Returns the current interpolated position for the named field, or `nil`.
  Spring:isActive( )  -- Returns `true` if the spring has not been cancelled or settled.
  Spring:isSettled( )  -- Returns `true` when all spring axes have converged within `precision`.
  Spring:setDamping( value )  -- Updates the damping coefficient on all axes.
  Spring:setStiffness( value )  -- Updates the stiffness constant on all axes.
  Spring:setTarget( fields_tbl )  -- Updates target values for all fields present in `fields_table`.
  Spring:update( dt )  -- Advances the spring by `dt` seconds and writes positions to the target table.
```

**`Tween`** methods:

> A managed interpolation from start to end values over time.

```lua
  Tween:getProgress( )  -> Progress  -- Returns raw 0..1 playback progress (not eased, not accounting for yoyo).
  Tween:isActive( )  -- Returns true if the tween is still running (not completed or cancelled).
  Tween:pause( )  -- Pauses this tween; time stops advancing but the tween is not cancelled.
  Tween:resume( )  -- Resumes a paused tween, continuing from the position where it was paused.
  Tween:setRepeat( n )  -- Sets the number of extra play cycles after the first (0 = play once, -1 = infinite).
  Tween:setYoyo( enabled )  -- Enables or disables yoyo (ping-pong) on each repeat cycle.
```

**`TweenParallel`** methods:

> A group of animations that run simultaneously over the same duration.

```lua
  TweenParallel:cancel( )  -- Cancels the parallel group immediately.
  TweenParallel:isActive( )  -- Returns true if the parallel is running and not yet complete.
```

**`TweenSequence`** methods:

> A chained sequence of animations that run one after another.

```lua
  TweenSequence:cancel( )  -- Cancels the sequence and stops all pending steps.
  TweenSequence:isActive( )  -- Returns true if the sequence has been started and has not yet completed.
```

**`TweenState`** methods:

> Lua-side wrapper around the pure-Rust [`TweenState`] timing core.

```lua
  TweenState:isComplete( )  -- Returns whether the tween state has completed.
  TweenState:lerp( start, finish )  -- Interpolates from `start` to `finish` using the eased tween progress.
  TweenState:reset( )  -- Resets the tween state to elapsed time zero.
  TweenState:t( )  -- Returns the raw 0..1 playback progress.
  TweenState:tick( dt )  -- Advances the tween state by `dt` seconds.
```

## lurek.ui {#ui}

> `lurek.ui` — Retained-mode widget UI system.

```lua
  lurek.ui.addChild( child )  -- Adds a child widget to this container.
  lurek.ui.addToast( toast_table )  -- Queues a toast notification from a table.
  lurek.ui.attachToEntity( entity_id )  -- Anchors this widget to a world-space entity by its numeric ID.
  lurek.ui.bind( key )  -- Registers a data-binding key on this widget.
  lurek.ui.clearAnchor( )  -- Removes all anchor constraints.
  lurek.ui.clearFocus( )  -- Removes keyboard focus from this widget so key events go to the next focusable.
  lurek.ui.containsPoint( x, y )  -- Returns whether (x, y) is inside this widget.
  lurek.ui.detachFromEntity( )  -- Removes the entity anchor from this widget, restoring normal layout positioning.
  lurek.ui.draw( )  -- Invokes all registered on_draw callbacks, each receiving the widget's
  lurek.ui.drawToImage( w, h )  -- Renders the UI widget tree to a CPU ImageData at the given resolution.
  lurek.ui.fadeIn( )  -- Instantly fades the widget in (sets alpha to `1.0`).
  lurek.ui.fadeOut( )  -- Instantly fades the widget out (sets alpha to `0.0` and hides it).
  lurek.ui.findById( id )  -- Recursively searches for a widget by id starting from this widget.
  lurek.ui.flushCache( )  -- Returns true if the widget tree changed since the last call, then resets the flag.
  lurek.ui.focusNext( )  -- Moves focus to the next focusable widget.
  lurek.ui.focusPrev( )  -- Moves focus to the previous focusable widget.
  lurek.ui.getAlpha( )  -> Alpha  -- Returns the widget's current alpha transparency.
  lurek.ui.getChildCount( )  -> ChildCount  -- Returns the number of children in this container.
  lurek.ui.getChildren( )  -> Children  -- Returns this container's children as widget-handle tables.
  lurek.ui.getFlexGrow( )  -> FlexGrow  -- Returns the flex-grow factor.
  lurek.ui.getFlexShrink( )  -> FlexShrink  -- Returns the flex-shrink factor.
  lurek.ui.getFocus( )  -> Focus  -- Returns the focused widget index or nil.
  lurek.ui.getId( )  -> Id  -- Returns the widget string identifier.
  lurek.ui.getMargin( )  -> Margin  -- Returns the widget margin (top, right, bottom, left).
  lurek.ui.getMaxSize( )  -> MaxSize  -- Returns the maximum widget size.
  lurek.ui.getMinSize( )  -> MinSize  -- Returns the minimum widget size.
  lurek.ui.getPadding( )  -> Padding  -- Returns the widget padding (top, right, bottom, left).
  lurek.ui.getPosition( )  -> Position  -- Returns the widget position.
  lurek.ui.getRect( )  -> Rect  -- Returns the computed screen-space rectangle after layout.
  lurek.ui.getRoot( )  -> Root  -- Returns the root panel widget table.
  lurek.ui.getSize( )  -> Size  -- Returns the current width and height of the widget in UI pixels.
  lurek.ui.getState( )  -> State  -- Returns the widget interaction state name.
  lurek.ui.getTheme( )  -> Theme  -- Returns whether a theme is set.
  lurek.ui.getToastCount( )  -> ToastCount  -- Returns the number of active toasts.
  lurek.ui.getTooltip( )  -> Tooltip  -- Returns the widget tooltip text.
  lurek.ui.getWidgetCount( )  -> WidgetCount  -- Returns the total widget count in the context.
  lurek.ui.getZOrder( )  -> ZOrder  -- Returns the widget z-order.
  lurek.ui.isEnabled( )  -- Returns whether the widget is enabled.
  lurek.ui.isVisible( )  -- Returns whether the widget is visible.
  lurek.ui.keypressed( key )  -- Forwards a key press event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.loadLayout( )  -- Load a widget tree from a Lua table definition and attach it to the UI
  lurek.ui.loadLayoutFile( path )  -- Load a widget tree from a TOML layout file and attach it to the UI root.
  lurek.ui.mousemoved( x, y )  -- Forwards a mouse move event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.mousepressed( x, y, [btn] )  -- Forwards a mouse press event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.mousereleased( x, y, [btn] )  -- Forwards a mouse release event to the GUI.
  lurek.ui.newAccordion( )  -> Accordion  -- Creates a collapsible accordion widget.
  lurek.ui.newAreaChart( opts )  -> AreaChart  -- Creates a new stacked-area chart.
  lurek.ui.newBadge( [count] )  -> Badge  -- Creates a badge widget displaying a numeric count.
  lurek.ui.newBarChart( opts )  -> BarChart  -- Creates and returns a new bar chart widget attached to this image widget.

  lurek.ui.removeChild( child )  -- Removes a child widget from this container.

  lurek.ui.setAnchor( )  -- Sets anchor edges (left, top, right, bottom).

  lurek.ui.setMinSize( w, h )  -- Sets the minimum widget size.
  lurek.ui.setOnChange( f )  -- Registers a callback invoked when this widget's value changes.
  lurek.ui.setOnClick( f )  -- Registers a callback invoked when this widget is clicked.
  lurek.ui.setOnDraw( self, f )  -- Stores a custom draw callback for later invocation.
  lurek.ui.setPadding( top, [right], [bottom], [left] )  -- Sets widget padding (CSS-like: top, right?, bottom?, left?).
  lurek.ui.setPosition( x, y )  -- Sets the widget position.
  lurek.ui.setSize( w, h )  -- Sets the width and height of the widget in UI pixels.
  lurek.ui.setTheme( theme_ud )  -- Sets the active GUI theme.
  lurek.ui.setTooltip( text )  -- Sets the widget tooltip text.
  lurek.ui.setViewport( w, h )  -- Sets the viewport dimensions used for anchor constraints and layout.
  lurek.ui.setVisible( v )  -- Shows or hides the widget; hidden widgets are not rendered or interactive.
  lurek.ui.setZOrder( z )  -- Sets the widget z-order for draw sorting.
  lurek.ui.slideIn( x, y )  -- Instantly moves the widget to `(x, y)` and makes it visible.
  lurek.ui.slideOut( x, y )  -- Instantly moves the widget to the off-screen position `(x, y)` and hides it.
  lurek.ui.textinput( text )  -- Forwards text input to the focused text input widget.
  lurek.ui.unbind( )  -- Removes the data-binding key from this widget.
  lurek.ui.update( dt )  -- Advances toast timers, removes expired toasts, and dispatches pending GUI events.
  lurek.ui.update_bindings( )  -- Updates all widgets that have a data-binding key registered via `:bind(key)`.
  lurek.ui.wheelmoved( x, y )  -- Forwards a mouse wheel event to the GUI.
```

**`LineChart`** methods:

> Lua wrapper for a line chart renderer.

```lua
  LineChart:addSeries( name, pts_tbl, r, g, b )  -- Adds a named data series to the chart.
```
